January 31, 2026

Learning Geometrically-Grounded 3D Visual Representations for View-Generalizable Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): Real-world robotic manipulation demands visuomotor policies capable of robust spatial scene understanding and strong generalization across diverse camera viewpoints. While recent advances in 3D-aware visual representations have shown promise, they still suffer from several key limitations, including reliance on multi-view observations during inference which is impractical in single-view restricted scenarios, incomplete scene modeling that fails to capture holistic and fine-grained geometric structures essential for precise manipulation, and lack of effective policy training strategies to retain and exploit the acquired 3D knowledge. To address these challenges, we present MethodName, a unified representation-policy learning framework for view-generalizable robotic manipulation. MethodName introduces a single-view 3D pretraining paradigm that leverages point cloud reconstruction and feed-forward gaussian splatting under multi-view supervision to learn holistic geometric representations. During policy learning, MethodName performs multi-step distillation to preserve the pretrained geometric understanding and effectively transfer it to manipulation skills. We conduct experiments on 12 RLBench tasks, where our approach outperforms the previous state-of-the-art method by 12.7% in average success rate. Further evaluation on six representative tasks demonstrates strong zero-shot view generalization, with success rate drops of only 22.0% and 29.7% under moderate and large viewpoint shifts respectively, whereas the state-of-the-art method suffers larger decreases of 41.6% and 51.5%.

摘要（中文）: 真实世界的机器人操作需要具备鲁棒空间场景理解能力和在不同相机视角下强大泛化能力的视觉运动策略。尽管近期三维感知视觉表征取得了显著进展，但它们仍然面临着一些关键的局限性，包括依赖推理过程中的多视角观测（这在单视角受限场景中是不切实际的）、无法捕捉整体和精细几何结构（这对精确操作至关重要）的不完整场景建模，以及缺乏有效的策略训练策略来保留和利用所获得的三维知识。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了MethodName，一个用于视角泛化机器人操作的统一的表征-策略学习框架。MethodName引入了单视角三维预训练范式，该范式利用点云重建和前馈高斯溅射在多视角监督下学习整体几何表征。在策略学习过程中，MethodName执行多步蒸馏，以保留预训练的几何理解并有效地将其转移到操作技能中。我们在12个RLBench任务上进行了实验，我们的方法在平均成功率方面比先前的最先进方法提高了12.7%。在六个代表性任务上的进一步评估表明了强大的零样本视角泛化能力，在中等和大幅度视角偏移下，成功率分别仅下降了22.0%和29.7%，而最先进方法则经历了更大的下降，分别为41.6%和51.5%。

TLDR: The paper introduces a novel representation-policy learning framework that uses single-view 3D pretraining with point cloud reconstruction and gaussian splatting to learn geometric representations for view-generalizable robotic manipulation, achieving state-of-the-art results on RLBench and strong zero-shot view generalization.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新颖的表示-策略学习框架，该框架使用单视图3D预训练、点云重建和高斯溅射来学习几何表示，从而实现视角泛化机器人操作，并在RLBench上取得最佳结果，并具有强大的zero-shot视角泛化能力。

Authors: Di Zhang, Weicheng Duan, Dasen Gu, Hongye Lu, Hai Zhang, Hang Yu, Junqiao Zhao, Guang Chen

DynamicVLA: A Vision-Language-Action Model for Dynamic Object Manipulation

Abstract (English): Manipulating dynamic objects remains an open challenge for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, which, despite strong generalization in static manipulation, struggle in dynamic scenarios requiring rapid perception, temporal anticipation, and continuous control. We present DynamicVLA, a framework for dynamic object manipulation that integrates temporal reasoning and closed-loop adaptation through three key designs: 1) a compact 0.4B VLA using a convolutional vision encoder for spatially efficient, structurally faithful encoding, enabling fast multimodal inference; 2) Continuous Inference, enabling overlapping reasoning and execution for lower latency and timely adaptation to object motion; and 3) Latent-aware Action Streaming, which bridges the perception-execution gap by enforcing temporally aligned action execution. To fill the missing foundation of dynamic manipulation data, we introduce the Dynamic Object Manipulation (DOM) benchmark, built from scratch with an auto data collection pipeline that efficiently gathers 200K synthetic episodes across 2.8K scenes and 206 objects, and enables fast collection of 2K real-world episodes without teleoperation. Extensive evaluations demonstrate remarkable improvements in response speed, perception, and generalization, positioning DynamicVLA as a unified framework for general dynamic object manipulation across embodiments.

摘要（中文）: 操纵动态物体对于视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型而言仍然是一个公开的挑战。尽管 VLA 模型在静态操纵中表现出强大的泛化能力，但在需要快速感知、时间预测和持续控制的动态场景中却表现不佳。我们提出了 DynamicVLA，一个用于动态物体操纵的框架，它通过三个关键设计整合了时间推理和闭环适应：1）一个紧凑的 0.4B VLA，使用卷积视觉编码器进行空间高效、结构保真的编码，从而实现快速的多模态推理；2）连续推理，实现重叠的推理和执行，以降低延迟并及时适应物体运动；3）潜在空间感知动作流，通过强制时间对齐的动作执行来弥合感知-执行的差距。为了填补动态操纵数据缺失的基础，我们引入了动态物体操纵 (DOM) 基准测试，该基准测试完全从零开始构建，并采用自动数据收集流程，该流程能够跨 2.8K 个场景和 206 个物体高效收集 20 万个合成片段，并能够在无需遥操作的情况下快速收集 2K 个真实世界片段。广泛的评估表明，DynamicVLA 在响应速度、感知和泛化方面都有显著改进，使其成为跨embodiment的通用动态物体操纵的统一框架。

TLDR: The paper introduces DynamicVLA, a Vision-Language-Action model designed for dynamic object manipulation, featuring a compact architecture, continuous inference, and latent-aware action streaming. They also introduce a new Dynamic Object Manipulation (DOM) benchmark with synthetic and real-world data.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DynamicVLA，一个为动态物体操作设计的视觉-语言-动作模型，具有紧凑的架构、连续推理和潜在感知动作流。他们还引入了一种新的动态对象操作（DOM）基准，其中包含合成和真实世界的数据。

Authors: Haozhe Xie, Beichen Wen, Jiarui Zheng, Zhaoxi Chen, Fangzhou Hong, Haiwen Diao, Ziwei Liu

Temporally Coherent Imitation Learning via Latent Action Flow Matching for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): Learning long-horizon robotic manipulation requires jointly achieving expressive behavior modeling, real-time inference, and stable execution, which remains challenging for existing generative policies. Diffusion-based approaches provide strong modeling capacity but typically incur high inference latency, while flow matching enables fast one-step generation yet often leads to unstable execution when applied directly in the raw action space. We propose LG-Flow Policy, a trajectory-level imitation learning framework that performs flow matching in a continuous latent action space. By encoding action sequences into temporally regularized latent trajectories and learning an explicit latent-space flow, the proposed approach decouples global motion structure from low-level control noise, resulting in smooth and reliable long-horizon execution. LG-Flow Policy further incorporates geometry-aware point cloud conditioning and execution-time multimodal modulation, with visual cues evaluated as a representative modality in real-world settings. Experimental results in simulation and on physical robot platforms demonstrate that LG-Flow Policy achieves near single-step inference, substantially improves trajectory smoothness and task success over flow-based baselines operating in the raw action space, and remains significantly more efficient than diffusion-based policies.

摘要（中文）: 学习长时程机器人操作需要联合实现富有表现力的行为建模、实时推理和稳定执行，这对现有的生成策略来说仍然具有挑战性。基于扩散的方法提供了强大的建模能力，但通常会导致较高的推理延迟，而流匹配能够实现快速的单步生成，但如果直接应用于原始动作空间，往往会导致不稳定的执行。 我们提出了LG-Flow Policy，一种轨迹级别的模仿学习框架，在连续潜在动作空间中执行流匹配。通过将动作序列编码为时间正则化的潜在轨迹，并学习显式的潜在空间流，该方法将全局运动结构与低级控制噪声分离，从而实现平滑且可靠的长时程执行。 LG-Flow Policy进一步结合了几何感知的点云条件和执行时的多模态调制，其中视觉线索被评估为真实场景中的代表性模态。在模拟和物理机器人平台上的实验结果表明，LG-Flow Policy实现了接近单步的推理速度，相较于在原始动作空间中运行的基于流的基线方法，显著提高了轨迹平滑度和任务成功率，并且比基于扩散的策略更有效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces LG-Flow Policy, a flow-matching based imitation learning framework that operates in a latent action space for smooth and stable long-horizon robotic manipulation, showing improved performance over raw action space flow-based methods and better efficiency than diffusion-based methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了LG-Flow Policy，一种基于流匹配的模仿学习框架，在潜在动作空间中运行，以实现平稳稳定的长时程机器人操作。实验表明，与原始动作空间的基于流的方法相比，该方法性能有所提高，并且比基于扩散的方法效率更高。

Authors: Wu Songwei, Jiang Zhiduo, Xie Guanghu, Liu Yang, Liu Hong

Robust and Generalized Humanoid Motion Tracking

Abstract (English): Learning a general humanoid whole-body controller is challenging because practical reference motions can exhibit noise and inconsistencies after being transferred to the robot domain, and local defects may be amplified by closed-loop execution, causing drift or failure in highly dynamic and contact-rich behaviors. We propose a dynamics-conditioned command aggregation framework that uses a causal temporal encoder to summarize recent proprioception and a multi-head cross-attention command encoder to selectively aggregate a context window based on the current dynamics. We further integrate a fall recovery curriculum with random unstable initialization and an annealed upward assistance force to improve robustness and disturbance rejection. The resulting policy requires only about 3.5 hours of motion data and supports single-stage end-to-end training without distillation. The proposed method is evaluated under diverse reference inputs and challenging motion regimes, demonstrating zero-shot transfer to unseen motions as well as robust sim-to-real transfer on a physical humanoid robot.

摘要（中文）: 学习通用人形机器人全身控制器极具挑战，因为实际参考运动在转移到机器人领域后可能表现出噪声和不一致性，并且局部缺陷可能会被闭环执行放大，导致高度动态和接触丰富的行为中出现漂移或失败。我们提出了一种动力学条件下的指令聚合框架，该框架使用因果时间编码器来概括最近的本体感觉，并使用多头交叉注意力指令编码器来基于当前动力学选择性地聚合上下文窗口。我们进一步整合了包含随机不稳定初始化和退火向上辅助力的跌倒恢复课程，以提高鲁棒性和抗扰动能力。由此产生的策略仅需要大约3.5小时的运动数据，并支持无需蒸馏的单阶段端到端训练。所提出的方法在各种参考输入和具有挑战性的运动体制下进行了评估，展示了对未见运动的零样本迁移以及在物理人形机器人上强大的仿真到真实迁移能力。

TLDR: This paper presents a dynamics-conditioned command aggregation framework for humanoid whole-body control, achieving robust zero-shot and sim-to-real transfer with limited motion data by incorporating a fall recovery curriculum.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个动力学条件下的命令聚合框架，用于人形机器人全身控制，通过结合跌倒恢复课程，实现了鲁棒的零样本和从模拟到现实的迁移，且只需要有限的运动数据。

Authors: Yubiao Ma, Han Yu, Jiayin Xie, Changtai Lv, Qiang Luo, Chi Zhang, Yunpeng Yin, Boyang Xing, Xuemei Ren, Dongdong Zheng

Self-Imitated Diffusion Policy for Efficient and Robust Visual Navigation

Abstract (English): Diffusion policies (DP) have demonstrated significant potential in visual navigation by capturing diverse multi-modal trajectory distributions. However, standard imitation learning (IL), which most DP methods rely on for training, often inherits sub-optimality and redundancy from expert demonstrations, thereby necessitating a computationally intensive "generate-then-filter" pipeline that relies on auxiliary selectors during inference. To address these challenges, we propose Self-Imitated Diffusion Policy (SIDP), a novel framework that learns improved planning by selectively imitating a set of trajectories sampled from itself. Specifically, SIDP introduces a reward-guided self-imitation mechanism that encourages the policy to consistently produce high-quality trajectories efficiently, rather than outputs of inconsistent quality, thereby reducing reliance on extensive sampling and post-filtering. During training, we employ a reward-driven curriculum learning paradigm to mitigate inefficient data utility, and goal-agnostic exploration for trajectory augmentation to improve planning robustness. Extensive evaluations on a comprehensive simulation benchmark show that SIDP significantly outperforms previous methods, with real-world experiments confirming its effectiveness across multiple robotic platforms. On Jetson Orin Nano, SIDP delivers a 2.5$\times$ faster inference than the baseline NavDP, i.e., 110ms VS 273ms, enabling efficient real-time deployment.

摘要（中文）: 扩散策略(DP)通过捕捉多模态轨迹分布，在视觉导航中展现出巨大的潜力。然而，大多数DP方法依赖的标准模仿学习(IL)常常继承专家演示中的次优性和冗余性，因此需要一个计算密集型的“生成-然后-过滤”流程，该流程在推理过程中依赖于辅助选择器。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出自模仿扩散策略(SIDP)，这是一种新颖的框架，通过选择性地模仿从自身采样的一组轨迹来学习改进的规划。具体而言，SIDP引入了一种奖励引导的自模仿机制，该机制鼓励策略持续高效地产生高质量的轨迹，而非质量不一致的输出，从而减少对大量采样和后处理的依赖。在训练过程中，我们采用奖励驱动的课程学习范式来缓解低效的数据利用率，并采用目标无关的探索来进行轨迹扩充，以提高规划的鲁棒性。在全面的模拟基准测试中进行的大量评估表明，SIDP明显优于先前的方法，真实的实验证实了其在多种机器人平台上的有效性。在Jetson Orin Nano上，SIDP的推理速度比基线NavDP快2.5倍，即110毫秒对273毫秒，从而实现了高效的实时部署。

TLDR: The paper introduces Self-Imitated Diffusion Policy (SIDP), a method for visual navigation that improves planning efficiency and robustness by self-imitating high-quality trajectories, reducing reliance on extensive sampling and post-filtering, and achieving faster inference times on resource-constrained hardware.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为自模仿扩散策略(SIDP)的视觉导航方法，该方法通过自模仿高质量轨迹来提高规划效率和鲁棒性，减少对大量采样和后处理的依赖，并在计算资源有限的硬件上实现更快的推理速度。

Authors: Runhua Zhang, Junyi Hou, Changxu Cheng, Qiyi Chen, Tao Wang, Wuyue Zhao

MTDrive: Multi-turn Interactive Reinforcement Learning for Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): Trajectory planning is a core task in autonomous driving, requiring the prediction of safe and comfortable paths across diverse scenarios. Integrating Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) with Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown promise in addressing "long-tail" scenarios. However, existing methods are constrained to single-turn reasoning, limiting their ability to handle complex tasks requiring iterative refinement. To overcome this limitation, we present MTDrive, a multi-turn framework that enables MLLMs to iteratively refine trajectories based on environmental feedback. MTDrive introduces Multi-Turn Group Relative Policy Optimization (mtGRPO), which mitigates reward sparsity by computing relative advantages across turns. We further construct an interactive trajectory understanding dataset from closed-loop simulation to support multi-turn training. Experiments on the NAVSIM benchmark demonstrate superior performance compared to existing methods, validating the effectiveness of our multi-turn reasoning paradigm. Additionally, we implement system-level optimizations to reduce data transfer overhead caused by high-resolution images and multi-turn sequences, achieving 2.5x training throughput. Our data, models, and code will be made available soon.

摘要（中文）: 轨迹规划是自动驾驶的核心任务，需要在各种场景中预测安全舒适的路径。将多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）与强化学习（RL）相结合，在解决“长尾”场景方面展现出潜力。然而，现有方法局限于单轮推理，限制了它们处理需要迭代优化的复杂任务的能力。为了克服这一局限性，我们提出了MTDrive，一个多轮框架，使MLLM能够根据环境反馈迭代优化轨迹。MTDrive引入了多轮组相对策略优化（mtGRPO），通过计算各轮之间的相对优势来缓解奖励稀疏性。我们进一步构建了一个来自闭环仿真的交互式轨迹理解数据集，以支持多轮训练。在NAVSIM基准测试上的实验表明，相比于现有方法，本方法表现出更优越的性能，验证了我们多轮推理范式的有效性。此外，我们实现了系统级优化，以减少由高分辨率图像和多轮序列引起的数据传输开销，实现了2.5倍的训练吞吐量。我们的数据、模型和代码即将开源。

TLDR: MTDrive introduces a multi-turn interactive reinforcement learning framework for autonomous driving, enabling iterative trajectory refinement using MLLMs and a novel multi-turn group relative policy optimization method, demonstrating superior performance and training throughput.

简要说明: MTDrive 引入了一个用于自动驾驶的多轮交互式强化学习框架，通过使用 MLLM 和一种新的多轮组相对策略优化方法来实现迭代轨迹优化，展示了卓越的性能和训练吞吐量。

Authors: Xidong Li, Mingyu Guo, Chenchao Xu, Bailin Li, Wenjing Zhu, Yangang Zou, Rui Chen, Zehuan Wang

A Comparative Evaluation of Large Vision-Language Models for 2D Object Detection under SOTIF Conditions

Abstract (English): Reliable environmental perception remains one of the main obstacles for safe operation of automated vehicles. Safety of the Intended Functionality (SOTIF) concerns safety risks from perception insufficiencies, particularly under adverse conditions where conventional detectors often falter. While Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) demonstrate promising semantic reasoning, their quantitative effectiveness for safety-critical 2D object detection is underexplored. This paper presents a systematic evaluation of ten representative LVLMs using the PeSOTIF dataset, a benchmark specifically curated for long-tail traffic scenarios and environmental degradations. Performance is quantitatively compared against the classical perception approach, a YOLO-based detector. Experimental results reveal a critical trade-off: top-performing LVLMs (e.g., Gemini 3, Doubao) surpass the YOLO baseline in recall by over 25% in complex natural scenarios, exhibiting superior robustness to visual degradation. Conversely, the baseline retains an advantage in geometric precision for synthetic perturbations. These findings highlight the complementary strengths of semantic reasoning versus geometric regression, supporting the use of LVLMs as high-level safety validators in SOTIF-oriented automated driving systems.

摘要（中文）: 可靠的环境感知仍然是自动驾驶汽车安全运行的主要障碍之一。预期功能安全（SOTIF）关注感知不足带来的安全风险，尤其是在传统检测器经常失效的恶劣条件下。虽然大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）展现出令人鼓舞的语义推理能力，但其在安全关键型二维目标检测中的定量有效性尚未得到充分探索。本文使用PeSOTIF数据集（一个专门为长尾交通场景和环境退化而设计的基准）对十个具有代表性的LVLM进行了系统评估。性能与基于YOLO的经典感知方法进行了定量比较。实验结果揭示了一个关键的权衡：性能最佳的LVLM（例如，Gemini 3、豆包）在复杂的自然场景中，与YOLO基线相比，召回率高出25%以上，表现出对视觉退化的卓越鲁棒性。相反，该基线在合成扰动的几何精度方面保持优势。这些发现突出了语义推理与几何回归的互补优势，支持将LVLM用作面向SOTIF的自动驾驶系统中的高级安全验证器。

TLDR: This paper evaluates the performance of Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) for 2D object detection in automated driving, specifically under Safety of the Intended Functionality (SOTIF) conditions, finding a trade-off between LVLM's recall in complex scenarios and traditional detectors' geometric precision.

简要说明: 本文评估了大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）在自动驾驶中2D物体检测方面的性能，尤其是在预期功能安全（SOTIF）条件下，发现LVLMs在复杂场景中的召回率与传统检测器几何精度之间存在权衡。

Authors: Ji Zhou, Yilin Ding, Yongqi Zhao, Jiachen Xu, Arno Eichberger

Adapting Reinforcement Learning for Path Planning in Constrained Parking Scenarios

Abstract (English): Real-time path planning in constrained environments remains a fundamental challenge for autonomous systems. Traditional classical planners, while effective under perfect perception assumptions, are often sensitive to real-world perception constraints and rely on online search procedures that incur high computational costs. In complex surroundings, this renders real-time deployment prohibitive. To overcome these limitations, we introduce a Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) framework for real-time path planning in parking scenarios. In particular, we focus on challenging scenes with tight spaces that require a high number of reversal maneuvers and adjustments. Unlike classical planners, our solution does not require ideal and structured perception, and in principle, could avoid the need for additional modules such as localization and tracking, resulting in a simpler and more practical implementation. Also, at test time, the policy generates actions through a single forward pass at each step, which is lightweight enough for real-time deployment. The task is formulated as a sequential decision-making problem grounded in a bicycle model dynamics, enabling the agent to directly learn navigation policies that respect vehicle kinematics and environmental constraints in the closed-loop setting. A new benchmark is developed to support both training and evaluation, capturing diverse and challenging scenarios. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art success rates and efficiency, surpassing classical planner baselines by +96% in success rate and +52% in efficiency. Furthermore, we release our benchmark as an open-source resource for the community to foster future research in autonomous systems. The benchmark and accompanying tools are available at https://github.com/dqm5rtfg9b-collab/Constrained_Parking_Scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 在受限环境中进行实时路径规划仍然是自主系统面临的一项根本性挑战。传统的经典规划器虽然在完美的感知假设下有效，但通常对现实世界的感知约束很敏感，并且依赖于产生高计算成本的在线搜索过程。在复杂环境中，这使得实时部署变得难以实现。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了一种基于深度强化学习（DRL）的框架，用于停车场场景中的实时路径规划。特别地，我们关注需要多次倒车和调整的狭小空间等具有挑战性的场景。与经典规划器不同，我们的解决方案不需要理想且结构化的感知，并且原则上可以避免对定位和跟踪等额外模块的需求，从而实现更简单和更实用的实现方案。此外，在测试阶段，策略在每一步通过单个前向传递生成动作，其计算量足够轻量化，可以进行实时部署。该任务被表述为一个基于自行车模型动力学的序列决策问题，使智能体能够直接学习尊重车辆运动学和环境约束的闭环导航策略。我们开发了一个新的基准，以支持训练和评估，捕捉了多样且具有挑战性的场景。我们的方法实现了最先进的成功率和效率，其成功率和效率分别比经典规划器基线高出+96%和+52%。此外，我们以开源资源的形式发布了我们的基准，以促进社区对自主系统未来的研究。该基准和配套工具可在https://github.com/dqm5rtfg9b-collab/Constrained_Parking_Scenarios 获得。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Deep Reinforcement Learning framework for real-time path planning in constrained parking scenarios, achieving state-of-the-art performance compared to classical planners and releasing a new benchmark for the community.

Authors: Feng Tao, Luca Paparusso, Chenyi Gu, Robin Koehler, Chenxu Wu, Xinyu Huang, Christian Juette, David Paz, Ren Liu

CARE: Multi-Task Pretraining for Latent Continuous Action Representation in Robot Control

Abstract (English): Recent advances in Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promise for robot control, but their dependence on action supervision limits scalability and generalization. To address this challenge, we introduce CARE, a novel framework designed to train VLA models for robotic task execution. Unlike existing methods that depend on action annotations during pretraining, CARE eliminates the need for explicit action labels by leveraging only video-text pairs. These weakly aligned data sources enable the model to learn continuous latent action representations through a newly designed multi-task pretraining objective. During fine-tuning, a small set of labeled data is used to train the action head for control. Experimental results across various simulation tasks demonstrate CARE's superior success rate, semantic interpretability, and ability to avoid shortcut learning. These results underscore CARE's scalability, interpretability, and effectiveness in robotic control with weak supervision.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型近期的进展在机器人控制方面展现出潜力，但其对动作监督的依赖限制了可扩展性和泛化能力。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了 CARE，一种旨在训练用于机器人任务执行的 VLA 模型的新型框架。与依赖于预训练期间的动作标注的现有方法不同，CARE 通过仅利用视频-文本对消除了对显式动作标签的需求。这些弱对齐的数据源使模型能够通过新设计的多任务预训练目标学习连续潜在动作表示。在微调期间，使用少量标记数据来训练用于控制的动作头。在各种模拟任务上的实验结果表明，CARE 具有更高的成功率、语义可解释性，以及避免捷径学习的能力。这些结果突显了 CARE 在弱监督机器人控制中的可扩展性、可解释性和有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces CARE, a VLA model training framework that learns continuous latent action representations from video-text pairs using a multi-task pretraining objective, eliminating the need for action labels during pretraining, and demonstrating superior performance in robotic control.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CARE，一个VLA模型训练框架，它使用多任务预训练目标，从视频文本对中学习连续的潜在动作表示，从而消除了在预训练期间对动作标签的需求，并在机器人控制中展示了卓越的性能。

Authors: Jiaqi Shi, Xulong Zhang, Xiaoyang Qu, Jianzong Wang

PoSafeNet: Safe Learning with Poset-Structured Neural Nets

Abstract (English): Safe learning is essential for deploying learningbased controllers in safety-critical robotic systems, yet existing approaches often enforce multiple safety constraints uniformly or via fixed priority orders, leading to infeasibility and brittle behavior. In practice, safety requirements are heterogeneous and admit only partial priority relations, where some constraints are comparable while others are inherently incomparable. We formalize this setting as poset-structured safety, modeling safety constraints as a partially ordered set and treating safety composition as a structural property of the policy class. Building on this formulation, we propose PoSafeNet, a differentiable neural safety layer that enforces safety via sequential closed-form projection under poset-consistent constraint orderings, enabling adaptive selection or mixing of valid safety executions while preserving priority semantics by construction. Experiments on multi-obstacle navigation, constrained robot manipulation, and vision-based autonomous driving demonstrate improved feasibility, robustness, and scalability over unstructured and differentiable quadratic program-based safety layers.

摘要（中文）: 安全学习对于在安全攸关型机器人系统中部署基于学习的控制器至关重要，然而现有方法常以统一方式或通过固定优先级顺序来实施多个安全约束，导致不可行和脆弱的行为。在实践中，安全需求是异构的，并且仅允许部分优先级关系，其中一些约束是可比较的，而另一些约束本质上是不可比较的。我们将此设定形式化为偏序集结构安全，将安全约束建模为偏序集，并将安全组合视为策略类的结构属性。在此形式化的基础上，我们提出 PoSafeNet，这是一个可微分的神经安全层，它通过在偏序集一致的约束排序下进行顺序闭式投影来强制执行安全性，从而能够在保持优先级语义的同时自适应地选择或混合有效的安全执行。在多障碍物导航、约束机器人操作和基于视觉的自动驾驶方面的实验表明，与非结构化和基于可微分二次规划的安全层相比，该方法在可行性、鲁棒性和可扩展性方面有所改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces PoSafeNet, a neural safety layer that enforces safety in robotic systems with partially ordered constraints, improving feasibility and robustness over existing safety layer methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PoSafeNet，一种神经安全层，用于在具有部分排序约束的机器人系统中强制安全，与现有的安全层方法相比，提高了可行性和鲁棒性。

Authors: Kiwan Wong, Wei Xiao, Daniela Rus

Guided by Trajectories: Repairing and Rewarding Tool-Use Trajectories for Tool-Integrated Reasoning

Abstract (English): Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) enables large language models (LLMs) to solve complex tasks by interacting with external tools, yet existing approaches depend on high-quality synthesized trajectories selected by scoring functions and sparse outcome-based rewards, providing limited and biased supervision for learning TIR. To address these challenges, in this paper, we propose AutoTraj, a two-stage framework that automatically learns TIR by repairing and rewarding tool-use trajectories. Specifically, in the supervised fine-tuning (SFT) stage, AutoTraj generates multiple candidate tool-use trajectories for each query and evaluates them along multiple dimensions. High-quality trajectories are directly retained, while low-quality ones are repaired using a LLM (i.e., LLM-as-Repairer). The resulting repaired and high-quality trajectories form a synthetic SFT dataset, while each repaired trajectory paired with its original low-quality counterpart constitutes a dataset for trajectory preference modeling. In the reinforcement learning (RL) stage, based on the preference dataset, we train a trajectory-level reward model to assess the quality of reasoning paths and combine it with outcome and format rewards, thereby explicitly guiding the optimization toward reliable TIR behaviors. Experiments on real-world benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of AutoTraj in TIR.

摘要（中文）: 工具集成推理（TIR）使大型语言模型（LLM）能够通过与外部工具交互来解决复杂任务，然而现有方法依赖于由评分函数选择的高质量合成轨迹和稀疏的基于结果的奖励，为学习TIR提供有限且有偏差的监督。为了应对这些挑战，本文提出了一种两阶段框架AutoTraj，它通过修复和奖励工具使用轨迹来自动学习TIR。具体而言，在监督微调（SFT）阶段，AutoTraj为每个查询生成多个候选工具使用轨迹，并从多个维度评估它们。高质量的轨迹被直接保留，而低质量的轨迹则使用LLM（即LLM作为修复器）进行修复。最终生成的修复轨迹和高质量轨迹构成一个合成SFT数据集，而每个修复过的轨迹与其原始低质量对应项构成一个用于轨迹偏好建模的数据集。在强化学习（RL）阶段，基于偏好数据集，我们训练一个轨迹级别的奖励模型来评估推理路径的质量，并将其与结果奖励和格式奖励相结合，从而明确地引导优化朝着可靠的TIR行为发展。在真实世界基准测试上的实验表明了AutoTraj在TIR中的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces AutoTraj, a two-stage framework that improves Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) in LLMs by repairing low-quality tool-use trajectories and training a trajectory-level reward model to guide optimization towards reliable reasoning behaviors.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为AutoTraj的两阶段框架，通过修复低质量的工具使用轨迹，并训练轨迹级别的奖励模型来指导优化，从而提高LLM中的工具集成推理(TIR)能力。

Authors: Siyu Gong, Linan Yue, Weibo Gao, Fangzhou Yao, Shimin Di, Lei Feng, Min-Ling Zhang

Alignment among Language, Vision and Action Representations

Abstract (English): A fundamental question in cognitive science and AI concerns whether different learning modalities: language, vision, and action, give rise to distinct or shared internal representations. Traditional views assume that models trained on different data types develop specialized, non-transferable representations. However, recent evidence suggests unexpected convergence: models optimized for distinct tasks may develop similar representational geometries. We investigate whether this convergence extends to embodied action learning by training a transformer-based agent to execute goal-directed behaviors in response to natural language instructions. Using behavioral cloning on the BabyAI platform, we generated action-grounded language embeddings shaped exclusively by sensorimotor control requirements. We then compared these representations with those extracted from state-of-the-art large language models (LLaMA, Qwen, DeepSeek, BERT) and vision-language models (CLIP, BLIP). Despite substantial differences in training data, modality, and objectives, we observed robust cross-modal alignment. Action representations aligned strongly with decoder-only language models and BLIP (precision@15: 0.70-0.73), approaching the alignment observed among language models themselves. Alignment with CLIP and BERT was significantly weaker. These findings indicate that linguistic, visual, and action representations converge toward partially shared semantic structures, supporting modality-independent semantic organization and highlighting potential for cross-domain transfer in embodied AI systems.

摘要（中文）: 认知科学和人工智能领域的一个基本问题在于，不同的学习模态：语言、视觉和行动，是否会产生截然不同或共享的内部表征。传统观点认为，在不同类型的数据上训练的模型会发展出专门化、不可迁移的表征。然而，最近的证据表明存在出乎意料的收敛：为不同任务优化的模型可能发展出相似的表征几何。我们通过训练一个基于Transformer的智能体，使其响应自然语言指令执行目标导向的行为，来研究这种收敛是否延伸到具身行动学习中。利用BabyAI平台上的行为克隆，我们生成了完全由感觉运动控制需求塑造的行动基础语言嵌入。然后，我们将这些表征与从最先进的大型语言模型（LLaMA、Qwen、DeepSeek、BERT）和视觉-语言模型（CLIP、BLIP）中提取的表征进行比较。尽管在训练数据、模态和目标方面存在显著差异，但我们观察到了稳健的跨模态对齐。行动表征与仅使用解码器的语言模型和BLIP高度对齐（precision@15：0.70-0.73），接近于语言模型自身之间的对齐程度。与CLIP和BERT的对齐程度明显较弱。这些发现表明，语言、视觉和行动表征收敛于部分共享的语义结构，支持模态独立的语义组织，并突出了具身人工智能系统中跨领域迁移的潜力。

TLDR: This paper explores the alignment between language, vision, and action representations, finding a surprising convergence between action representations (trained via behavioral cloning) and language models, suggesting shared semantic structures across modalities.

简要说明: 本文探讨了语言、视觉和动作表征之间的对齐关系，发现动作表征（通过行为克隆训练）与语言模型之间存在令人惊讶的收敛，表明跨模态之间存在共享的语义结构。

Authors: Nicola Milano, Stefano Nolfi

MulFeRL: Enhancing Reinforcement Learning with Verbal Feedback in a Multi-turn Loop

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is widely used to improve reasoning in multiple domains, yet outcome-only scalar rewards are often sparse and uninformative, especially on failed samples, where they merely indicate failure and provide no insight into why the reasoning fails. In this paper, we investigate how to leverage richer verbal feedback to guide RLVR training on failed samples, and how to convert such feedback into a trainable learning signal. Specifically, we propose a multi-turn feedback-guided reinforcement learning framework. It builds on three mechanisms: (1) dynamic multi-turn regeneration guided by feedback, triggered only on failed samples, (2) two complementary learning signals for within-turn and cross-turn optimization, and (3) structured feedback injection into the model's reasoning process. Trained on sampled OpenR1-Math, the approach outperforms supervised fine-tuning and RLVR baselines in-domain and generalizes well out-of-domain.

摘要（中文）: 具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）被广泛应用于提升多个领域的推理能力，但是，仅依赖结果的标量奖励往往是稀疏且缺乏信息的，尤其是在失败的样本上，这些奖励仅仅表明失败，而未能提供关于推理为何失败的洞察。在本文中，我们研究了如何利用更丰富的口头反馈来指导RLVR对失败样本的训练，以及如何将此类反馈转化为可训练的学习信号。具体而言，我们提出了一种多轮反馈引导的强化学习框架。该框架构建于三种机制之上：（1）仅在失败样本上触发的，由反馈引导的动态多轮再生，（2）用于轮内和跨轮优化的两种互补学习信号，以及（3）结构化的反馈注入到模型的推理过程中。在采样的OpenR1-Math上进行训练后，该方法在领域内优于监督式微调和RLVR基线，并且在领域外具有良好的泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces MulFeRL, a multi-turn feedback-guided reinforcement learning framework that uses verbal feedback on failed samples to improve reasoning, particularly in mathematical problem-solving, outperforming existing methods.

Authors: Xuancheng Li, Haitao Li, Yujia Zhou, YiqunLiu, Qingyao Ai

Game-Theoretic Co-Evolution for LLM-Based Heuristic Discovery

Abstract (English): Large language models (LLMs) have enabled rapid progress in automatic heuristic discovery (AHD), yet most existing methods are predominantly limited by static evaluation against fixed instance distributions, leading to potential overfitting and poor generalization under distributional shifts. We propose Algorithm Space Response Oracles (ASRO), a game-theoretic framework that reframes heuristic discovery as a program level co-evolution between solver and instance generator. ASRO models their interaction as a two-player zero-sum game, maintains growing strategy pools on both sides, and iteratively expands them via LLM-based best-response oracles against mixed opponent meta-strategies, thereby replacing static evaluation with an adaptive, self-generated curriculum. Across multiple combinatorial optimization domains, ASRO consistently outperforms static-training AHD baselines built on the same program search mechanisms, achieving substantially improved generalization and robustness on diverse and out-of-distribution instances.

摘要（中文）: 大规模语言模型（LLMs）推动了自动启发式发现（AHD）的快速发展，然而，现有的大多数方法主要局限于针对固定实例分布的静态评估，导致潜在的过拟合和分布偏移下的泛化能力不足。我们提出了算法空间响应预言机（ASRO），这是一个博弈论框架，它将启发式发现重新定义为求解器和实例生成器之间的程序级协同进化。ASRO将它们的交互建模为一个双人零和博弈，维护双方不断增长的策略池，并通过基于LLM的最佳响应预言机，针对混合对手元策略迭代地扩展它们，从而用自适应、自生成的课程取代静态评估。在多个组合优化领域，ASRO始终优于基于相同程序搜索机制构建的静态训练AHD基线，在各种和超出分布的实例上实现了显著改进的泛化能力和鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces Algorithm Space Response Oracles (ASRO), a game-theoretic co-evolution framework using LLMs to improve automatic heuristic discovery by iteratively co-evolving solvers and instance generators, leading to better generalization.

Authors: Xinyi Ke, Kai Li, Junliang Xing, Yifan Zhang, Jian Cheng

Learning with Challenges: Adaptive Difficulty-Aware Data Generation for Mobile GUI Agent Training

Abstract (English): Large-scale, high-quality interaction trajectories are essential for advancing mobile Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents. While existing methods typically rely on labor-intensive human demonstrations or automated model exploration to generate GUI trajectories, they lack fine-grained control over task difficulty. This fundamentally restricts learning effectiveness due to the mismatch between the training difficulty and the agent's capabilities. Inspired by how humans acquire skills through progressively challenging tasks, we propose MobileGen, a novel data generation framework that adaptively aligns training difficulty with the GUI agent's capability frontier. Specifically, MobileGen explicitly decouples task difficulty into structural (e.g., trajectory length) and semantic (e.g., task goal) dimensions. It then iteratively evaluates the agent on a curated prior dataset to construct a systematic profile of its capability frontier across these two dimensions. With this profile, the probability distribution of task difficulty is adaptively computed, from which the target difficulty for the next round of training can be sampled. Guided by the sampled difficulty, a multi-agent controllable generator is finally used to synthesize high-quality interaction trajectories along with corresponding task instructions. Extensive experiments show that MobileGen consistently outperforms existing data generation methods by improving the average performance of GUI agents by 1.57 times across multiple challenging benchmarks. This highlights the importance of capability-aligned data generation for effective mobile GUI agent training.

摘要（中文）: 大规模、高质量的交互轨迹对于推进移动图形用户界面（GUI）智能体至关重要。然而，现有的方法通常依赖于劳动密集型的人工演示或自动模型探索来生成GUI轨迹，但它们缺乏对任务难度的细粒度控制。这从根本上限制了学习效果，原因是训练难度与智能体的能力不匹配。受人类通过渐进性挑战任务习得技能的启发，我们提出了MobileGen，一种新颖的数据生成框架，该框架自适应地将训练难度与GUI智能体的能力边界对齐。具体来说，MobileGen将任务难度显式地解耦为结构（例如，轨迹长度）和语义（例如，任务目标）维度。然后，它在精选的先验数据集上迭代评估智能体，以构建其在这两个维度上的能力边界的系统性轮廓。基于此轮廓，自适应地计算任务难度的概率分布，从中可以采样下一轮训练的目标难度。在采样的难度指导下，最终使用一种多智能体可控生成器来合成高质量的交互轨迹以及相应的任务指令。大量实验表明，MobileGen在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中，通过将GUI智能体的平均性能提高1.57倍，始终优于现有的数据生成方法。这突出了能力对齐的数据生成对于有效的移动GUI智能体训练的重要性。

TLDR: The paper introduces MobileGen, a framework for adaptively generating GUI interaction trajectories for agent training by aligning task difficulty with the agent's capabilities, leading to improved performance.

Authors: Linjia Kang, Zhimin Wang, Yongkang Zhang, Duo Wu, Jinghe Wang, Ming Ma, Haopeng Yan, Zhi Wang

TSPO: Breaking the Double Homogenization Dilemma in Multi-turn Search Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Multi-turn tool-integrated reasoning enables Large Language Models (LLMs) to solve complex tasks through iterative information retrieval. However, current reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks for search-augmented reasoning predominantly rely on sparse outcome-level rewards, leading to a "Double Homogenization Dilemma." This manifests as (1) Process homogenization, where the thinking, reasoning, and tooling involved in generation are ignored. (2) Intra-group homogenization, coarse-grained outcome rewards often lead to inefficiencies in intra-group advantage estimation with methods like Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) during sampling. To address this, we propose Turn-level Stage-aware Policy Optimization (TSPO). TSPO introduces the First-Occurrence Latent Reward (FOLR) mechanism, allocating partial rewards to the step where the ground-truth answer first appears, thereby preserving process-level signals and increasing reward variance within groups without requiring external reward models or any annotations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TSPO significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving average performance gains of 24% and 13.6% on Qwen2.5-3B and 7B models, respectively.

摘要（中文）: 多轮工具集成推理使得大型语言模型（LLMs）能够通过迭代式信息检索解决复杂任务。然而，当前用于搜索增强推理的强化学习（RL）框架主要依赖于稀疏的结果级奖励，导致了“双重同质化困境”。这表现为（1）过程同质化，即忽略了生成过程中的思考、推理和工具使用。（2）组内同质化，粗粒度的结果奖励通常导致在使用诸如组相对策略优化（GRPO）等方法进行抽样时，组内优势估计的效率低下。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了回合级阶段感知策略优化（TSPO）。TSPO引入了首次出现潜在奖励（FOLR）机制，将部分奖励分配给首次出现真实答案的步骤，从而保留过程级信号并提高组内奖励方差，而无需外部奖励模型或任何标注。大量实验表明，TSPO显著优于最先进的基线方法，在Qwen2.5-3B和7B模型上分别实现了平均24%和13.6%的性能提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces TSPO, a reinforcement learning method that tackles the 'Double Homogenization Dilemma' in multi-turn search policy optimization for LLMs by using a First-Occurrence Latent Reward mechanism. It shows significant performance gains over existing baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TSPO，一种强化学习方法，通过使用首次出现潜在奖励机制来解决LLM多轮搜索策略优化中的“双重同质化困境”。实验表明，该方法比现有基线方法有显著的性能提升。

Authors: Shichao Ma, Zhiyuan Ma, Ming Yang, Xiaofan Li, Xing Wu, Jintao Du, Yu Cheng, Weiqiang Wang, Qiliang Liu, Zhengyang Zhou, Yang Wang

AutoRefine: From Trajectories to Reusable Expertise for Continual LLM Agent Refinement

Abstract (English): Large language model agents often fail to accumulate knowledge from experience, treating each task as an independent challenge. Recent methods extract experience as flattened textual knowledge, which cannot capture procedural logic of complex subtasks. They also lack maintenance mechanisms, causing repository degradation as experience accumulates. We introduce AutoRefine, a framework that extracts and maintains dual-form Experience Patterns from agent execution histories. For procedural subtasks, we extract specialized subagents with independent reasoning and memory. For static knowledge, we extract skill patterns as guidelines or code snippets. A continuous maintenance mechanism scores, prunes, and merges patterns to prevent repository degradation. Evaluated on ALFWorld, ScienceWorld, and TravelPlanner, AutoRefine achieves 98.4%, 70.4%, and 27.1% respectively, with 20-73% step reductions. On TravelPlanner, automatic extraction exceeds manually designed systems (27.1% vs 12.1%), demonstrating its ability to capture procedural coordination.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型智能体往往无法从经验中积累知识，而是将每个任务视为独立的挑战。最近的方法将经验提取为扁平化的文本知识，无法捕捉复杂子任务的程序性逻辑。它们也缺乏维护机制，导致经验积累时知识库退化。我们引入了AutoRefine，一个从智能体执行历史中提取并维护双形式经验模式的框架。对于程序性子任务，我们提取具有独立推理和记忆的专业化子智能体。对于静态知识，我们提取技能模式作为指导或代码片段。一个连续维护机制对模式进行评分、修剪和合并，以防止知识库退化。在ALFWorld、ScienceWorld和TravelPlanner上的评估表明，AutoRefine分别取得了98.4%、70.4%和27.1%的成功率，并减少了20-73%的步骤。在TravelPlanner上，自动提取超越了手动设计的系统（27.1% vs 12.1%），证明了其捕捉程序性协调的能力。

TLDR: AutoRefine extracts and maintains reusable expertise from LLM agent execution histories in the form of specialized subagents and skill patterns, demonstrating improved performance and efficiency across several tasks.

简要说明: AutoRefine从LLM智能体的执行历史中提取并维护可重用的专业知识，以专业化的子智能体和技能模式的形式呈现，在多个任务中表现出更高的性能和效率。

Authors: Libin Qiu, Zhirong Gao, Junfu Chen, Yuhang Ye, Weizhi Huang, Xiaobo Xue, Wenkai Qiu, Shuo Tang

A Step Back: Prefix Importance Ratio Stabilizes Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) post-training has increasingly demonstrated strong ability to elicit reasoning behaviors in large language models (LLMs). For training efficiency, rollouts are typically generated in an off-policy manner using an older sampling policy and then used to update the current target policy. To correct the resulting discrepancy between the sampling and target policies, most existing RL objectives rely on a token-level importance sampling ratio, primarily due to its computational simplicity and numerical stability. However, we observe that token-level correction often leads to unstable training dynamics when the degree of off-policyness is large. In this paper, we revisit LLM policy optimization under off-policy conditions and show that the theoretically rigorous correction term is the prefix importance ratio, and that relaxing it to a token-level approximation can induce instability in RL post-training. To stabilize LLM optimization under large off-policy drift, we propose a simple yet effective objective, Minimum Prefix Ratio (MinPRO). MinPRO replaces the unstable cumulative prefix ratio with a non-cumulative surrogate based on the minimum token-level ratio observed in the preceding prefix. Extensive experiments on both dense and mixture-of-experts LLMs, across multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks, demonstrate that MinPRO substantially improves training stability and peak performance in off-policy regimes.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）后训练已逐渐展现出激发大型语言模型（LLM）推理行为的强大能力。为了训练效率，通常以离线方式使用较旧的抽样策略生成轨迹，然后用于更新当前的target策略。为了纠正抽样策略和target策略之间由此产生的差异，大多数现有的RL目标都依赖于token级别的重要性抽样比率，这主要是因为其计算简单和数值稳定性。然而，我们观察到，当策略偏移程度较大时，token级别的校正通常会导致不稳定的训练动态。在本文中，我们重新审视了离线条件下的LLM策略优化，并表明理论上严谨的校正项是前缀重要性比率，而将其放宽为token级别的近似会诱导RL后训练中的不稳定性。为了在大的策略偏移下稳定LLM优化，我们提出了一种简单而有效的目标函数，即最小前缀比率（MinPRO）。MinPRO用一个基于先前前缀中观察到的最小token级别比率的非累积代理项来代替不稳定的累积前缀比率。在多个数学推理基准测试中，对密集和混合专家LLM的大量实验表明，MinPRO在离线状态下显著提高了训练稳定性和峰值性能。

TLDR: The paper identifies instability issues with token-level importance sampling in off-policy RL fine-tuning of LLMs and proposes MinPRO, a more stable training objective using a minimum prefix ratio to improve performance on mathematical reasoning tasks.

简要说明: 该论文指出在LLM的离策略强化学习微调中，token级别的重要性采样存在不稳定性问题，并提出了MinPRO方法。MinPRO使用最小前缀比率，作为更稳定的训练目标，从而提高了在数学推理任务上的性能。

Authors: Shiye Lei, Zhihao Cheng, Dacheng Tao

Vision-Language Models Unlock Task-Centric Latent Actions

Abstract (English): Latent Action Models (LAMs) have rapidly gained traction as an important component in the pre-training pipelines of leading Vision-Language-Action models. However, they fail when observations contain action-correlated distractors, often encoding noise instead of meaningful latent actions. Humans, on the other hand, can effortlessly distinguish task-relevant motions from irrelevant details in any video given only a brief task description. In this work, we propose to utilize the common-sense reasoning abilities of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to provide promptable representations, effectively separating controllable changes from the noise in unsupervised way. We use these representations as targets during LAM training and benchmark a wide variety of popular VLMs, revealing substantial variation in the quality of promptable representations as well as their robustness to different prompts and hyperparameters. Interestingly, we find that more recent VLMs may perform worse than older ones. Finally, we show that simply asking VLMs to ignore distractors can substantially improve latent action quality, yielding up to a six-fold increase in downstream success rates on Distracting MetaWorld.

摘要（中文）: 潜在动作模型 (LAM) 作为领先视觉-语言-动作模型预训练流程中的重要组成部分，已迅速获得关注。然而，当观测包含与动作相关的干扰因素时，它们会失效，常常编码噪声而非有意义的潜在动作。另一方面，人类只需简短的任务描述，就能轻松区分任何视频中与任务相关的运动和不相关的细节。在这项工作中，我们建议利用视觉-语言模型 (VLM) 的常识推理能力来提供可提示的表征，从而以无监督的方式有效地将可控变化与噪声分离。我们使用这些表征作为 LAM 训练期间的目标，并对各种流行的 VLM 进行基准测试，揭示了可提示表征质量的显著差异，以及它们对不同提示和超参数的鲁棒性。有趣的是，我们发现较新的 VLM 可能比旧的 VLM 表现更差。最后，我们表明，仅仅要求 VLM 忽略干扰因素就能显著提高潜在动作的质量，在 Distracting MetaWorld 上使下游成功率提高高达六倍。

TLDR: This paper proposes using Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to improve Latent Action Models (LAMs) by providing promptable representations that filter out action-correlated distractors, leading to significant performance gains in robotic tasks.

简要说明: 本文提出利用视觉语言模型 (VLMs) 通过提供可提示的表达来改进潜在动作模型 (LAMs)，过滤掉与动作相关的干扰因素，从而显著提高机器人任务的性能。

Authors: Alexander Nikulin, Ilya Zisman, Albina Klepach, Denis Tarasov, Alexander Derevyagin, Andrei Polubarov, Lyubaykin Nikita, Vladislav Kurenkov

Best-of-Q: Improving VLM agents with Q-function Action Ranking at Inference

Abstract (English): Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have become powerful backbones for agents to autonomously operate in digital environments like the web and operating systems. However, these models suffer from inadaptability to fast-changing environments like the web, which can be alleviated by fine-tuning requiring expansive model training and data collection. In this work, we introduce a novel paradigm for enhancing agentic VLM policies at inference without policy retraining. Fundamentally, our approach decouples the VLM's role as a high-capacity action proposer from the final action selection mechanism. We keep the VLM policy frozen and use it to generate a set of candidate actions for a given state. Then, a lightweight, offline-trained Q-function reranks these candidates, and the agent executes the action with the highest estimated value. The main contribution is to apply the Q-function directly during inference for immediate policy improvement, and not offline to relabel data for policy retraining. We demonstrate on the academic WebVoyager benchmark that our method significantly boosts agent success rates, improving a Qwen2.5-VL-7B agent from 38.8% to 55.7% and a proprietary GPT-4.1 agent from 82.4% to 88.8%.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言模型（VLMs）已成为强大的骨干网络，用于智能体在数字环境中自主运行，例如网络和操作系统。然而，这些模型难以适应快速变化的环境（如网络），而微调可以缓解这一问题，但需要大量的模型训练和数据收集。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新的范式，用于在推理时增强智能体VLM策略，而无需重新训练策略。从根本上说，我们的方法将VLM作为高容量动作提议者的角色与最终动作选择机制解耦。我们保持VLM策略冻结，并用它为给定状态生成一组候选动作。然后，一个轻量级的、离线训练的Q函数对这些候选动作进行重新排序，智能体执行具有最高估计值的动作。主要的贡献是将Q函数直接应用于推理，以实现即时策略改进，而不是离线地重新标记数据以进行策略再训练。我们在学术WebVoyager基准测试中证明，我们的方法显著提高了智能体的成功率，将Qwen2.5-VL-7B智能体的成功率从38.8%提高到55.7%，并将专有的GPT-4.1智能体的成功率从82.4%提高到88.8%。

TLDR: The paper introduces a method, Best-of-Q, for improving VLM agent performance in dynamic environments by using a Q-function to rerank candidate actions generated by a frozen VLM policy at inference time, demonstrating significant improvements on the WebVoyager benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为 Best-of-Q 的方法，通过在推理时使用 Q 函数对冻结的 VLM 策略生成的候选动作进行重新排序，从而提高 VLM 代理在动态环境中的性能，并在 WebVoyager 基准测试中展示了显著的改进。

Authors: Emilien Biré, María Santos, Kai Yuan

Test-Time Mixture of World Models for Embodied Agents in Dynamic Environments

Abstract (English): Language model (LM)-based embodied agents are increasingly deployed in real-world settings. Yet, their adaptability remains limited in dynamic environments, where constructing accurate and flexible world models is crucial for effective reasoning and decision-making. To address this challenge, we extend the Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) paradigm to embodied agents. While conventional MoE architectures modularize knowledge into expert components with pre-trained routing, they remain rigid once deployed, making them less effective for adapting to unseen domains in dynamic environments. We therefore propose Test-time Mixture of World Models (TMoW), a framework that enhances adaptability to unseen and evolving domains. TMoW updates its routing function over world models at test time, unlike conventional MoE where the function remains fixed, enabling agents to recombine existing models and integrate new ones for continual adaptation. It achieves this through (i) multi-granular prototype-based routing, which adapts mixtures across object- to scene-level similarities, (ii) test-time refinement that aligns unseen domain features with prototypes during inference, and (iii) distilled mixture-based augmentation, which efficiently constructs new models from few-shot data and existing prototypes. We evaluate TMoW on VirtualHome, ALFWorld, and RLBench benchmarks, demonstrating strong performance in both zero-shot adaptation and few-shot expansion scenarios, and showing that it enables embodied agents to operate effectively in dynamic environments.

摘要（中文）: 基于语言模型（LM）的具身智能体正越来越多地部署在现实世界环境中。然而，它们在动态环境中的适应性仍然有限，在这些环境中，构建准确且灵活的世界模型对于有效的推理和决策至关重要。为了应对这一挑战，我们将混合专家（MoE）范式扩展到具身智能体。虽然传统的MoE架构将知识模块化为具有预训练路由的专家组件，但它们一旦部署就变得僵化，使得它们在适应动态环境中未见领域时效果较差。因此，我们提出了测试时世界模型混合（TMoW），一个增强对未见和演化领域适应性的框架。与传统MoE中函数保持固定不同，TMoW在测试时更新其世界模型上的路由函数，使智能体能够重新组合现有模型并集成新模型以进行持续适应。它通过以下方式实现：（i）多粒度原型路由，根据从对象到场景级别的相似性调整混合；（ii）测试时细化，在推理过程中将未见领域的特征与原型对齐；以及（iii）基于混合的蒸馏增强，从少样本数据和现有原型中高效地构建新模型。我们在 VirtualHome、ALFWorld 和 RLBench 基准上评估了 TMoW，证明其在零样本适应和少样本扩展场景中都表现出色，并表明它使具身智能体能够在动态环境中有效运行。

TLDR: The paper introduces TMoW, a framework that extends the Mixture-of-Experts paradigm for embodied agents, enabling them to adapt to dynamic environments by updating the routing function over world models at test time, demonstrating strong zero-shot and few-shot adaptation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TMoW，一个扩展了基于语言模型的具身智能体中混合专家范式的框架，通过在测试时更新世界模型的路由函数，使它们能够适应动态环境，并在零样本和少样本自适应方面表现出色。

Authors: Jinwoo Jang, Minjong Yoo, Sihyung Yoon, Honguk Woo

SYMPHONY: Synergistic Multi-agent Planning with Heterogeneous Language Model Assembly

Abstract (English): Recent advancements have increasingly focused on leveraging large language models (LLMs) to construct autonomous agents for complex problem-solving tasks. However, existing approaches predominantly employ a single-agent framework to generate search branches and estimate rewards during Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) planning. This single-agent paradigm inherently limits exploration capabilities, often resulting in insufficient diversity among generated branches and suboptimal planning performance. To overcome these limitations, we propose Synergistic Multi-agent Planning with Heterogeneous langauge model assembly (SYMPHONY), a novel multi-agent planning framework that integrates a pool of heterogeneous language model-based agents. By leveraging diverse reasoning patterns across agents, SYMPHONY enhances rollout diversity and facilitates more effective exploration. Empirical results across multiple benchmark tasks show that SYMPHONY achieves strong performance even when instantiated with open-source LLMs deployable on consumer-grade hardware. When enhanced with cloud-based LLMs accessible via API, SYMPHONY demonstrates further improvements, outperforming existing state-of-the-art baselines and underscoring the effectiveness of heterogeneous multi-agent coordination in planning tasks.

摘要（中文）: 近期进展越来越关注利用大型语言模型（LLM）构建自主 Agent，用于解决复杂的任务问题。然而，现有方法主要采用单 Agent 框架，在蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）规划期间生成搜索分支并估计奖励。这种单 Agent 范式固有地限制了探索能力，通常导致生成分支间的多样性不足和次优的规划性能。为了克服这些局限性，我们提出了一种名为异构语言模型组装的协同多 Agent 规划（SYMPHONY）的新型多 Agent 规划框架，该框架集成了基于异构语言模型的 Agent 池。通过利用不同 Agent 之间的多样化推理模式，SYMPHONY 提高了 rollout 多样性，并促进了更有效的探索。在多个基准任务上的实验结果表明，即使使用部署在消费级硬件上的开源 LLM 进行实例化，SYMPHONY 也能实现强大的性能。当通过 API 访问的云端 LLM 增强时，SYMPHONY 表现出进一步的改进，超越了现有的最先进基线，并突出了异构多 Agent 协同在规划任务中的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces SYMPHONY, a multi-agent planning framework using a diverse pool of LLMs to enhance exploration and improve performance in complex tasks, achieving strong results with both open-source and cloud-based models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了SYMPHONY，一个使用多样化LLM池的多智能体规划框架，旨在提升探索能力并改善复杂任务中的性能，在使用开源和云端模型时均取得了良好效果。

Authors: Wei Zhu, Zhiwen Tang, Kun Yue

From Self-Evolving Synthetic Data to Verifiable-Reward RL: Post-Training Multi-turn Interactive Tool-Using Agents

Abstract (English): Interactive tool-using agents must solve real-world tasks via multi-turn interaction with both humans and external environments, requiring dialogue state tracking, multi-step tool execution, while following complex instructions. Post-training such agents is challenging because synthesis for high-quality multi-turn tool-use data is difficult to scale, and reinforcement learning (RL) could face noisy signals caused by user simulation, leading to degraded training efficiency. We propose a unified framework that combines a self-evolving data agent with verifier-based RL. Our system, EigenData, is a hierarchical multi-agent engine that synthesizes tool-grounded dialogues together with executable per-instance checkers, and improves generation reliability via closed-loop self-evolving process that updates prompts and workflow. Building on the synthetic data, we develop an RL recipe that first fine-tunes the user model and then applies GRPO-style training with trajectory-level group-relative advantages and dynamic filtering, yielding consistent improvements beyond SFT. Evaluated on tau^2-bench, our best model reaches 73.0% pass^1 on Airline and 98.3% pass^1 on Telecom, matching or exceeding frontier models. Overall, our results suggest a scalable pathway for bootstrapping complex tool-using behaviors without expensive human annotation.

摘要（中文）: 交互式工具使用智能体必须通过与人类和外部环境的多轮交互来解决真实世界的任务，这需要对话状态跟踪、多步骤工具执行以及遵循复杂指令。对这类智能体进行后训练颇具挑战性，因为高质量多轮工具使用数据的合成难以规模化，并且强化学习（RL）可能会面临由用户模拟导致的噪声信号，从而降低训练效率。我们提出了一种统一框架，将自演化数据智能体与基于验证器的强化学习相结合。我们的系统EigenData是一个分层多智能体引擎，它可以合成工具导向的对话，并带有可执行的每实例检查器，并通过闭环自演化过程（更新提示和工作流）来提高生成可靠性。在合成数据的基础上，我们开发了一种强化学习配方，该配方首先对用户模型进行微调，然后应用GRPO风格的训练，同时使用轨迹级别的组相对优势和动态过滤，从而在监督式微调（SFT）的基础上实现持续改进。在tau^2-bench上的评估表明，我们最好的模型在Airline任务上达到了73.0%的通过率（pass^1），在Telecom任务上达到了98.3%的通过率（pass^1），达到或超过了最先进的模型。总而言之，我们的结果表明在无需昂贵的人工标注的情况下，我们可以找到一条可扩展的途径来引导出复杂的工具使用行为。

TLDR: The paper introduces EigenData, a framework using self-evolving synthetic data and verifier-based Reinforcement Learning to train tool-using agents, achieving state-of-the-art performance on multi-turn interactive tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为EigenData的框架，它结合了自演进合成数据和基于验证器的强化学习来训练工具使用代理，并在多轮交互式任务中取得了最先进的性能。

Authors: Jiaxuan Gao, Jiaao Chen, Chuyi He, Wei-Chen Wang, Shusheng Xu, Hanrui Wang, Di Jin, Yi Wu

Learn More with Less: Uncertainty Consistency Guided Query Selection for RLVR

Abstract (English): Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently improved mathematical reasoning through Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR). However, existing RLVR algorithms require large query budgets, making annotation costly. We investigate whether fewer but more informative queries can yield similar or superior performance, introducing active learning (AL) into RLVR. We identify that classic AL sampling strategies fail to outperform random selection in this setting, due to ignoring objective uncertainty when only selecting by subjective uncertainty. This work proposes an uncertainty consistency metric to evaluate how well subjective uncertainty aligns with objective uncertainty. In the offline setting, this alignment is measured using the Point-Biserial Correlation Coefficient (PBC). For online training, because of limited sampling and dynamically shifting output distributions, PBC estimation is difficult. Therefore, we introduce a new online variant, computed from normalized advantage and subjective uncertainty. Theoretically, we prove that the online variant is strictly negatively correlated with offline PBC and supports better sample selection. Experiments show our method consistently outperforms random and classic AL baselines, achieving full-dataset performance while training on only 30% of the data, effectively reducing the cost of RLVR for reasoning tasks.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）最近通过带有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）提高了数学推理能力。然而，现有的RLVR算法需要大量的查询预算，使得标注成本高昂。我们研究了数量较少但信息量更大的查询是否能够产生相似或更优越的性能，并将主动学习（AL）引入到RLVR中。我们发现，经典的AL采样策略在这种设置下无法胜过随机选择，这是因为在仅通过主观不确定性进行选择时，忽略了目标不确定性。本文提出了一种不确定性一致性度量，以评估主观不确定性与目标不确定性的一致程度。在离线设置中，这种一致性使用点二列相关系数（PBC）衡量。对于在线训练，由于采样有限和输出分布动态变化，PBC估计具有挑战性。因此，我们引入了一种新的在线变体，该变体通过归一化的优势函数和主观不确定性计算得出。从理论上讲，我们证明了在线变体与离线PBC严格负相关，并支持更好的样本选择。实验表明，我们的方法始终优于随机和经典的AL基线，在仅使用30%的数据进行训练的情况下实现了完整数据集的性能，从而有效地降低了RLVR在推理任务中的成本。

TLDR: This paper introduces an uncertainty consistency metric to improve active learning for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR), enabling similar performance with significantly less data by addressing the shortcomings of traditional AL sampling strategies.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种不确定性一致性指标，用于改进基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）中的主动学习，通过解决传统主动学习采样策略的不足，以显着更少的数据实现相似的性能。

Authors: Hao Yi, Yulan Hu, Xin Li, Sheng Ouyang, Lizhong Ding, Yong Liu

Mitigating Hallucinations in Video Large Language Models via Spatiotemporal-Semantic Contrastive Decoding

Abstract (English): Although Video Large Language Models perform remarkably well across tasks such as video understanding, question answering, and reasoning, they still suffer from the problem of hallucination, which refers to generating outputs that are inconsistent with explicit video content or factual evidence. However, existing decoding methods for mitigating video hallucinations, while considering the spatiotemporal characteristics of videos, mostly rely on heuristic designs. As a result, they fail to precisely capture the root causes of hallucinations and their fine-grained temporal and semantic correlations, leading to limited robustness and generalization in complex scenarios. To more effectively mitigate video hallucinations, we propose a novel decoding strategy termed Spatiotemporal-Semantic Contrastive Decoding. This strategy constructs negative features by deliberately disrupting the spatiotemporal consistency and semantic associations of video features, and suppresses video hallucinations through contrastive decoding against the original video features during inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method not only effectively mitigates the occurrence of hallucinations, but also preserves the general video understanding and reasoning capabilities of the model.

摘要（中文）: 虽然视频大语言模型在视频理解、问答和推理等任务中表现出色，但它们仍然存在幻觉问题，即生成与明确的视频内容或事实证据不一致的输出。然而，现有的缓解视频幻觉的解码方法，虽然考虑了视频的时空特征，但大多依赖于启发式设计。因此，它们无法精确地捕捉幻觉的根本原因及其细粒度的时间和语义相关性，导致在复杂场景中鲁棒性和泛化性有限。为了更有效地缓解视频幻觉，我们提出了一种新的解码策略，称为时空-语义对比解码。该策略通过故意破坏视频特征的时空一致性和语义关联来构建负特征，并在推理过程中通过与原始视频特征的对比解码来抑制视频幻觉。大量实验表明，我们的方法不仅能有效缓解幻觉的发生，而且还能保留模型的一般视频理解和推理能力。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel decoding strategy, Spatiotemporal-Semantic Contrastive Decoding, to mitigate hallucinations in Video Large Language Models (VLLMs) by contrasting original video features with deliberately disrupted negative features. It claims improved robustness and generalization compared to existing heuristic methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的解码策略，即时空语义对比解码，通过将原始视频特征与故意扰动的负特征进行对比，来减轻视频大型语言模型（VLLM）中的幻觉。 与现有的启发式方法相比，它声称具有更高的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Authors: Yuansheng Gao, Jinman Zhao, Tong Zhang, Xingguo Xu, Han Bao, Zonghui Wang, Wenzhi Chen

PerfGuard: A Performance-Aware Agent for Visual Content Generation

Abstract (English): The advancement of Large Language Model (LLM)-powered agents has enabled automated task processing through reasoning and tool invocation capabilities. However, existing frameworks often operate under the idealized assumption that tool executions are invariably successful, relying solely on textual descriptions that fail to distinguish precise performance boundaries and cannot adapt to iterative tool updates. This gap introduces uncertainty in planning and execution, particularly in domains like visual content generation (AIGC), where nuanced tool performance significantly impacts outcomes. To address this, we propose PerfGuard, a performance-aware agent framework for visual content generation that systematically models tool performance boundaries and integrates them into task planning and scheduling. Our framework introduces three core mechanisms: (1) Performance-Aware Selection Modeling (PASM), which replaces generic tool descriptions with a multi-dimensional scoring system based on fine-grained performance evaluations; (2) Adaptive Preference Update (APU), which dynamically optimizes tool selection by comparing theoretical rankings with actual execution rankings; and (3) Capability-Aligned Planning Optimization (CAPO), which guides the planner to generate subtasks aligned with performance-aware strategies. Experimental comparisons against state-of-the-art methods demonstrate PerfGuard's advantages in tool selection accuracy, execution reliability, and alignment with user intent, validating its robustness and practical utility for complex AIGC tasks. The project code is available at https://github.com/FelixChan9527/PerfGuard.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型 (LLM) 驱动的代理的进步，使得通过推理和工具调用能力实现自动化任务处理成为可能。然而，现有框架通常在工具执行总是成功这种理想化假设下运行，仅仅依赖于无法区分精确性能边界且无法适应迭代式工具更新的文本描述。这种差距在规划和执行中引入了不确定性，尤其是在视觉内容生成 (AIGC) 等领域，细微的工具性能会显著影响结果。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 PerfGuard，一种用于视觉内容生成的性能感知代理框架，它系统地建模工具性能边界，并将它们集成到任务规划和调度中。我们的框架引入了三个核心机制：（1）性能感知选择建模 (PASM)，它用基于细粒度性能评估的多维评分系统取代了通用的工具描述；（2）自适应偏好更新 (APU)，它通过比较理论排名与实际执行排名，动态地优化工具选择；以及（3）能力对齐规划优化 (CAPO)，它引导规划器生成与性能感知策略对齐的子任务。与最先进方法的实验比较表明，PerfGuard 在工具选择准确性、执行可靠性以及与用户意图的对齐方面具有优势，验证了其在复杂 AIGC 任务中的鲁棒性和实用性。项目代码可在 https://github.com/FelixChan9527/PerfGuard 获取。

TLDR: PerfGuard is a performance-aware agent framework for visual content generation that models tool performance boundaries and integrates them into task planning, demonstrating improved tool selection accuracy and execution reliability.

简要说明: PerfGuard是一个性能感知的视觉内容生成代理框架，它对工具性能边界进行建模，并将其集成到任务规划中，展示了更高的工具选择准确性和执行可靠性。

Authors: Zhipeng Chen, Zhongrui Zhang, Chao Zhang, Yifan Xu, Lan Yang, Jun Liu, Ke Li, Yi-Zhe Song

Darwinian Memory: A Training-Free Self-Regulating Memory System for GUI Agent Evolution

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) agents facilitate Graphical User Interface (GUI) automation but struggle with long-horizon, cross-application tasks due to limited context windows. While memory systems provide a viable solution, existing paradigms struggle to adapt to dynamic GUI environments, suffering from a granularity mismatch between high-level intent and low-level execution, and context pollution where the static accumulation of outdated experiences drives agents into hallucination. To address these bottlenecks, we propose the Darwinian Memory System (DMS), a self-evolving architecture that constructs memory as a dynamic ecosystem governed by the law of survival of the fittest. DMS decomposes complex trajectories into independent, reusable units for compositional flexibility, and implements Utility-driven Natural Selection to track survival value, actively pruning suboptimal paths and inhibiting high-risk plans. This evolutionary pressure compels the agent to derive superior strategies. Extensive experiments on real-world multi-app benchmarks validate that DMS boosts general-purpose MLLMs without training costs or architectural overhead, achieving average gains of 18.0% in success rate and 33.9% in execution stability, while reducing task latency, establishing it as an effective self-evolving memory system for GUI tasks.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型 (MLLM) 智能体促进了图形用户界面 (GUI) 自动化，但由于上下文窗口的限制，它们在长时程、跨应用程序的任务中表现不佳。虽然记忆系统提供了一个可行的解决方案，但现有的范式难以适应动态的 GUI 环境，遭受着高层意图和低层执行之间的粒度不匹配，以及静态积累的过时经验导致智能体产生幻觉的上下文污染。为了解决这些瓶颈，我们提出了达尔文记忆系统 (DMS)，这是一种自我进化的架构，它将记忆构建为一个由适者生存法则所支配的动态生态系统。DMS 将复杂的轨迹分解为独立的、可重用的单元，以实现组合灵活性，并实施效用驱动的自然选择来追踪生存价值，主动剪除次优路径并抑制高风险计划。这种进化压力促使智能体推导出更优的策略。在真实世界的多元应用基准测试中的大量实验验证了 DMS 可以提升通用 MLLM 的性能，而无需训练成本或架构开销，在成功率方面平均提升 18.0%，在执行稳定性方面平均提升 33.9%，同时降低了任务延迟，从而确立了其作为 GUI 任务的有效自我进化记忆系统的地位。

TLDR: The paper proposes a Darwinian Memory System (DMS) for GUI automation agents that dynamically adapts to GUI environments by pruning suboptimal plans and promoting superior strategies, improving success rates and stability without training.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于GUI自动化代理的达尔文记忆系统（DMS），该系统通过剪除次优计划并促进卓越策略来动态适应GUI环境，从而在无需训练的情况下提高成功率和稳定性。

Authors: Hongze Mi, Yibo Feng, WenJie Lu, Song Cao, Jinyuan Li, Yanming Li, Xuelin Zhang, Haotian Luo, Songyang Peng, He Cui, Tengfei Tian, Jun Fang, Hua Chai, Naiqiang Tan

Recoverability Has a Law: The ERR Measure for Tool-Augmented Agents

Abstract (English): Language model agents often appear capable of self-recovery after failing tool call executions, yet this behavior lacks a formal explanation. We present a predictive theory that resolves this gap by showing that recoverability follows a measurable law. To elaborate, we formalize recoverability through Expected Recovery Regret (ERR), which quantifies the deviation of a recovery policy from the optimal one under stochastic execution noise, and derive a first-order relationship between ERR and an empirical observable quantity, the Efficiency Score (ES). This yields a falsifiable first-order quantitative law of recovery dynamics in tool-using agents. We empirically validate the law across five tool-use benchmarks spanning controlled perturbations, diagnostic reasoning, and real-world APIs. Across model scales, perturbation regimes, and recovery horizons, predicted regret under the ERR-ES law closely matched observed post-failure regret measured from Monte Carlo rollouts, within delta less than or equal to 0.05. Our results reveal that recoverability is not an artifact of model scale or architecture, but a governed property of interaction dynamics, providing a theoretical foundation for execution-level robustness in language agents.

摘要（中文）: 语言模型智能体在工具调用执行失败后通常表现出自我恢复的能力，但这种行为缺乏正式的解释。为了弥补这一空白，我们提出了一种预测理论，表明可恢复性遵循一个可测量的定律。具体来说，我们通过期望恢复遗憾（ERR）来形式化可恢复性，它量化了在随机执行噪声下恢复策略与最优策略之间的偏差，并推导了ERR与一个可观察的经验指标——效率得分（ES）之间的一阶关系。这产生了一个可证伪的关于工具使用型智能体中恢复动态的一阶定量定律。我们在五个工具使用基准上，通过受控扰动、诊断推理和真实世界API，对该定律进行了经验验证。在不同的模型规模、扰动机制和恢复范围内，根据ERR-ES定律预测的遗憾与从蒙特卡洛展开中测得的失败后观察到的遗憾相似度很高，差异小于等于0.05。我们的结果表明，可恢复性不是模型规模或架构的人为产物，而是交互动态的一个受支配的属性，为语言智能体中的执行层鲁棒性提供了理论基础。

TLDR: This paper introduces a formal measure (ERR) and an empirical observable (ES) to quantify and predict the recoverability of tool-augmented language agents after failed tool calls, demonstrating its validity across various benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种形式化的度量 (ERR) 和一个经验可观察量 (ES)，用于量化和预测工具增强型语言智能体在工具调用失败后的可恢复性，并在各种基准测试中验证了其有效性。

Authors: Sri Vatsa Vuddanti, Satwik Kumar Chittiprolu

Why Reasoning Fails to Plan: A Planning-Centric Analysis of Long-Horizon Decision Making in LLM Agents

Abstract (English): Large language model (LLM)-based agents exhibit strong step-by-step reasoning capabilities over short horizons, yet often fail to sustain coherent behavior over long planning horizons. We argue that this failure reflects a fundamental mismatch: step-wise reasoning induces a form of step-wise greedy policy that is adequate for short horizons but fails in long-horizon planning, where early actions must account for delayed consequences. From this planning-centric perspective, we study LLM-based agents in deterministic, fully structured environments with explicit state transitions and evaluation signals. Our analysis reveals a core failure mode of reasoning-based policies: locally optimal choices induced by step-wise scoring lead to early myopic commitments that are systematically amplified over time and difficult to recover from. We introduce FLARE (Future-aware Lookahead with Reward Estimation) as a minimal instantiation of future-aware planning to enforce explicit lookahead, value propagation, and limited commitment in a single model, allowing downstream outcomes to influence early decisions. Across multiple benchmarks, agent frameworks, and LLM backbones, FLARE consistently improves task performance and planning-level behavior, frequently allowing LLaMA-8B with FLARE to outperform GPT-4o with standard step-by-step reasoning. These results establish a clear distinction between reasoning and planning.

摘要（中文）: 基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体在短时间内展现出强大的逐步推理能力，但往往无法在长程规划中维持连贯的行为。我们认为这种失败反映了一个根本性的不匹配：逐步推理产生了一种短视的贪婪策略，这种策略足以应对短程场景，但在长程规划中却失效，因为早期行动必须考虑到延迟的影响。从这个以规划为中心的角度出发，我们在具有显式状态转移和评估信号的、确定性的、完全结构化的环境中研究了基于LLM的智能体。我们的分析揭示了基于推理的策略的一个核心失效模式：由逐步评分导致的局部最优选择会导致早期的短视承诺，这些承诺会随着时间的推移被系统性地放大，并且难以挽回。我们引入了FLARE（具有奖励估计的未来感知前瞻），作为未来感知型规划的一个最小实例化，以便在单个模型中强制执行显式的前瞻、价值传播和有限承诺，从而允许下游结果影响早期决策。在多个基准测试、智能体框架和LLM骨干网络中，FLARE始终如一地提高了任务性能和规划层面的行为，经常使得配备FLARE的LLaMA-8B胜过具有标准逐步推理的GPT-4o。这些结果确立了推理和规划之间的一个明确区别。

TLDR: The paper identifies a mismatch between step-wise reasoning in LLMs and long-horizon planning, proposes FLARE for future-aware planning, and demonstrates its effectiveness in improving task performance across diverse benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文指出LLM中逐步推理与长程规划之间的不匹配，提出了FLARE用于未来感知的规划，并证明了其在提高各种基准测试中的任务性能方面的有效性。

Authors: Zehong Wang, Fang Wu, Hongru Wang, Xiangru Tang, Bolian Li, Zhenfei Yin, Yijun Ma, Yiyang Li, Weixiang Sun, Xiusi Chen, Yanfang Ye

Exploring Reasoning Reward Model for Agents

Abstract (English): Agentic Reinforcement Learning (Agentic RL) has achieved notable success in enabling agents to perform complex reasoning and tool use. However, most methods still relies on sparse outcome-based reward for training. Such feedback fails to differentiate intermediate reasoning quality, leading to suboptimal training results. In this paper, we introduce Agent Reasoning Reward Model (Agent-RRM), a multi-faceted reward model that produces structured feedback for agentic trajectories, including (1) an explicit reasoning trace , (2) a focused critique that provides refinement guidance by highlighting reasoning flaws, and (3) an overall score that evaluates process performance. Leveraging these signals, we systematically investigate three integration strategies: Reagent-C (text-augmented refinement), Reagent-R (reward-augmented guidance), and Reagent-U (unified feedback integration). Extensive evaluations across 12 diverse benchmarks demonstrate that Reagent-U yields substantial performance leaps, achieving 43.7% on GAIA and 46.2% on WebWalkerQA, validating the effectiveness of our reasoning reward model and training schemes. Code, models, and datasets are all released to facilitate future research.

摘要（中文）: 主动式强化学习（Agentic RL）已在使智能体执行复杂推理和工具使用方面取得了显著成功。然而，大多数方法仍然依赖于基于稀疏结果的奖励进行训练。这种反馈无法区分中间推理质量，导致次优的训练结果。在本文中，我们引入了智能体推理奖励模型（Agent-RRM），这是一个多方面的奖励模型，为主动式轨迹生成结构化反馈，包括（1）显式推理轨迹，（2）通过突出推理缺陷提供改进指导的重点评论，以及（3）评估过程性能的总体评分。利用这些信号，我们系统地研究了三种集成策略：Reagent-C（文本增强型改进）、Reagent-R（奖励增强型指导）和Reagent-U（统一反馈集成）。在12个不同的基准测试中进行的大量评估表明，Reagent-U产生了显著的性能飞跃，在GAIA上实现了43.7%的提升，在WebWalkerQA上实现了46.2%的提升，验证了我们的推理奖励模型和训练方案的有效性。代码、模型和数据集均已发布，以促进未来的研究。

TLDR: The paper introduces Agent-RRM, a multi-faceted reward model for agentic RL that provides structured feedback including reasoning traces, critiques, and scores. It demonstrates significant performance improvements on various benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了 Agent-RRM，一种用于智能体强化学习的多方面奖励模型，它提供结构化的反馈，包括推理轨迹、评论和分数。它在各种基准测试中表现出显著的性能提升。

Authors: Kaixuan Fan, Kaituo Feng, Manyuan Zhang, Tianshuo Peng, Zhixun Li, Yilei Jiang, Shuang Chen, Peng Pei, Xunliang Cai, Xiangyu Yue

DynaWeb: Model-Based Reinforcement Learning of Web Agents

Abstract (English): The development of autonomous web agents, powered by Large Language Models (LLMs) and reinforcement learning (RL), represents a significant step towards general-purpose AI assistants. However, training these agents is severely hampered by the challenges of interacting with the live internet, which is inefficient, costly, and fraught with risks. Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) offers a promising solution by learning a world model of the environment to enable simulated interaction. This paper introduces DynaWeb, a novel MBRL framework that trains web agents through interacting with a web world model trained to predict naturalistic web page representations given agent actions. This model serves as a synthetic web environment where an agent policy can dream by generating vast quantities of rollout action trajectories for efficient online reinforcement learning. Beyond free policy rollouts, DynaWeb incorporates real expert trajectories from training data, which are randomly interleaved with on-policy rollouts during training to improve stability and sample efficiency. Experiments conducted on the challenging WebArena and WebVoyager benchmarks demonstrate that DynaWeb consistently and significantly improves the performance of state-of-the-art open-source web agent models. Our findings establish the viability of training web agents through imagination, offering a scalable and efficient way to scale up online agentic RL.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 由大型语言模型 (LLM) 和强化学习 (RL) 驱动的自主网络代理的开发，代表着迈向通用人工智能助手的重要一步。然而，训练这些代理严重受到与实时互联网交互所带来的挑战的阻碍，这既低效又昂贵，且充满风险。基于模型的强化学习 (MBRL) 通过学习环境的世界模型来实现模拟交互，提供了一个有前景的解决方案。本文介绍了一种新型 MBRL 框架 DynaWeb，它通过与网络世界模型交互来训练网络代理，该模型旨在根据代理行为预测自然的网络页面表示。该模型充当了一个合成网络环境，代理策略可以通过生成大量的 rollout 行为轨迹来梦想，从而实现高效的在线强化学习。除了自由策略 rollout 之外，DynaWeb 还整合了来自训练数据的真实专家轨迹，这些轨迹在训练期间与 on-policy rollout 随机交织，以提高稳定性和样本效率。在具有挑战性的 WebArena 和 WebVoyager 基准测试中进行的实验表明，DynaWeb 持续且显著地提高了最先进的开源网络代理模型的性能。我们的研究结果确立了通过想象训练网络代理的可行性，从而提供了一种可扩展且高效的方式来扩大在线代理 RL。

TLDR: DynaWeb is a novel model-based RL framework using a learned world model to train web agents with improved efficiency and stability, achieving strong performance on WebArena and WebVoyager benchmarks.

简要说明: DynaWeb 是一种新颖的基于模型的强化学习框架，它使用学习到的世界模型来训练 Web 代理，从而提高效率和稳定性，并在 WebArena 和 WebVoyager 基准测试中实现了强大的性能。

Authors: Hang Ding, Peidong Liu, Junqiao Wang, Ziwei Ji, Meng Cao, Rongzhao Zhang, Lynn Ai, Eric Yang, Tianyu Shi, Lei Yu

Triage: Hierarchical Visual Budgeting for Efficient Video Reasoning in Vision-Language Models

Abstract (English): Vision-Language Models (VLMs) face significant computational challenges in video processing due to massive data redundancy, which creates prohibitively long token sequences. To address this, we introduce Triage, a training-free, plug-and-play framework that reframes video reasoning as a resource allocation problem via hierarchical visual budgeting. Its first stage, Frame-Level Budgeting, identifies keyframes by evaluating their visual dynamics and relevance, generating a strategic prior based on their importance scores. Guided by this prior, the second stage, Token-Level Budgeting, allocates tokens in two phases: it first secures high-relevance Core Tokens, followed by diverse Context Tokens selected with an efficient batched Maximal Marginal Relevance (MMR) algorithm. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Triage improves inference speed and reduces memory footprint, while maintaining or surpassing the performance of baselines and other methods on various video reasoning benchmarks.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言模型（VLMs）在视频处理中面临着巨大的计算挑战，这是由于大量的数据冗余导致了过长的token序列。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了Triage，一个无需训练、即插即用的框架，它通过分层视觉预算将视频推理重新定义为一个资源分配问题。它的第一阶段，帧级别预算，通过评估关键帧的视觉动态和相关性来识别关键帧，从而基于其重要性得分生成一个战略先验。在这一先验的指导下，第二阶段，token级别预算，分两个阶段分配token：首先确保高相关性的核心Token，然后使用高效的批量最大边缘相关性（MMR）算法选择多样化的上下文Token。大量的实验表明，Triage提高了推理速度并减少了内存占用，同时在各种视频推理基准测试中保持或超过了基线和其他方法的性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Triage, a training-free framework for efficient video reasoning in VLMs via hierarchical visual budgeting, improving speed and reducing memory while maintaining performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Triage，一个免训练的框架，通过分层视觉预算来实现VLM中高效的视频推理，从而提高速度并减少内存，同时保持性能。

VisionTrim: Unified Vision Token Compression for Training-Free MLLM Acceleration

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) suffer from high computational costs due to excessive visual tokens, particularly in high-resolution and video-based scenarios. Existing token reduction methods typically focus on isolated pipeline components and often neglect textual alignment, leading to performance degradation. In this paper, we propose VisionTrim, a unified framework for training-free MLLM acceleration, integrating two effective plug-and-play modules: 1) the Dominant Vision Token Selection (DVTS) module, which preserves essential visual tokens via a global-local view, and 2) the Text-Guided Vision Complement (TGVC) module, which facilitates context-aware token merging guided by textual cues. Extensive experiments across diverse image and video multimodal benchmarks demonstrate the performance superiority of our VisionTrim, advancing practical MLLM deployment in real-world applications. The code is available at: https://github.com/hanxunyu/VisionTrim.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）由于过多的视觉tokens而面临高计算成本，尤其是在高分辨率和基于视频的场景中。现有的token缩减方法通常侧重于孤立的pipeline组件，并且常常忽视文本对齐，导致性能下降。本文提出VisionTrim，一个用于无需训练的MLLM加速的统一框架，集成了两个有效的即插即用模块：1）主导视觉Token 选择（DVTS）模块，通过全局-局部视角保留必要的视觉tokens；2）文本引导的视觉补充（TGVC）模块，有助于在文本线索指导下进行上下文感知的token合并。在各种图像和视频多模态基准上的大量实验证明了我们VisionTrim的性能优势，推动了MLLM在实际应用中的部署。代码可在以下链接获取：https://github.com/hanxunyu/VisionTrim。

Authors: Hanxun Yu, Wentong Li, Xuan Qu, Song Wang, Junbo Chen, Jianke Zhu

PhoStream: Benchmarking Real-World Streaming for Omnimodal Assistants in Mobile Scenarios

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models excel at offline audio-visual understanding, but their ability to serve as mobile assistants in continuous real-world streams remains underexplored. In daily phone use, mobile assistants must track streaming audio-visual inputs and respond at the right time, yet existing benchmarks are often restricted to multiple-choice questions or use shorter videos. In this paper, we introduce PhoStream, the first mobile-centric streaming benchmark that unifies on-screen and off-screen scenarios to evaluate video, audio, and temporal reasoning. PhoStream contains 5,572 open-ended QA pairs from 578 videos across 4 scenarios and 10 capabilities. We build it with an Automated Generative Pipeline backed by rigorous human verification, and evaluate models using a realistic Online Inference Pipeline and LLM-as-a-Judge evaluation for open-ended responses. Experiments reveal a temporal asymmetry in LLM-judged scores (0-100): models perform well on Instant and Backward tasks (Gemini 3 Pro exceeds 80), but drop sharply on Forward tasks (16.40), largely due to early responses before the required visual and audio cues appear. This highlights a fundamental limitation: current MLLMs struggle to decide when to speak, not just what to say. Code and datasets used in this work will be made publicly accessible at https://github.com/Lucky-Lance/PhoStream.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型擅长离线音视频理解，但它们在持续真实世界流中作为移动助手的能力仍未得到充分探索。在日常手机使用中，移动助手必须跟踪流式音视频输入并在正确的时间做出响应，然而现有的基准测试通常局限于多项选择题或使用较短的视频。在本文中，我们推出了PhoStream，这是第一个以移动为中心的流式基准测试，它统一了屏幕上和屏幕外的场景以评估视频、音频和时间推理。PhoStream包含来自578个视频的5572个开放式问答对，涵盖4个场景和10项能力。我们通过一个由严格的人工验证支持的自动化生成流程构建了它，并使用一个真实的在线推理流程和LLM-as-a-Judge评估方法来评估模型的开放式回答。实验揭示了LLM评分（0-100）中的时间不对称性：模型在即时和回溯任务中表现良好（Gemini 3 Pro超过80），但在前瞻任务中急剧下降（16.40），这主要是由于在所需的视觉和音频提示出现之前就进行了早期响应。这突显了一个根本性的局限：当前的MLLM难以决定何时说话，而不仅仅是说什么。本工作中使用的代码和数据集将在https://github.com/Lucky-Lance/PhoStream上公开提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces PhoStream, a new mobile-centric streaming benchmark for evaluating multimodal LLMs in real-world mobile assistant scenarios, highlighting the difficulty current models have in determining *when* to respond to streaming audio-visual inputs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PhoStream，这是一个新的以移动设备为中心的流媒体基准，用于评估多模态LLM在现实移动助手场景中的表现，强调了当前模型在确定*何时*响应流式音视频输入方面存在的困难。

Authors: Xudong Lu, Huankang Guan, Yang Bo, Jinpeng Chen, Xintong Guo, Shuhan Li, Fang Liu, Peiwen Sun, Xueying Li, Wei Zhang, Xue Yang, Rui Liu, Hongsheng Li

From Absolute to Relative: Rethinking Reward Shaping in Group-Based Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning has become a cornerstone for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models, where group-based approaches such as GRPO have emerged as efficient paradigms that optimize policies by leveraging intra-group performance differences. However, these methods typically rely on absolute numerical rewards, introducing intrinsic limitations. In verifiable tasks, identical group evaluations often result in sparse supervision, while in open-ended scenarios, the score range instability of reward models undermines advantage estimation based on group means. To address these limitations, we propose Reinforcement Learning with Relative Rewards (RLRR), a framework that shifts reward shaping from absolute scoring to relative ranking. Complementing this framework, we introduce the Ranking Reward Model, a listwise preference model tailored for group-based optimization to directly generate relative rankings. By transforming raw evaluations into robust relative signals, RLRR effectively mitigates signal sparsity and reward instability. Experimental results demonstrate that RLRR yields consistent performance improvements over standard group-based baselines across reasoning benchmarks and open-ended generation tasks.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习已成为增强大型语言模型推理能力的重要基石，其中 GRPO 等基于群体的方法已成为高效的范式，通过利用群体内部的性能差异来优化策略。然而，这些方法通常依赖于绝对数值奖励，从而引入了内在的局限性。在可验证的任务中，相同的群体评估通常导致稀疏的监督信号；而在开放式场景中，奖励模型的评分范围不稳定会破坏基于群体均值的优势估计。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了基于相对奖励的强化学习 (RLRR)，该框架将奖励塑造从绝对评分转变为相对排名。作为该框架的补充，我们引入了排名奖励模型 (Ranking Reward Model)，这是一种为基于群体的优化量身定制的列表式偏好模型，用于直接生成相对排名。通过将原始评估转化为稳健的相对信号，RLRR 有效地缓解了信号稀疏性和奖励不稳定性。实验结果表明，在推理基准测试和开放式生成任务中，RLRR 相对于标准基于群体的基线方法，均能产生持续的性能提升。

TLDR: The paper introduces Reinforcement Learning with Relative Rewards (RLRR), a framework that uses relative ranking instead of absolute rewards in group-based RL, addressing signal sparsity and reward instability issues, and demonstrating performance improvements in reasoning and generation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了具有相对奖励的强化学习（RLRR）框架，该框架在基于群体的强化学习中使用相对排序而不是绝对奖励，解决了信号稀疏性和奖励不稳定性问题，并在推理和生成任务中展示了性能改进。
