Authors: Wenzhe Niu, Wei He, Zongxia Xie, Jinpeng Ou, Huichuan Fan, Yuchen Ge, Yanru Sun, Ziyin Wang, Yizhao Sun, Chengshun Shi, Jiuchong Gao, Jinghua Hao, Renqing He

Divide-and-Conquer CoT: RL for Reducing Latency via Parallel Reasoning

Abstract (English): Long chain-of-thought reasoning (Long CoT) is now fundamental to state-of-the-art LLMs, especially in mathematical reasoning. However, LLM generation is highly sequential, and long CoTs lead to a high latency. We propose to train Divide-and-Conquer CoT (DC-CoT) to reduce the latency. With DC-CoT, the model can act as a director that identifies distinct subtasks that can be performed in parallel in its reasoning process, and then spawns workers to execute the subtasks. Our goal is to achieve high accuracy, with a low longest path length, which is a theoretical measure of the latency needed for the response. We start with a long CoT base model (DeepScaleR-1.5B-Preview), and first use SFT with a small curated demonstration set to initialize its ability to spawn workers in a certain format. Because SFT degrades the accuracy significantly, we design a multi-stage RL algorithm, with various data filtering strategies, to recover the accuracy while decreasing the longest path length. Across several benchmarks including AIME 2024 and HMMT 2025, DC-CoT achieves similar accuracy as DeepScaleR-1.5B-Preview while decreasing longest path length by 35-40%. Our code, SFT dataset and models are publicly available at https://github.com/amahankali10/DC_CoT_RL_for_Low_Latency_CoT_with_Parallel_Reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 长程思维链推理（Long CoT）现在是先进大型语言模型（LLM）的基础，尤其是在数学推理方面。然而，LLM的生成过程高度序列化，而长CoT会导致高延迟。我们提出训练分而治之CoT（DC-CoT）来降低延迟。使用DC-CoT，模型可以充当指导者，识别推理过程中可以并行执行的不同子任务，然后生成工作者来执行这些子任务。我们的目标是在保持高准确率的同时，降低最长路径长度，这是响应所需延迟的理论度量。我们从一个长CoT基础模型（DeepScaleR-1.5B-Preview）开始，首先使用SFT和一个小的精选演示集来初始化其以特定格式生成工作者的能力。由于SFT会显著降低准确率，我们设计了一个多阶段RL算法，结合各种数据过滤策略，以在降低最长路径长度的同时恢复准确率。在包括AIME 2024和HMMT 2025在内的多个基准测试中，DC-CoT实现了与DeepScaleR-1.5B-Preview相似的准确率，同时最长路径长度降低了35-40%。我们的代码、SFT数据集和模型已在https://github.com/amahankali10/DC_CoT_RL_for_Low_Latency_CoT_with_Parallel_Reasoning上公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces Divide-and-Conquer CoT (DC-CoT), a reinforcement learning approach to reduce the latency of long chain-of-thought reasoning in LLMs by parallelizing subtasks, achieving comparable accuracy to the base model with significantly reduced longest path length.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Divide-and-Conquer CoT (DC-CoT)，一种通过并行化子任务来减少LLM中长链式思考推理延迟的强化学习方法，在实现与基础模型相当的准确率的同时，显著降低了最长路径长度。

Authors: Arvind Mahankali, Kaiyue Wen, Tengyu Ma

Mem-T: Densifying Rewards for Long-Horizon Memory Agents

Abstract (English): Memory agents, which depart from predefined memory-processing pipelines by endogenously managing the processing, storage, and retrieval of memories, have garnered increasing attention for their autonomy and adaptability. However, existing training paradigms remain constrained: agents often traverse long-horizon sequences of memory operations before receiving sparse and delayed rewards, which hinders truly end-to-end optimization of memory management policies. To address this limitation, we introduce Mem-T, an autonomous memory agent that interfaces with a lightweight hierarchical memory database to perform dynamic updates and multi-turn retrieval over streaming inputs. To effectively train long-horizon memory management capabilities, we further propose MoT-GRPO, a tree-guided reinforcement learning framework that transforms sparse terminal feedback into dense, step-wise supervision via memory operation tree backpropagation and hindsight credit assignment, thereby enabling the joint optimization of memory construction and retrieval. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Mem-T is (1) high-performing, surpassing frameworks such as A-Mem and Mem0 by up to $14.92\%$, and (2) economical, operating on a favorable accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier and reducing inference tokens per query by $\sim24.45\%$ relative to GAM without sacrificing performance.

摘要（中文）: 记忆代理，凭借其自主性和适应性，越来越受到关注，这类代理摆脱了预定义的记忆处理流程，能够内生地管理记忆的处理、存储和检索。然而，现有的训练范式仍然存在局限：代理通常在收到稀疏且延迟的回报之前，需要遍历长期的记忆操作序列，这阻碍了记忆管理策略的真正端到端优化。为了解决这一局限性，我们引入了Mem-T，一种自主记忆代理，它与一个轻量级的分层记忆数据库交互，以对流式输入执行动态更新和多轮检索。为了有效地训练长期的记忆管理能力，我们进一步提出了MoT-GRPO，一种树引导的强化学习框架，该框架通过记忆操作树反向传播和后见之明信用分配，将稀疏的终端反馈转化为密集的逐步监督，从而实现记忆构建和检索的联合优化。大量的实验表明，Mem-T具有以下优点：（1）高性能，超越了A-Mem和Mem0等框架，最高提升达到14.92%；（2）经济性，运作在有利的准确率-效率帕累托前沿，并且相对于GAM，在不牺牲性能的前提下，每次查询减少约24.45%的推理tokens。

TLDR: The paper introduces Mem-T, an autonomous memory agent trained with a novel tree-guided reinforcement learning framework (MoT-GRPO) to improve long-horizon memory management, demonstrating superior performance and efficiency compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Mem-T，一种自主记忆代理，通过一种新的树引导强化学习框架(MoT-GRPO)进行训练，以改进长时程记忆管理。实验表明，与现有方法相比，该方法具有更优越的性能和效率。

Authors: Yanwei Yue, Guibin Zhang, Boci Peng, Xuanbo Fan, Jiaxin Guo, Qiankun Li, Yan Zhang

PlatoLTL: Learning to Generalize Across Symbols in LTL Instructions for Multi-Task RL

Abstract (English): A central challenge in multi-task reinforcement learning (RL) is to train generalist policies capable of performing tasks not seen during training. To facilitate such generalization, linear temporal logic (LTL) has recently emerged as a powerful formalism for specifying structured, temporally extended tasks to RL agents. While existing approaches to LTL-guided multi-task RL demonstrate successful generalization across LTL specifications, they are unable to generalize to unseen vocabularies of propositions (or "symbols"), which describe high-level events in LTL. We present PlatoLTL, a novel approach that enables policies to zero-shot generalize not only compositionally across LTL formula structures, but also parametrically across propositions. We achieve this by treating propositions as instances of parameterized predicates rather than discrete symbols, allowing policies to learn shared structure across related propositions. We propose a novel architecture that embeds and composes predicates to represent LTL specifications, and demonstrate successful zero-shot generalization to novel propositions and tasks across challenging environments.

摘要（中文）: 多任务强化学习（RL）的核心挑战是训练能够执行训练过程中未见任务的通用策略。为促进这种泛化，线性时序逻辑（LTL）最近作为一种强大的形式化方法出现，用于向RL智能体指定结构化、时间扩展的任务。虽然现有的LTL引导的多任务RL方法在LTL规范中展示了成功的泛化能力，但它们无法泛化到未见的命题词汇表（或“符号”），这些符号描述了LTL中的高级事件。我们提出了PlatoLTL，一种新颖的方法，使策略不仅可以在LTL公式结构中进行组合泛化，还可以在命题中进行参数泛化，从而实现零样本泛化。我们通过将命题视为参数化谓词的实例而不是离散符号来实现这一点，从而允许策略学习相关命题之间的共享结构。我们提出了一种新颖的架构，该架构嵌入并组合谓词以表示LTL规范，并在具有挑战性的环境中展示了对新命题和任务的成功零样本泛化。

TLDR: The paper introduces PlatoLTL, an RL method that enables zero-shot generalization across both LTL formula structures and unseen vocabularies of propositions by treating propositions as parameterized predicates and learning shared structure.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PlatoLTL，一种RL方法，它通过将命题视为参数化谓词并学习共享结构，实现了在LTL公式结构和未见过的命题词汇表上的零样本泛化。

Authors: Jacques Cloete, Mathias Jackermeier, Ioannis Havoutis, Alessandro Abate

HeaPA: Difficulty-Aware Heap Sampling and On-Policy Query Augmentation for LLM Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): RLVR is now a standard way to train LLMs on reasoning tasks with verifiable outcomes, but when rollout generation dominates the cost, efficiency depends heavily on which prompts you sample and when. In practice, prompt pools are often static or only loosely tied to the model's learning progress, so uniform sampling can't keep up with the shifting capability frontier and ends up wasting rollouts on prompts that are already solved or still out of reach. Existing approaches improve efficiency through filtering, curricula, adaptive rollout allocation, or teacher guidance, but they typically assume a fixed pool-which makes it hard to support stable on-policy pool growth-or they add extra teacher cost and latency. We introduce HeaPA (Heap Sampling and On-Policy Query Augmentation), which maintains a bounded, evolving pool, tracks the frontier using heap-based boundary sampling, expands the pool via on-policy augmentation with lightweight asynchronous validation, and stabilizes correlated queries through topology-aware re-estimation of pool statistics and controlled reinsertion. Across two training corpora, two training recipes, and seven benchmarks, HeaPA consistently improves accuracy and reaches target performance with fewer computations while keeping wall-clock time comparable. Our analyses suggest these gains come from frontier-focused sampling and on-policy pool growth, with the benefits becoming larger as model scale increases. Our code is available at https://github.com/horizon-rl/HeaPA.

摘要（中文）: RLVR现在是训练LLM解决具有可验证结果的推理任务的标准方法。然而，当rollout生成占据主要成本时，效率会高度依赖于你采样的提示以及采样的时间。在实践中，提示池通常是静态的，或仅与模型的学习进度松散关联，因此均匀采样无法跟上不断变化的能力前沿，最终导致rollout被浪费在已解决或仍无法触及的提示上。现有方法通过过滤、课程、自适应rollout分配或教师指导来提高效率，但它们通常假设一个固定的池——这使得难以支持稳定的on-policy池增长——或者它们会增加额外的教师成本和延迟。我们引入了HeaPA (Heap Sampling and On-Policy Query Augmentation，堆采样和On-Policy查询增强)，它维护一个有界、可演化的池，使用基于堆的边界采样来跟踪前沿，通过带有轻量级异步验证的on-policy增强来扩展池，并通过拓扑感知的池统计信息重新估计和受控的重新插入来稳定相关查询。在两个训练语料库、两种训练方案和七个基准测试中，HeaPA始终如一地提高准确性，并以更少的计算量达到目标性能，同时保持相近的挂钟时间。我们的分析表明，这些收益来自于以frontier为中心的采样和on-policy池增长，并且随着模型规模的增加，收益会变得更大。我们的代码可在https://github.com/horizon-rl/HeaPA获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces HeaPA, a method for efficient LLM reinforcement learning that uses heap-based sampling and on-policy query augmentation to focus rollouts on prompts at the learning frontier, improving accuracy and computational efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HeaPA，一种高效的LLM强化学习方法，通过堆式抽样和在线策略查询增强，集中rollout在学习前沿的提示上，从而提高准确性和计算效率。

Authors: Weiqi Wang, Xin Liu, Binxuan Huang, Hejie Cui, Rongzhi Zhang, Changlong Yu, Shuowei Jin, Jingfeng Yang, Qingyu Yin, Zhengyang Wang, Zheng Li, Yifan Gao, Priyanka Nigam, Bing Yin, Lihong Li, Yangqiu Song

SAIR: Cost-Efficient Multi-Stage ML Pipeline Autoscaling via In-Context Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Multi-stage ML inference pipelines are difficult to autoscale due to heterogeneous resources, cross-stage coupling, and dynamic bottleneck migration. We present SAIR, an autoscaling framework that uses an LLM as an in-context reinforcement learning controller, improving its policy online from reward-labeled interaction histories without gradient updates. SAIR combines Pareto-dominance reward shaping with a provable separation margin, surprisal-guided experience retrieval for context efficiency, and fine-grained GPU rate control via user-space CUDA interception. We provide regret analysis decomposing error into retrieval coverage and LLM selection components. On four ML serving pipelines under three workload patterns, SAIR achieves the best or tied-best P99 latency and effective resource cost among deployed baselines, improving P99 by up to 50% and reducing effective cost by up to 97% (under GPU rate-control assumptions), with 86% bottleneck detection accuracy and no offline training.

摘要（中文）: 多阶段机器学习推理流水线由于异构资源、跨阶段耦合和动态瓶颈迁移而难以自动伸缩。我们提出了SAIR，一个使用LLM作为上下文强化学习控制器的自动伸缩框架，通过从奖励标记的交互历史记录中在线改进其策略，而无需梯度更新。SAIR结合了帕累托支配奖励塑造与可证明的分离裕度、用于上下文效率的惊奇度引导的经验检索，以及通过用户空间CUDA拦截实现的细粒度GPU速率控制。我们提供了遗憾分析，将误差分解为检索覆盖率和LLM选择两个组成部分。在三种工作负载模式下的四个ML服务流水线上，SAIR实现了已部署基线中最佳或并列最佳的P99延迟和有效资源成本，在P99延迟上提升高达50%，在有效成本上降低高达97%（在GPU速率控制假设下），并且具有86%的瓶颈检测准确率，无需离线训练。

TLDR: The paper introduces SAIR, an autoscaling framework using an LLM as an in-context reinforcement learning controller for multi-stage ML inference pipelines, demonstrating significant improvements in latency and resource cost without offline training.

Authors: Jianchang Su, Yifan Zhang, Shengkai Lin, Shizhen Zhao, Yusheng Zheng, Yiwei Yang, Wei Zhang

Failing to Explore: Language Models on Interactive Tasks

Abstract (English): We evaluate language models on their ability to explore interactive environments under a limited interaction budget. We introduce three parametric tasks with controllable exploration difficulty, spanning continuous and discrete environments. Across state-of-the-art models, we find systematic under-exploration and suboptimal solutions, with performance often significantly worse than simple explore--exploit heuristic baselines and scaling weakly as the budget increases. Finally, we study two lightweight interventions: splitting a fixed budget into parallel executions, which surprisingly improves performance despite a no-gain theoretical result for our tasks, and periodically summarizing the interaction history, which preserves key discoveries and further improves exploration.

摘要（中文）: 我们评估了语言模型在有限交互预算下探索交互式环境的能力。我们引入了三种参数化任务，其探索难度可控，涵盖连续和离散环境。在最先进的模型中，我们发现了系统性的探索不足和次优解，其性能通常明显低于简单的探索-利用启发式基线，并且随着预算的增加而扩展性较弱。最后，我们研究了两种轻量级干预手段：将固定预算拆分为并行执行，令人惊讶的是，尽管我们的任务在理论上没有收益，但它提高了性能；以及定期总结交互历史，这保留了关键发现并进一步改善了探索。

TLDR: This paper evaluates the exploration abilities of language models in interactive environments, finding they systematically under-explore and perform worse than simple heuristics. Simple interventions like parallel execution and periodic summarization improve exploration.

简要说明: 该论文评估了语言模型在交互式环境中探索的能力，发现它们系统性地探索不足，并且表现不如简单的启发式方法。 简单的干预措施，如并行执行和定期总结，可以提高探索能力。

Authors: Mahdi JafariRaviz, Keivan Rezaei, Arshia Soltani Moakhar, Zahra Sodagar, Yize Cheng, Soheil Feizi

RN-D: Discretized Categorical Actors with Regularized Networks for On-Policy Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): On-policy deep reinforcement learning remains a dominant paradigm for continuous control, yet standard implementations rely on Gaussian actors and relatively shallow MLP policies, often leading to brittle optimization when gradients are noisy and policy updates must be conservative. In this paper, we revisit policy representation as a first-class design choice for on-policy optimization. We study discretized categorical actors that represent each action dimension with a distribution over bins, yielding a policy objective that resembles a cross-entropy loss. Building on architectural advances from supervised learning, we further propose regularized actor networks, while keeping critic design fixed. Our results show that simply replacing the standard actor network with our discretized regularized actor yields consistent gains and achieve the state-of-the-art performance across diverse continuous-control benchmarks.

摘要（中文）: 在连续控制领域，同策略深度强化学习仍然是主流范式，然而，标准的实现依赖于高斯动作器和相对浅层的多层感知机策略，这通常会导致在梯度噪声较大且策略更新必须保守时出现脆弱的优化。在本文中，我们重新审视了策略表示，将其作为同策略优化的首要设计选择。我们研究了离散化的分类动作器，它使用关于区间的分布来表示每个动作维度，从而产生一个类似于交叉熵损失的策略目标。在监督学习的架构进步的基础上，我们进一步提出了正则化的动作器网络，同时保持了批评器设计的固定。我们的结果表明，简单地用我们离散化的正则化动作器替换标准动作器网络，就能在各种连续控制基准测试中获得一致的增益并达到最先进的性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel on-policy RL approach using discretized categorical actors with regularized networks, achieving state-of-the-art performance on continuous control benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种新颖的on-policy强化学习方法，该方法使用离散化的分类actor和正则化网络，在连续控制基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Yuexin Bian, Jie Feng, Tao Wang, Yijiang Li, Sicun Gao, Yuanyuan Shi

MOSAIC: Modular Scalable Autonomy for Intelligent Coordination of Heterogeneous Robotic Teams

Abstract (English): Mobile robots have become indispensable for exploring hostile environments, such as in space or disaster relief scenarios, but often remain limited to teleoperation by a human operator. This restricts the deployment scale and requires near-continuous low-latency communication between the operator and the robot. We present MOSAIC: a scalable autonomy framework for multi-robot scientific exploration using a unified mission abstraction based on Points of Interest (POIs) and multiple layers of autonomy, enabling supervision by a single operator. The framework dynamically allocates exploration and measurement tasks based on each robot's capabilities, leveraging team-level redundancy and specialization to enable continuous operation. We validated the framework in a space-analog field experiment emulating a lunar prospecting scenario, involving a heterogeneous team of five robots and a single operator. Despite the complete failure of one robot during the mission, the team completed 82.3% of assigned tasks at an Autonomy Ratio of 86%, while the operator workload remained at only 78.2%. These results demonstrate that the proposed framework enables robust, scalable multi-robot scientific exploration with limited operator intervention. We further derive practical lessons learned in robot interoperability, networking architecture, team composition, and operator workload management to inform future multi-robot exploration missions.

摘要（中文）: 移动机器人已成为探索恶劣环境（如太空或灾难救援场景）不可或缺的工具，但通常仍局限于人工遥控。这限制了部署规模，并且需要在操作员和机器人之间进行近乎连续的低延迟通信。我们提出了MOSAIC：一个可扩展的自主框架，用于基于兴趣点（POI）的统一任务抽象和多层自主性实现的多机器人科学探索，从而能够由单个操作员进行监督。该框架根据每个机器人的能力动态分配探索和测量任务，利用团队层面的冗余和专业化来实现连续运行。我们在一个模拟月球勘探场景的空间模拟外场实验中验证了该框架，实验包括一个由五个机器人和一名操作员组成的异构团队。尽管在任务期间一台机器人完全失效，但该团队仍以86%的自主率完成了82.3%的分配任务，同时操作员的工作量仅为78.2%。这些结果表明，所提出的框架能够以有限的操作员干预实现稳健、可扩展的多机器人科学探索。我们进一步得出在机器人互操作性、网络架构、团队组成和操作员工作量管理方面的实践经验教训，为未来的多机器人探索任务提供参考。

TLDR: The paper presents MOSAIC, a scalable autonomy framework for heterogeneous robot teams performing scientific exploration, demonstrated in a lunar prospecting analog with high autonomy and task completion rates despite robot failure.

Authors: David Oberacker, Julia Richer, Philip Arm, Marvin Grosse Besselmann, Lennart Puck, William Talbot, Maximilian Schik, Sabine Bellmann, Tristan Schnell, Hendrik Kolvenbach, Rüdiger Dillmann, Marco Hutter, Arne Roennau

Robust Rigid Body Assembly via Contact-Implicit Optimal Control with Exact Second-Order Derivatives

Abstract (English): Efficient planning of assembly motions is a long standing challenge in the field of robotics that has been primarily tackled with reinforcement learning and sampling-based methods by using extensive physics simulations. This paper proposes a sample-efficient robust optimal control approach for the determination of assembly motions, which requires significantly less physics simulation steps during planning through the efficient use of derivative information. To this end, a differentiable physics simulation is constructed that provides second-order analytic derivatives to the numerical solver and allows one to traverse seamlessly from informative derivatives to accurate contact simulation. The solution of the physics simulation problem is made differentiable by using smoothing inspired by interior-point methods applied to both the collision detection as well as the contact resolution problem. We propose a modified variant of an optimization-based formulation of collision detection formulated as a linear program and present an efficient implementation for the nominal evaluation and corresponding first- and second-order derivatives. Moreover, a multi-scenario-based trajectory optimization problem that ensures robustness with respect to sim-to-real mismatches is derived. The capability of the considered formulation is illustrated by results where over 99\% successful executions are achieved in real-world experiments. Thereby, we carefully investigate the effect of smooth approximations of the contact dynamics and robust modeling on the success rates. Furthermore, the method's capability is tested on different peg-in-hole problems in simulation to show the benefit of using exact Hessians over commonly used Hessian approximations.

摘要（中文）: 高效的装配运动规划一直是机器人领域一个长期存在的挑战，主要通过强化学习和基于采样的算法，并借助大量的物理仿真来解决。本文提出了一种采样高效的鲁棒最优控制方法，用于确定装配运动，该方法通过高效利用导数信息，在规划过程中显著减少了物理仿真步骤。为此，构建了一个可微的物理仿真器，它为数值求解器提供二阶解析导数，并允许从信息丰富的导数无缝过渡到精确的接触仿真。通过使用受内点法启发的平滑策略，将其应用于碰撞检测和接触求解问题，使物理仿真问题的求解过程可微。我们提出了一种改进的基于优化的碰撞检测公式，将其表示成线性规划问题，并展示了名义评估以及相应的一阶和二阶导数的有效实现。此外，还推导出了一个基于多场景的轨迹优化问题，以确保对sim-to-real差异的鲁棒性。所考虑的公式的能力通过真实世界实验中超过99%的成功执行率来验证。在此，我们仔细研究了接触动力学平滑近似和鲁棒建模对成功率的影响。此外，该方法的能力还在不同的孔轴配合问题仿真中进行了测试，以展示使用精确Hessian矩阵相对于常用的Hessian矩阵近似的优势。

TLDR: This paper introduces a sample-efficient, robust optimal control approach for robotic assembly, leveraging differentiable physics and exact second-order derivatives to achieve high success rates in real-world peg-in-hole experiments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于机器人装配的高效、鲁棒的最优控制方法，利用可微分物理和精确的二阶导数，在真实的插孔实验中实现了很高的成功率。

Authors: Christian Dietz, Sebastian Albrecht, Gianluca Frison, Moritz Diehl, Armin Nurkanović

Offline Reinforcement Learning of High-Quality Behaviors Under Robust Style Alignment

Abstract (English): We study offline reinforcement learning of style-conditioned policies using explicit style supervision via subtrajectory labeling functions. In this setting, aligning style with high task performance is particularly challenging due to distribution shift and inherent conflicts between style and reward. Existing methods, despite introducing numerous definitions of style, often fail to reconcile these objectives effectively. To address these challenges, we propose a unified definition of behavior style and instantiate it into a practical framework. Building on this, we introduce Style-Conditioned Implicit Q-Learning (SCIQL), which leverages offline goal-conditioned RL techniques, such as hindsight relabeling and value learning, and combine it with a new Gated Advantage Weighted Regression mechanism to efficiently optimize task performance while preserving style alignment. Experiments demonstrate that SCIQL achieves superior performance on both objectives compared to prior offline methods. Code, datasets and visuals are available in: https://sciql-iclr-2026.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了使用子轨迹标注函数进行显式风格监督的离线强化学习风格条件策略。在这种情况下，由于分布偏移以及风格和奖励之间的内在冲突，使风格与高任务性能对齐尤其具有挑战性。尽管现有方法引入了大量的风格定义，但往往无法有效地协调这些目标。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种统一的行为风格定义，并将其实例化为一个实用的框架。在此基础上，我们引入了风格条件隐式Q学习（SCIQL），它利用离线目标条件强化学习技术，例如后见之明重标记和价值学习，并将其与一种新的门控优势加权回归机制相结合，以在保持风格对齐的同时有效地优化任务性能。实验表明，与之前的离线方法相比，SCIQL在两个目标上都取得了更优越的性能。代码、数据集和可视化效果可在以下网址获得：https://sciql-iclr-2026.github.io/。

TLDR: This paper introduces Style-Conditioned Implicit Q-Learning (SCIQL) for offline reinforcement learning of style-conditioned policies, addressing the challenge of aligning style with task performance by combining goal-conditioned RL techniques with a gated advantage-weighted regression mechanism. Authors: Mathieu Petitbois, Rémy Portelas, Sylvain Lamprier

FlyAware: Inertia-Aware Aerial Manipulation via Vision-Based Estimation and Post-Grasp Adaptation

Abstract (English): Aerial manipulators (AMs) are gaining increasing attention in automated transportation and emergency services due to their superior dexterity compared to conventional multirotor drones. However, their practical deployment is challenged by the complexity of time-varying inertial parameters, which are highly sensitive to payload variations and manipulator configurations. Inspired by human strategies for interacting with unknown objects, this letter presents a novel onboard framework for robust aerial manipulation. The proposed system integrates a vision-based pre-grasp inertia estimation module with a post-grasp adaptation mechanism, enabling real-time estimation and adaptation of inertial dynamics. For control, we develop an inertia-aware adaptive control strategy based on gain scheduling, and assess its robustness via frequency-domain system identification. Our study provides new insights into post-grasp control for AMs, and real-world experiments validate the effectiveness and feasibility of the proposed framework.

摘要（中文）: 空中操作臂（AMs）因其相比传统多旋翼无人机的卓越灵活性，在自动化运输和应急服务领域正受到越来越多的关注。然而，其实际部署面临着时变惯性参数复杂性的挑战，这些参数对有效载荷变化和操作臂构型高度敏感。受人类与未知物体交互策略的启发，本文提出了一种用于稳健空中操作的新型机载框架。所提出的系统集成了基于视觉的预抓取惯性估计模块和抓取后自适应机制，实现了惯性动力学的实时估计和自适应调整。在控制方面，我们开发了一种基于增益调度的惯性感知自适应控制策略，并通过频域系统辨识评估其鲁棒性。我们的研究为空中操作臂的抓取后控制提供了新的见解，并且真实的实验验证了所提出框架的有效性和可行性。

Authors: Biyu Ye, Na Fan, Zhengping Fan, Weiliang Deng, Hongming Chen, Qifeng Chen, Ximin Lyu

Exo-Plore: Exploring Exoskeleton Control Space through Human-aligned Simulation

Abstract (English): Exoskeletons show great promise for enhancing mobility, but providing appropriate assistance remains challenging due to the complexity of human adaptation to external forces. Current state-of-the-art approaches for optimizing exoskeleton controllers require extensive human experiments in which participants must walk for hours, creating a paradox: those who could benefit most from exoskeleton assistance, such as individuals with mobility impairments, are rarely able to participate in such demanding procedures. We present Exo-plore, a simulation framework that combines neuromechanical simulation with deep reinforcement learning to optimize hip exoskeleton assistance without requiring real human experiments. Exo-plore can (1) generate realistic gait data that captures human adaptation to assistive forces, (2) produce reliable optimization results despite the stochastic nature of human gait, and (3) generalize to pathological gaits, showing strong linear relationships between pathology severity and optimal assistance.

摘要（中文）: 外骨骼在增强行动能力方面展现出巨大的潜力，但由于人体对外力的适应具有复杂性，提供适当的辅助仍然具有挑战性。目前最先进的外骨骼控制器优化方法需要大量的人体实验，参与者必须步行数小时，这造成了一个悖论：那些最能从外骨骼辅助中获益的人，例如行动障碍者，却很少能够参与到如此高要求的程序中。我们提出了Exo-plore，一个将神经-机械仿真与深度强化学习相结合的仿真框架，无需真实人体实验即可优化髋部外骨骼的辅助。Exo-plore能够（1）生成能够捕捉人体对辅助力适应的逼真步态数据，（2）在人体步态的随机性下产生可靠的优化结果，以及（3）推广到病态步态，显示出病理严重程度与最佳辅助之间的强线性关系。

TLDR: The paper introduces Exo-plore, a simulation framework using neuromechanical simulation and deep reinforcement learning to optimize hip exoskeleton assistance, reducing the need for extensive human experiments and enabling personalization for pathological gaits.

Authors: Geonho Leem, Jaedong Lee, Jehee Lee, Seungmoon Song, Jungdam Won

RoboStriker: Hierarchical Decision-Making for Autonomous Humanoid Boxing

Abstract (English): Achieving human-level competitive intelligence and physical agility in humanoid robots remains a major challenge, particularly in contact-rich and highly dynamic tasks such as boxing. While Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) offers a principled framework for strategic interaction, its direct application to humanoid control is hindered by high-dimensional contact dynamics and the absence of strong physical motion priors. We propose RoboStriker, a hierarchical three-stage framework that enables fully autonomous humanoid boxing by decoupling high-level strategic reasoning from low-level physical execution. The framework first learns a comprehensive repertoire of boxing skills by training a single-agent motion tracker on human motion capture data. These skills are subsequently distilled into a structured latent manifold, regularized by projecting the Gaussian-parameterized distribution onto a unit hypersphere. This topological constraint effectively confines exploration to the subspace of physically plausible motions. In the final stage, we introduce Latent-Space Neural Fictitious Self-Play (LS-NFSP), where competing agents learn competitive tactics by interacting within the latent action space rather than the raw motor space, significantly stabilizing multi-agent training. Experimental results demonstrate that RoboStriker achieves superior competitive performance in simulation and exhibits sim-to-real transfer. Our website is available at RoboStriker.

摘要（中文）: 在人形机器人中实现人类水平的竞争智能和身体敏捷性仍然是一项重大挑战，尤其是在诸如拳击等接触频繁且高度动态的任务中。虽然多智能体强化学习 (MARL) 为战略互动提供了一个有原则的框架，但由于高维接触动力学和缺乏强大的物理运动先验知识，它直接应用于人形机器人控制受到阻碍。我们提出了 RoboStriker，一个分层三阶段框架，通过将高层战略推理与低层物理执行分离，实现完全自主的人形拳击。该框架首先通过在人类运动捕捉数据上训练单智能体运动跟踪器来学习全面的拳击技能库。随后，这些技能被提炼成一个结构化的潜在流形，通过将高斯参数化分布投影到单位超球面上来对其进行正则化。这种拓扑约束有效地将探索限制在物理上合理的运动子空间内。在最后阶段，我们引入了 Latent-Space Neural Fictitious Self-Play (LS-NFSP)，其中竞争智能体通过在潜在动作空间而非原始电机空间内进行交互来学习竞争策略，从而显著稳定多智能体训练。实验结果表明，RoboStriker 在模拟中实现了卓越的竞争性能，并表现出从模拟到真实的迁移能力。我们的网站可在 RoboStriker 上访问。

TLDR: RoboStriker introduces a hierarchical RL framework for autonomous humanoid boxing, leveraging motion capture data and latent space learning to achieve stable multi-agent training and sim-to-real transfer.

简要说明: RoboStriker 提出了一个用于自主人形机器人拳击的分层强化学习框架，利用运动捕捉数据和潜在空间学习来实现稳定的多智能体训练和从仿真到现实的迁移。

Authors: Kangning Yin, Zhe Cao, Wentao Dong, Weishuai Zeng, Tianyi Zhang, Qiang Zhang, Jingbo Wang, Jiangmiao Pang, Ming Zhou, Weinan Zhang

High-Definition 5MP Stereo Vision Sensing for Robotics

Abstract (English): High-resolution (5MP+) stereo vision systems are essential for advancing robotic capabilities, enabling operation over longer ranges and generating significantly denser and accurate 3D point clouds. However, realizing the full potential of high-angular-resolution sensors requires a commensurately higher level of calibration accuracy and faster processing -- requirements often unmet by conventional methods. This study addresses that critical gap by processing 5MP camera imagery using a novel, advanced frame-to-frame calibration and stereo matching methodology designed to achieve both high accuracy and speed. Furthermore, we introduce a new approach to evaluate real-time performance by comparing real-time disparity maps with ground-truth disparity maps derived from more computationally intensive stereo matching algorithms. Crucially, the research demonstrates that high-pixel-count cameras yield high-quality point clouds only through the implementation of high-accuracy calibration.

摘要（中文）: 高分辨率（5MP+）立体视觉系统对于提升机器人性能至关重要，能够实现更远距离的操作并生成密度更高、精度更高的3D点云。 然而，要充分发挥高角分辨率传感器的潜力，必须达到相应更高的校准精度和更快的处理速度——而传统方法通常无法满足这些要求。 本研究通过采用一种新颖的、先进的逐帧校准和立体匹配方法处理5MP相机图像，旨在实现高精度和高速度，从而弥补了这一关键差距。 此外，我们引入了一种新方法来评估实时性能，通过将实时视差图与从计算密集型立体匹配算法获得的真实视差图进行比较。 关键在于，该研究表明，只有通过实施高精度校准，高像素相机才能产生高质量的点云。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel calibration and stereo matching method for high-resolution (5MP) stereo vision systems, demonstrating that high-accuracy calibration is crucial for generating high-quality 3D point clouds from high-pixel-count cameras and proposes a way to evaluate real-time performance.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于高分辨率 (5MP) 立体视觉系统的新型校准和立体匹配方法，证明了高精度校准对于从高像素相机生成高质量 3D 点云至关重要，并提出了一种评估实时性能的方法。

mjlab: A Lightweight Framework for GPU-Accelerated Robot Learning

Abstract (English): We present mjlab, a lightweight, open-source framework for robot learning that combines GPU-accelerated simulation with composable environments and minimal setup friction. mjlab adopts the manager-based API introduced by Isaac Lab, where users compose modular building blocks for observations, rewards, and events, and pairs it with MuJoCo Warp for GPU-accelerated physics. The result is a framework installable with a single command, requiring minimal dependencies, and providing direct access to native MuJoCo data structures. mjlab ships with reference implementations of velocity tracking, motion imitation, and manipulation tasks.

TLDR: mjlab is a lightweight, open-source robot learning framework leveraging GPU-accelerated MuJoCo through a modular, manager-based API, designed for easy installation and use.

Authors: Kevin Zakka, Qiayuan Liao, Brent Yi, Louis Le Lay, Koushil Sreenath, Pieter Abbeel

Automatic Constraint Policy Optimization based on Continuous Constraint Interpolation Framework for Offline Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Offline Reinforcement Learning (RL) relies on policy constraints to mitigate extrapolation error, where both the constraint form and constraint strength critically shape performance. However, most existing methods commit to a single constraint family: weighted behavior cloning, density regularization, or support constraints, without a unified principle that explains their connections or trade-offs. In this work, we propose Continuous Constraint Interpolation (CCI), a unified optimization framework in which these three constraint families arise as special cases along a common constraint spectrum. The CCI framework introduces a single interpolation parameter that enables smooth transitions and principled combinations across constraint types. Building on CCI, we develop Automatic Constraint Policy Optimization (ACPO), a practical primal--dual algorithm that adapts the interpolation parameter via a Lagrangian dual update. Moreover, we establish a maximum-entropy performance difference lemma and derive performance lower bounds for both the closed-form optimal policy and its parametric projection. Experiments on D4RL and NeoRL2 demonstrate robust gains across diverse domains, achieving state-of-the-art performance overall.

摘要（中文）: 离线强化学习（RL）依赖于策略约束来缓解外推误差，其中约束的形式和约束强度对性能起着至关重要的作用。然而，大多数现有方法都致力于单一的约束族：加权行为克隆、密度正则化或支撑约束，而缺乏一个统一的原则来解释它们之间的联系或权衡。在这项工作中，我们提出了连续约束插值（CCI），一个统一的优化框架，其中这三个约束族都作为通用约束谱上的特例出现。CCI框架引入了一个单一的插值参数，该参数能够实现跨约束类型的平滑过渡和原则性组合。基于CCI，我们开发了自动约束策略优化（ACPO），一种实用的原始-对偶算法，通过拉格朗日对偶更新来调整插值参数。此外，我们建立了最大熵性能差异引理，并推导了闭式最优策略及其参数化投影的性能下界。在D4RL和NeoRL2上的实验表明，在不同领域都取得了稳健的提升，实现了总体上的最先进性能。

TLDR: This paper proposes a unified framework, Continuous Constraint Interpolation (CCI), for offline reinforcement learning constraints, allowing for smooth transitions between different constraint types and demonstrating state-of-the-art performance using Automatic Constraint Policy Optimization (ACPO).

简要说明: 本文提出了一个统一的离线强化学习约束框架，即连续约束插值（CCI），允许在不同约束类型之间平滑过渡，并使用自动约束策略优化（ACPO）展示了最先进的性能。

Authors: Xinchen Han, Qiuyang Fang, Hossam Afifi, Michel Marot

TriCEGAR: A Trace-Driven Abstraction Mechanism for Agentic AI

Abstract (English): Agentic AI systems act through tools and evolve their behavior over long, stochastic interaction traces. This setting complicates assurance, because behavior depends on nondeterministic environments and probabilistic model outputs. Prior work introduced runtime verification for agentic AI via Dynamic Probabilistic Assurance (DPA), learning an MDP online and model checking quantitative properties. A key limitation is that developers must manually define the state abstraction, which couples verification to application-specific heuristics and increases adoption friction. This paper proposes TriCEGAR, a trace-driven abstraction mechanism that automates state construction from execution logs and supports online construction of an agent behavioral MDP. TriCEGAR represents abstractions as predicate trees learned from traces and refined using counterexamples. We describe a framework-native implementation that (i) captures typed agent lifecycle events, (ii) builds abstractions from traces, (iii) constructs an MDP, and (iv) performs probabilistic model checking to compute bounds such as Pmax(success) and Pmin(failure). We also show how run likelihoods enable anomaly detection as a guardrailing signal.

摘要（中文）: 智能体人工智能系统通过工具行动，并在漫长的、随机的交互轨迹中演化其行为。这种设定使得保障变得复杂，因为行为依赖于非确定性的环境和概率模型输出。 之前的研究引入了通过动态概率保障(DPA)对智能体人工智能进行运行时验证的方法，该方法在线学习一个MDP并进行定量属性的模型检查。一个关键限制是，开发者必须手动定义状态抽象，这使得验证与特定于应用的启发式方法相耦合，并增加了采用摩擦。 本文提出了一种由轨迹驱动的抽象机制TriCEGAR，该机制自动化了从执行日志中构建状态的过程，并支持在线构建智能体行为MDP。 TriCEGAR将抽象表示为从轨迹中学习并使用反例细化的谓词树。 我们描述了一个框架原生实现，它(i)捕获类型化的智能体生命周期事件，(ii)从轨迹构建抽象，(iii)构建一个MDP，以及(iv)执行概率模型检查以计算诸如Pmax(成功)和Pmin(失败)之类的界限。我们还展示了运行似然性如何实现异常检测作为一种防护信号。

TLDR: The paper introduces TriCEGAR, a trace-driven abstraction mechanism to automate state construction for runtime verification in agentic AI systems, enabling probabilistic model checking and anomaly detection.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TriCEGAR，一种基于跟踪的抽象机制，用于自动构建智能体AI系统中运行时验证的状态，从而实现概率模型检测和异常检测。

Authors: Roham Koohestani, Ateş Görpelioğlu, Egor Klimov, Burcu Kulahcioglu Ozkan, Maliheh Izadi

Why Your Deep Research Agent Fails? On Hallucination Evaluation in Full Research Trajectory

Abstract (English): Diagnosing the failure mechanisms of Deep Research Agents (DRAs) remains a critical challenge. Existing benchmarks predominantly rely on end-to-end evaluation, obscuring critical intermediate hallucinations, such as flawed planning, that accumulate throughout the research trajectory. To bridge this gap, we propose a shift from outcome-based to process-aware evaluation by auditing the full research trajectory. We introduce the PIES Taxonomy to categorize hallucinations along functional components (Planning vs. Summarization) and error properties (Explicit vs. Implicit). We instantiate this taxonomy into a fine-grained evaluation framework that decomposes the trajectory to rigorously quantify these hallucinations. Leveraging this framework to isolate 100 distinctively hallucination-prone tasks including adversarial scenarios, we curate DeepHalluBench. Experiments on six state-of-theart DRAs reveal that no system achieves robust reliability. Furthermore, our diagnostic analysis traces the etiology of these failures to systemic deficits, specifically hallucination propagation and cognitive biases, providing foundational insights to guide future architectural optimization. Data and code are available at https://github.com/yuhao-zhan/DeepHalluBench.

摘要（中文）: 诊断深度研究代理（DRAs）的失效机制仍然是一项关键挑战。现有的基准测试主要依赖于端到端评估，掩盖了贯穿整个研究轨迹的严重中间幻觉，例如有缺陷的规划。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出从基于结果的评估转变为过程感知的评估，通过审计完整的研究轨迹来实现。我们引入了PIES分类法，以根据功能组件（规划 vs. 总结）和错误属性（显式 vs. 隐式）对幻觉进行分类。 我们将此分类法实例化为一个细粒度的评估框架，该框架分解研究轨迹以严格量化这些幻觉。利用此框架来隔离100项独特的易于产生幻觉的任务，包括对抗性场景，我们策划了DeepHalluBench。在六种最先进的DRAs上的实验表明，没有一个系统能够实现稳健的可靠性。此外，我们的诊断分析将这些失败的病因追溯到系统性缺陷，特别是幻觉传播和认知偏差，从而提供了指导未来架构优化的基础性见解。数据和代码可在https://github.com/yuhao-zhan/DeepHalluBench获得。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new benchmark, DeepHalluBench, and a taxonomy (PIES) for evaluating hallucinations in Deep Research Agents (DRAs) by auditing their full research trajectory, revealing significant reliability issues and failure patterns in state-of-the-art DRAs.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个新的基准测试DeepHalluBench和一个分类法(PIES)，通过审计深度研究Agent（DRA）的完整研究轨迹来评估其幻觉，揭示了现有DRA在可靠性方面的重要问题和失败模式。

Authors: Yuhao Zhan, Tianyu Fan, Linxuan Huang, Zirui Guo, Chao Huang

Stabilizing the Q-Gradient Field for Policy Smoothness in Actor-Critic

Abstract (English): Policies learned via continuous actor-critic methods often exhibit erratic, high-frequency oscillations, making them unsuitable for physical deployment. Current approaches attempt to enforce smoothness by directly regularizing the policy's output. We argue that this approach treats the symptom rather than the cause. In this work, we theoretically establish that policy non-smoothness is fundamentally governed by the differential geometry of the critic. By applying implicit differentiation to the actor-critic objective, we prove that the sensitivity of the optimal policy is bounded by the ratio of the Q-function's mixed-partial derivative (noise sensitivity) to its action-space curvature (signal distinctness). To empirically validate this theoretical insight, we introduce PAVE (Policy-Aware Value-field Equalization), a critic-centric regularization framework that treats the critic as a scalar field and stabilizes its induced action-gradient field. PAVE rectifies the learning signal by minimizing the Q-gradient volatility while preserving local curvature. Experimental results demonstrate that PAVE achieves smoothness and robustness comparable to policy-side smoothness regularization methods, while maintaining competitive task performance, without modifying the actor.

摘要（中文）: 通过连续行动者-评论家方法学习到的策略通常表现出不稳定、高频振荡，使其不适用于物理部署。目前的做法试图通过直接正则化策略的输出来强制平滑。我们认为这种方法治标不治本。在这项工作中，我们从理论上证明策略的非平滑性从根本上由评论家的微分几何性质决定。通过对行动者-评论家目标函数应用隐式微分，我们证明了最优策略的敏感度受Q函数的混合偏导数（噪声敏感度）与其动作空间曲率（信号区分度）之比的约束。为了通过实验验证这一理论见解，我们引入了PAVE（策略感知值域均衡），这是一个以评论家为中心的正则化框架，它将评论家视为标量场，并稳定其诱导的动作梯度场。PAVE通过最小化Q梯度的波动性同时保持局部曲率来纠正学习信号。实验结果表明，PAVE实现了与策略侧平滑正则化方法相当的平滑性和鲁棒性，同时保持了具有竞争力的任务性能，而无需修改行动者。

TLDR: This paper addresses the problem of policy oscillations in actor-critic methods by theoretically analyzing the Q-gradient field and introducing a critic-centric regularization framework (PAVE) to stabilize it, achieving smooth policies without actor modifications.

简要说明: 本文通过理论分析Q梯度场，并引入一种以评论家为中心的正则化框架(PAVE)来稳定它，从而解决actor-critic方法中策略振荡的问题，在不修改actor的情况下实现平滑的策略。

Authors: Jeong Woon Lee, Kyoleen Kwak, Daeho Kim, Hyoseok Hwang

DiffuSpeech: Silent Thought, Spoken Answer via Unified Speech-Text Diffusion

Abstract (English): Current speech language models generate responses directly without explicit reasoning, leading to errors that cannot be corrected once audio is produced. We introduce \textbf{``Silent Thought, Spoken Answer''} -- a paradigm where speech LLMs generate internal text reasoning alongside spoken responses, with thinking traces informing speech quality. To realize this, we present \method{}, the first diffusion-based speech-text language model supporting both understanding and generation, unifying discrete text and tokenized speech under a single masked diffusion framework. Unlike autoregressive approaches, \method{} jointly generates reasoning traces and speech tokens through iterative denoising, with modality-specific masking schedules. We also construct \dataset{}, the first speech QA dataset with paired text reasoning traces, containing 26K samples totaling 319 hours. Experiments show \method{} achieves state-of-the-art speech-to-speech QA accuracy, outperforming the best baseline by up to 9 points, while attaining the best TTS quality among generative models (6.2\% WER) and preserving language understanding (66.2\% MMLU). Ablations confirm that both the diffusion architecture and thinking traces contribute to these gains.

摘要（中文）: 当前语音语言模型直接生成回复，缺乏显式推理，导致一旦生成音频就无法纠正错误。我们引入了一个称为“**静默思考，语音回答**”的范式，其中语音LLM在生成语音回复的同时生成内部文本推理，思考轨迹能够提升语音质量。为了实现这一点，我们提出了\method{}，这是第一个基于扩散的语音-文本语言模型，支持理解和生成，在单个掩码扩散框架下统一了离散文本和令牌化语音。与自回归方法不同，\method{}通过迭代去噪联合生成推理轨迹和语音令牌，并采用特定于模态的掩码策略。我们还构建了\dataset{}，这是第一个带有配对文本推理轨迹的语音问答数据集，包含2.6万个样本，总计319小时。实验表明，\method{}实现了最先进的语音到语音问答准确率，优于最佳基线高达9个百分点，同时在生成模型中达到了最佳的TTS质量（6.2%的WER），并保持了语言理解能力（66.2%的MMLU）。消融实验证实，扩散架构和思考轨迹都对这些提升有所贡献。

Procedural Knowledge Extraction from Industrial Troubleshooting Guides Using Vision Language Models

Abstract (English): Industrial troubleshooting guides encode diagnostic procedures in flowchart-like diagrams where spatial layout and technical language jointly convey meaning. To integrate this knowledge into operator support systems, which assist shop-floor personnel in diagnosing and resolving equipment issues, the information must first be extracted and structured for machine interpretation. However, when performed manually, this extraction is labor-intensive and error-prone. Vision Language Models offer potential to automate this process by jointly interpreting visual and textual meaning, yet their performance on such guides remains underexplored. This paper evaluates two VLMs on extracting structured knowledge, comparing two prompting strategies: standard instruction-guided versus an augmented approach that cues troubleshooting layout patterns. Results reveal model-specific trade-offs between layout sensitivity and semantic robustness, informing practical deployment decisions.

摘要（中文）: 工业故障排除指南将诊断程序编码成类似于流程图的图表，其中空间布局和技术语言共同传达意义。为了将这些知识集成到操作员支持系统中（该系统旨在协助车间人员诊断和解决设备问题），必须首先提取信息并将其结构化，以便机器能够理解。然而，如果手动执行，此提取过程既费力又容易出错。视觉语言模型有望通过共同解释视觉和文本含义来自动化此过程，但它们在这些指南上的性能仍有待探索。本文评估了两个视觉语言模型在提取结构化知识方面的表现，并比较了两种提示策略：标准的指令引导方法与提示故障排除布局模式的增强方法。结果揭示了模型之间在布局敏感性和语义稳健性方面的特定权衡，为实际部署决策提供了依据。

Authors: Guillermo Gil de Avalle, Laura Maruster, Christos Emmanouilidis

MC-GRPO: Median-Centered Group Relative Policy Optimization for Small-Rollout Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Group-relative policy optimization methods train language models by generating multiple rollouts per prompt and normalizing rewards with a shared mean reward baseline. In resource-constrained settings where the rollout budget is small, accuracy often degrades. We find that noise in the shared baseline induces advantage sign flips, where some rollouts receive an incorrect advantage sign, and the update direction is reversed. To address this, we propose Median-Centered Group Relative Policy Optimization (MC-GRPO), a simple and effective solution for small-rollout training. Our main idea is to replace the mean baseline with a median baseline: the median is far less sensitive to outlier rewards than the mean, mitigating the sign flips under small rollout size (G). We generate one additional rollout for median reference (G+1), and compute advantages by using the group median. With an odd-sized group, exactly one completion is the median and receives zero advantage, we exclude this pivot rollout from backpropagation so the number of gradient-contributing samples per prompt remains G, preserving the core update cost of standard G-rollout training. Across various GRPO-family methods and a wide range of models and scales, this median-centered training consistently improves stability and final accuracy in the low-rollout regime, reducing the gap between G=2 and G=8 to within 1%. Code is available at https://github.com/lotusroot-kim/MC-GRPO

摘要（中文）: 基于群体相对策略优化的方法通过为每个提示生成多个轨迹，并使用共享的均值奖励基线对奖励进行归一化来训练语言模型。在资源受限、轨迹预算较小的环境中，准确率通常会下降。我们发现共享基线中的噪声会引起优势符号翻转，其中一些轨迹会获得错误的优势符号，导致更新方向反转。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了中值中心群体相对策略优化(MC-GRPO)，这是一种简单有效的适用于小轨迹训练的解决方案。我们的主要思想是用中值基线取代均值基线：与均值相比，中值对异常值奖励的敏感度远低于均值，从而减轻了小轨迹大小(G)下的符号翻转。我们额外生成一个轨迹用于中值参考(G+1)，并通过使用群体中值来计算优势。由于奇数大小的群体中恰好有一个生成结果是中值并获得零优势，我们将从反向传播中排除这个中心轨迹，因此每个提示的梯度贡献样本数量仍然为G，从而保留了标准G轨迹训练的核心更新成本。 在各种GRPO系列方法以及各种模型和规模上，这种以中值为中心的训练始终如一地提高了低轨迹情况下的稳定性和最终准确率，将G=2和G=8之间的差距缩小到1%以内。代码可在 https://github.com/lotusroot-kim/MC-GRPO 获取。

TLDR: This paper introduces Median-Centered Group Relative Policy Optimization (MC-GRPO), which replaces the mean reward baseline with a median baseline in group-relative policy optimization methods to improve training stability and accuracy in small-rollout reinforcement learning settings.

简要说明: 本文介绍了中心化中位数群组相对策略优化（MC-GRPO），该方法在群组相对策略优化方法中使用中位数基线替代均值奖励基线，从而提高小样本强化学习设置中的训练稳定性和准确性。

Authors: Youngeun Kim

Demystifying Design Choices of Reinforcement Fine-tuning: A Batched Contextual Bandit Learning Perspective

Abstract (English): The reinforcement fine-tuning area is undergoing an explosion papers largely on optimizing design choices. Though performance gains are often claimed, inconsistent conclusions also arise from time to time, making the progress illusive. Reflecting on this illusion, we still lack principled answers to two fundamental questions: 1) what is the role of each design choice? 2) which ones are critical? This paper aims to shed light on them. The underlying challenge is that design choices are entangled together, making their contribution to learning and generalization difficult to attribute. To address this challenge, we first construct a minimalist baseline for disentangling factors: one rollout per query in each round, the outcome reward serving as the training signal without any advantage trick, and a batch size of thirty-two. This baseline connects to batched contextual bandit learning, which facilitates experimental analysis. Centering around this baseline, we design an experiment pipeline, examining the marginal gains of factors like advantage, number of rollouts, etc. Experiments on three base models and two datasets, not only reveal new understanding on the role of various design choices on learning and generalization dynamics, but also identify critical ones that deserve more effort.

摘要（中文）: 强化精调领域正经历着论文数量的爆发式增长，其中大部分关注优化设计选择。尽管经常声称有性能提升，但有时也会出现不一致的结论，使得进展显得虚幻。反思这种幻觉，我们仍然缺乏对两个基本问题的有原则的回答：1) 每种设计选择的作用是什么？2) 哪些是关键的？本文旨在阐明这些问题。根本挑战在于设计选择相互纠缠在一起，使得它们对学习和泛化的贡献难以归因。为了应对这一挑战，我们首先构建了一个极简基线来解耦因素：每轮查询一次 rollout，结果奖励作为训练信号，不使用任何优势技巧，批大小为三十二。这个基线与批量上下文赌博机学习相关联，这有助于实验分析。围绕这个基线，我们设计了一个实验流程，考察了诸如优势函数、rollout 数量等因素的边际收益。在三种基础模型和两个数据集上的实验，不仅揭示了对各种设计选择在学习和泛化动态中的作用的新理解，而且还识别出了值得付出更多努力的关键因素。

TLDR: This paper investigates the impact of various design choices in reinforcement fine-tuning by framing the problem as batched contextual bandit learning, aiming to identify critical factors for improved learning and generalization.

简要说明: 本文通过将强化微调问题框架化为批量上下文bandit学习，研究了其中各种设计选择的影响，旨在识别对于改进学习和泛化能力的关键因素。

Authors: Hong Xie, Xiao Hu, Tao Tan, Haoran Gu, Xin Li, Jianyu Han, Defu Lian, Enhong Chen

Enhancing TableQA through Verifiable Reasoning Trace Reward

Abstract (English): A major challenge in training TableQA agents, compared to standard text- and image-based agents, is that answers cannot be inferred from a static input but must be reasoned through stepwise transformations of the table state, introducing multi-step reasoning complexity and environmental interaction. This leads to a research question: Can explicit feedback on table transformation action improve model reasoning capability? In this work, we introduce RE-Tab, a plug-and-play framework that architecturally enhances trajectory search via lightweight, training-free reward modeling by formulating the problem as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process. We demonstrate that providing explicit verifiable rewards during State Transition (``What is the best action?'') and Simulative Reasoning (``Am I sure about the output?'') is crucial to steer the agent's navigation in table states. By enforcing stepwise reasoning with reward feedback in table transformations, RE-Tab achieves state-of-the-art performance in TableQA with almost 25\% drop in inference cost. Furthermore, a direct plug-and-play implementation of RE-Tab brings up to 41.77% improvement in QA accuracy and 33.33% drop in test-time inference samples for consistent answer. Consistent improvement pattern across various LLMs and state-of-the-art benchmarks further confirms RE-Tab's generalisability. The repository is available at https://github.com/ThomasK1018/RE_Tab .

摘要（中文）: 与标准的基于文本和图像的智能体相比，训练表格问答 (TableQA) 智能体的一个主要挑战在于，答案不能从静态输入中推断出来，而必须通过表格状态的逐步转换进行推理，从而引入了多步推理复杂性和环境交互。这就引出了一个研究问题：关于表格转换动作的显式反馈能否提高模型的推理能力？在这项工作中，我们引入了 RE-Tab，这是一个即插即用的框架，通过将问题形式化为一个部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程，利用轻量级的、无需训练的奖励建模，在架构上增强了轨迹搜索。我们证明，在状态转移（“什么是最佳动作？”）和模拟推理（“我确定输出结果吗？”）期间提供可验证的显式奖励对于引导智能体在表格状态中导航至关重要。通过在表格转换中利用奖励反馈强制执行逐步推理，RE-Tab 在 TableQA 中实现了最先进的性能，同时推理成本降低了近 25%。此外，直接即插即用的 RE-Tab 实现可在 QA 准确率方面提高高达 41.77%，并在测试时推理样本方面减少 33.33%，以获得一致的答案。RE-Tab 在各种大型语言模型 (LLM) 和最先进的基准测试中表现出一致的改进模式，进一步证实了其通用性。代码仓库位于 https://github.com/ThomasK1018/RE_Tab 。

TLDR: The paper introduces RE-Tab, a training-free framework that uses explicit, verifiable rewards during table transformation to improve TableQA agent reasoning, achieving state-of-the-art performance with reduced inference costs and plug-and-play improvements across various LLMs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为RE-Tab的免训练框架，它通过在表格转换过程中使用显式的、可验证的奖励来提高 TableQA 代理的推理能力，在降低推理成本的同时，实现了最先进的性能，并且可以在各种大型语言模型中即插即用。

Authors: Tung Sum Thomas Kwok, Xinyu Wang, Hengzhi He, Xiaofeng Lin, Peng Lu, Liheng Ma, Chunhe Wang, Ying Nian Wu, Lei Ding, Guang Cheng

Action-Sufficient Goal Representations

Abstract (English): Hierarchical policies in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) addresses long-horizon tasks by decomposing control into high-level subgoal planning and low-level action execution. A critical design choice in such architectures is the goal representation-the compressed encoding of goals that serves as the interface between these levels. Existing approaches commonly derive goal representations while learning value functions, implicitly assuming that preserving information sufficient for value estimation is adequate for optimal control. We show that this assumption can fail, even when the value estimation is exact, as such representations may collapse goal states that need to be differentiated for action learning. To address this, we introduce an information-theoretic framework that defines action sufficiency, a condition on goal representations necessary for optimal action selection. We prove that value sufficiency does not imply action sufficiency and empirically verify that the latter is more strongly associated with control success in a discrete environment. We further demonstrate that standard log-loss training of low-level policies naturally induces action-sufficient representations. Our experimental results a popular benchmark demonstrate that our actor-derived representations consistently outperform representations learned via value estimation.

摘要（中文）: 离线目标条件强化学习（GCRL）中的分层策略通过将控制分解为高层子目标规划和低层动作执行来处理长程任务。这种架构中的一个关键设计选择是目标表征——目标的压缩编码，它作为这些层之间的接口。现有的方法通常在学习价值函数的同时推导出目标表征，隐式地假设保留足以进行价值估计的信息足以实现最优控制。我们表明，即使在价值估计精确的情况下，这种假设也可能失效，因为这种表征可能会坍缩需要区分以进行动作学习的目标状态。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一个信息论框架，该框架定义了动作充分性，这是目标表征对最优动作选择的必要条件。我们证明价值充分性并不意味着动作充分性，并且通过实验验证后者与离散环境中的控制成功更密切相关。我们进一步证明，低层策略的标准对数损失训练自然会诱导动作充分的表征。我们在一个流行的基准测试上的实验结果表明，我们基于Actor推导的表征始终优于通过价值估计学习的表征。

TLDR: This paper introduces an information-theoretic framework for learning action-sufficient goal representations in hierarchical offline GCRL, showing that value-sufficient representations are not always action-sufficient and that actor-derived representations perform better.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个信息论框架，用于在分层离线GCRL中学习行动充分的目标表示，表明价值充分的表示并不总是行动充分的，并且actor导出的表示效果更好。

Authors: Jinu Hyeon, Woobin Park, Hongjoon Ahn, Taesup Moon

Controllable Information Production

Abstract (English): Intrinsic Motivation (IM) is a paradigm for generating intelligent behavior without external utilities. The existing information-theoretic methods for IM are predominantly based on information transmission, which explicitly depends on the designer's choice of which random variables engage in transmission. In this work, we introduce a novel IM principle, Controllable Information Production (CIP), that avoids both external utilities and designer-specified variables. We derive the CIP objective from Optimal Control, showing a connection between extrinsic and intrinsic behaviors. CIP appears as the gap between open-loop and closed-loop Kolmogorov-Sinai entropies, which simultaneously rewards the pursuit and regulation of chaos. We establish key theoretical properties of CIP and demonstrate its effectiveness on standard IM benchmarks.

摘要（中文）: 内在动机 (IM) 是一种无需外部效用函数即可生成智能行为的范式。现有的基于信息论的内在动机方法主要基于信息传递，这明确地依赖于设计者选择哪些随机变量参与传递。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种新的内在动机原则，即可控信息产生 (CIP)，它避免了外部效用函数和设计者指定的变量。我们从最优控制中推导出 CIP 目标，展示了外在行为和内在行为之间的联系。CIP 表现为开环 Kolmogorov-Sinai 熵和闭环 Kolmogorov-Sinai 熵之间的差距，这同时奖励了对混沌的追求和调控。我们确立了 CIP 的关键理论性质，并在标准的 IM 基准测试上证明了其有效性。

TLDR: This paper introduces Controllable Information Production (CIP), a novel intrinsic motivation principle derived from optimal control that rewards both the pursuit and regulation of chaos, demonstrating its effectiveness on standard benchmarks without relying on external utilities or designer-specified variables.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为可控信息产生(CIP)的新型内在动机原则，该原则源于最优控制，奖励对混沌的追求和调节，并在标准基准上展示了其有效性，而无需依赖外部效用或设计者指定的变量。

Authors: Tristan Shah, Stas Tiomkin

Learning Policy Representations for Steerable Behavior Synthesis

Abstract (English): Given a Markov decision process (MDP), we seek to learn representations for a range of policies to facilitate behavior steering at test time. As policies of an MDP are uniquely determined by their occupancy measures, we propose modeling policy representations as expectations of state-action feature maps with respect to occupancy measures. We show that these representations can be approximated uniformly for a range of policies using a set-based architecture. Our model encodes a set of state-action samples into a latent embedding, from which we decode both the policy and its value functions corresponding to multiple rewards. We use variational generative approach to induce a smooth latent space, and further shape it with contrastive learning so that latent distances align with differences in value functions. This geometry permits gradient-based optimization directly in the latent space. Leveraging this capability, we solve a novel behavior synthesis task, where policies are steered to satisfy previously unseen value function constraints without additional training.

摘要（中文）: 给定一个马尔可夫决策过程 (MDP)，我们力求学习一系列策略的表示，以便于在测试时进行行为引导。由于 MDP 的策略由其占用测度唯一确定，我们提出将策略表示建模为状态-动作特征图关于占用测度的期望。我们表明，可以使用基于集合的架构对一系列策略统一近似这些表示。 我们的模型将一组状态-动作样本编码到潜在嵌入中，从中解码对应于多个奖励的策略及其价值函数。 我们使用变分生成方法来诱导一个平滑的潜在空间，并进一步通过对比学习来塑造它，使得潜在距离与价值函数的差异对齐。 这种几何性质允许直接在潜在空间中进行基于梯度的优化。 利用这种能力，我们解决了一个新的行为合成任务，其中策略被引导以满足先前未见的价值函数约束，而无需额外的训练。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method for learning policy representations in MDPs that allows for steering behavior at test time by optimizing in a latent space conditioned on value function constraints, enabling behavior synthesis without retraining.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种在MDP中学习策略表达的方法，该方法允许通过在潜在空间中基于价值函数约束进行优化来在测试时控制行为，从而无需重新训练即可实现行为合成。

Authors: Beiming Li, Sergio Rozada, Alejandro Ribeiro

StepShield: When, Not Whether to Intervene on Rogue Agents

Abstract (English): Existing agent safety benchmarks report binary accuracy, conflating early intervention with post-mortem analysis. A detector that flags a violation at step 8 enables intervention; one that reports it at step 48 provides only forensic value. This distinction is critical, yet current benchmarks cannot measure it. We introduce StepShield, the first benchmark to evaluate when violations are detected, not just whether. StepShield contains 9,213 code agent trajectories, including 1,278 meticulously annotated training pairs and a 7,935-trajectory test set with a realistic 8.1% rogue rate. Rogue behaviors are grounded in real-world security incidents across six categories. We propose three novel temporal metrics: Early Intervention Rate (EIR), Intervention Gap, and Tokens Saved. Surprisingly, our evaluation reveals that an LLM-based judge achieves 59% EIR while a static analyzer achieves only 26%, a 2.3x performance gap that is entirely invisible to standard accuracy metrics. We further show that early detection has direct economic benefits: our cascaded HybridGuard detector reduces monitoring costs by 75% and projects to $108M in cumulative savings over five years at enterprise scale. By shifting the focus of evaluation from whether to when, StepShield provides a new foundation for building safer and more economically viable AI agents. The code and data are released under an Apache 2.0 license.

摘要（中文）: 现有智能体安全基准测试报告二元准确率，混淆了早期干预和事后分析。一个在第8步标记违规行为的检测器能够实现干预；而一个在第48步报告违规行为的检测器仅提供取证价值。这种区别至关重要，但当前的基准测试无法衡量它。我们引入了StepShield，这是第一个评估违规行为何时被检测到的基准测试，而不仅仅是是否检测到。StepShield包含9,213个代码智能体轨迹，其中包括1,278个精心标注的训练对和一个包含7,935个轨迹的测试集，其真实违规率（rogue rate）为8.1%。违规行为基于真实世界的安全事件，涵盖六个类别。我们提出了三个新的时间指标：早期干预率（EIR）、干预差距和节省的Token数量。令人惊讶的是，我们的评估表明，基于LLM的judge实现了59%的EIR，而静态分析器仅实现了26%，这种2.3倍的性能差距在标准的准确率指标中完全不可见。我们进一步表明，早期检测具有直接的经济效益：我们级联的HybridGuard检测器将监控成本降低了75%，并预计在五年内为企业规模节省累计1.08亿美元。通过将评估的重点从“是否”转移到“何时”，StepShield为构建更安全、更经济可行的AI智能体提供了新的基础。代码和数据以Apache 2.0许可证发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces StepShield, a new benchmark for evaluating the temporal aspect of agent safety violations, focusing on *when* violations are detected rather than merely *whether* they occur, and demonstrates its value with an LLM-based judge and a HybridGuard detector.

简要说明: 本文介绍了StepShield，一个用于评估代理安全违规行为时序方面的新基准，重点关注违规行为*何时*被检测到，而不仅仅是*是否*发生违规行为，并通过基于LLM的判断器和HybridGuard检测器展示了其价值。

Authors: Gloria Felicia, Michael Eniolade, Jinfeng He, Zitha Sasindran, Hemant Kumar, Milan Hussain Angati, Sandeep Bandarupalli

Q-Hawkeye: Reliable Visual Policy Optimization for Image Quality Assessment

Abstract (English): Image Quality Assessment (IQA) predicts perceptual quality scores consistent with human judgments. Recent RL-based IQA methods built on MLLMs focus on generating visual quality descriptions and scores, ignoring two key reliability limitations: (i) although the model's prediction stability varies significantly across training samples, existing GRPO-based methods apply uniform advantage weighting, thereby amplifying noisy signals from unstable samples in gradient updates; (ii) most works emphasize text-grounded reasoning over images while overlooking the model's visual perception ability of image content. In this paper, we propose Q-Hawkeye, an RL-based reliable visual policy optimization framework that redesigns the learning signal through unified Uncertainty-Aware Dynamic Optimization and Perception-Aware Optimization. Q-Hawkeye estimates predictive uncertainty using the variance of predicted scores across multiple rollouts and leverages this uncertainty to reweight each sample's update strength, stabilizing policy optimization. To strengthen perceptual reliability, we construct paired inputs of degraded images and their original images and introduce an Implicit Perception Loss that constrains the model to ground its quality judgments in genuine visual evidence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Q-Hawkeye outperforms state-of-the-art methods and generalizes better across multiple datasets. The code and models will be made available.

摘要（中文）: 图像质量评估（IQA）旨在预测与人类主观判断一致的感知质量分数。近年来，基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的强化学习（RL）图像质量评估方法侧重于生成视觉质量描述和评分，却忽略了两个关键的可靠性限制：（i）尽管模型对不同训练样本的预测稳定性差异显著，但现有的基于广义策略优化（GRPO）的方法采用统一优势权重，从而在梯度更新中放大了来自不稳定样本的噪声信号；（ii）大多数工作强调文本引导的推理胜过图像，却忽视了模型对图像内容的视觉感知能力。在本文中，我们提出了Q-Hawkeye，一个基于强化学习的可靠视觉策略优化框架，该框架通过统一的不确定性感知动态优化和感知感知优化来重新设计学习信号。Q-Hawkeye通过多次展开（rollout）中预测分数的方差来估计预测的不确定性，并利用该不确定性来重新加权每个样本的更新强度，从而稳定策略优化。为了加强感知可靠性，我们构建了退化图像及其原始图像的配对输入，并引入了隐式感知损失，以约束模型将其质量判断建立在真实的视觉证据之上。大量的实验表明，Q-Hawkeye优于最先进的方法，并且在多个数据集上具有更好的泛化能力。代码和模型将会公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces Q-Hawkeye, a reinforcement learning-based framework for Image Quality Assessment that improves reliability by addressing unstable training samples and strengthening visual perception capabilities.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Q-Hawkeye，一个基于强化学习的图像质量评估框架，通过解决不稳定的训练样本和加强视觉感知能力来提高可靠性。

Authors: Wulin Xie, Rui Dai, Ruidong Ding, Kaikui Liu, Xiangxiang Chu, Xinwen Hou, Jie Wen

StreamSense: Streaming Social Task Detection with Selective Vision-Language Model Routing

Abstract (English): Live streaming platforms require real-time monitoring and reaction to social signals, utilizing partial and asynchronous evidence from video, text, and audio. We propose StreamSense, a streaming detector that couples a lightweight streaming encoder with selective routing to a Vision-Language Model (VLM) expert. StreamSense handles most timestamps with the lightweight streaming encoder, escalates hard/ambiguous cases to the VLM, and defers decisions when context is insufficient. The encoder is trained using (i) a cross-modal contrastive term to align visual/audio cues with textual signals, and (ii) an IoU-weighted loss that down-weights poorly overlapping target segments, mitigating label interference across segment boundaries. We evaluate StreamSense on multiple social streaming detection tasks (e.g., sentiment classification and hate content moderation), and the results show that StreamSense achieves higher accuracy than VLM-only streaming while only occasionally invoking the VLM, thereby reducing average latency and compute. Our results indicate that selective escalation and deferral are effective primitives for understanding streaming social tasks. Code is publicly available on GitHub.

摘要（中文）: 直播平台需要对社会信号进行实时监控和响应，利用来自视频、文本和音频的部分和异步证据。我们提出StreamSense，一种流式检测器，它将轻量级流式编码器与选择性路由耦合到视觉-语言模型（VLM）专家。StreamSense使用轻量级流式编码器处理大多数时间戳，将困难/模糊的情况升级到VLM，并在上下文信息不足时推迟决策。该编码器通过以下方式进行训练：（i）跨模态对比项，使视觉/音频线索与文本信号对齐；以及（ii）IoU加权损失，降低不良重叠目标片段的权重，从而减轻片段边界上的标签干扰。我们在多个社会流式检测任务（例如，情感分类和仇恨内容审核）上评估了StreamSense，结果表明，StreamSense实现了比仅VLM流式更高的准确率，同时只偶尔调用VLM，从而降低了平均延迟和计算量。我们的结果表明，选择性升级和延迟是理解流式社会任务的有效原语。代码已在GitHub上公开提供。

TLDR: StreamSense is proposed to monitor live streams using a lightweight encoder with selective routing to a VLM, improving accuracy and reducing latency for social task detection, especially around challenges such as sentiment analysis and content moderation.

简要说明: StreamSense 旨在通过轻量级编码器和选择性路由到 VLM 来监控直播流，从而提高社会任务检测的准确性并降低延迟，尤其是在诸如情感分析和内容审核等挑战方面。

Authors: Han Wang, Deyi Ji, Lanyun Zhu, Jiebo Luo, Roy Ka-Wei Lee

Stabilizing Consistency Training: A Flow Map Analysis and Self-Distillation

Abstract (English): Consistency models have been proposed for fast generative modeling, achieving results competitive with diffusion and flow models. However, these methods exhibit inherent instability and limited reproducibility when training from scratch, motivating subsequent work to explain and stabilize these issues. While these efforts have provided valuable insights, the explanations remain fragmented, and the theoretical relationships remain unclear. In this work, we provide a theoretical examination of consistency models by analyzing them from a flow map-based perspective. This joint analysis clarifies how training stability and convergence behavior can give rise to degenerate solutions. Building on these insights, we revisit self-distillation as a practical remedy for certain forms of suboptimal convergence and reformulate it to avoid excessive gradient norms for stable optimization. We further demonstrate that our strategy extends beyond image generation to diffusion-based policy learning, without reliance on a pretrained diffusion model for initialization, thereby illustrating its broader applicability.

摘要（中文）: 一致性模型已被提出用于快速生成建模，其成果可与扩散模型和流模型相媲美。然而，这些方法在从头训练时表现出内在的不稳定性和有限的可复现性，这促使后续工作解释和稳定这些问题。尽管这些努力提供了宝贵的见解，但解释仍然是零散的，并且理论关系仍不明确。在这项工作中，我们通过从基于流映射的视角分析一致性模型，从而对其进行理论考察。这种联合分析阐明了训练稳定性和收敛行为如何导致退化解。基于这些见解，我们重新审视自蒸馏作为某些次优收敛形式的实用补救措施，并对其进行重新调整，以避免过度梯度范数从而实现稳定优化。我们进一步证明，我们的策略可以扩展到基于扩散的策略学习，而无需依赖预训练的扩散模型进行初始化，从而证明了其更广泛的适用性。

TLDR: This paper analyzes the instability of consistency models using a flow map perspective, proposes a self-distillation based stabilization method, and demonstrates its applicability in both image generation and diffusion-based policy learning.

简要说明: 本文通过流图视角分析了一致性模型的不稳定性，提出一种基于自蒸馏的稳定方法，并展示了其在图像生成和基于扩散的策略学习中的适用性。

Authors: Youngjoong Kim, Duhoe Kim, Woosung Kim, Jaesik Park

SHED Light on Segmentation for Dense Prediction

Abstract (English): Dense prediction infers per-pixel values from a single image and is fundamental to 3D perception and robotics. Although real-world scenes exhibit strong structure, existing methods treat it as an independent pixel-wise prediction, often resulting in structural inconsistencies. We propose SHED, a novel encoder-decoder architecture that enforces geometric prior explicitly by incorporating segmentation into dense prediction. By bidirectional hierarchical reasoning, segment tokens are hierarchically pooled in the encoder and unpooled in the decoder to reverse the hierarchy. The model is supervised only at the final output, allowing the segment hierarchy to emerge without explicit segmentation supervision. SHED improves depth boundary sharpness and segment coherence, while demonstrating strong cross-domain generalization from synthetic to the real-world environments. Its hierarchy-aware decoder better captures global 3D scene layouts, leading to improved semantic segmentation performance. Moreover, SHED enhances 3D reconstruction quality and reveals interpretable part-level structures that are often missed by conventional pixel-wise methods.

摘要（中文）: 密集预测从单张图像推断每个像素的值，是3D感知和机器人学的基石。尽管真实世界场景展现出很强的结构性，但现有方法将其视为独立的像素级预测，往往导致结构上的不一致性。我们提出了一种新颖的编码器-解码器架构SHED，它通过将分割纳入密集预测来显式地强制执行几何先验。通过双向分层推理，分割令牌在编码器中进行分层池化，并在解码器中进行反池化，以逆转层级结构。该模型仅在最终输出处进行监督，从而允许分割层级在没有显式分割监督的情况下涌现。SHED提高了深度边界的清晰度和分割一致性，同时展示了从合成到真实世界环境的强大跨域泛化能力。其具有层级感知能力的解码器能更好地捕捉全局3D场景布局，从而提高了语义分割性能。此外，SHED增强了3D重建质量，并揭示了传统像素级方法经常遗漏的可解释的部分级结构。

TLDR: The paper introduces SHED, an encoder-decoder architecture that incorporates segmentation into dense prediction tasks, improving depth boundary sharpness, segment coherence, and cross-domain generalization without explicit segmentation supervision.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SHED，一种将分割融入密集预测任务的编码器-解码器架构，提高了深度边界清晰度、分割一致性和跨域泛化能力，且无需显式分割监督。

Authors: Seung Hyun Lee, Sangwoo Mo, Stella X. Yu

FlexMap: Generalized HD Map Construction from Flexible Camera Configurations

Abstract (English): High-definition (HD) maps provide essential semantic information of road structures for autonomous driving systems, yet current HD map construction methods require calibrated multi-camera setups and either implicit or explicit 2D-to-BEV transformations, making them fragile when sensors fail or camera configurations vary across vehicle fleets. We introduce FlexMap, unlike prior methods that are fixed to a specific N-camera rig, our approach adapts to variable camera configurations without any architectural changes or per-configuration retraining. Our key innovation eliminates explicit geometric projections by using a geometry-aware foundation model with cross-frame attention to implicitly encode 3D scene understanding in feature space. FlexMap features two core components: a spatial-temporal enhancement module that separates cross-view spatial reasoning from temporal dynamics, and a camera-aware decoder with latent camera tokens, enabling view-adaptive attention without the need for projection matrices. Experiments demonstrate that FlexMap outperforms existing methods across multiple configurations while maintaining robustness to missing views and sensor variations, enabling more practical real-world deployment.

摘要（中文）: 高清（HD）地图为自动驾驶系统提供道路结构的基本语义信息，然而，当前的HD地图构建方法需要校准的多相机设置，以及隐式或显式的2D到BEV的转换，这使得它们在传感器故障或车辆群体的相机配置变化时显得脆弱。我们引入了FlexMap，与固定于特定N相机平台的先前方法不同，我们的方法能够适应可变的相机配置，而无需任何架构更改或针对每种配置的重新训练。我们的关键创新在于消除了显式几何投影，通过使用具备几何感知能力的基模型，利用跨帧注意力隐式地在特征空间中编码3D场景理解。FlexMap包含两个核心组件：一个空间-时间增强模块，将跨视图的空间推理与时间动态分离；以及一个带有潜在相机令牌的相机感知解码器，无需投影矩阵即可实现视图自适应的注意力机制。实验表明，FlexMap在多种配置下优于现有方法，同时保持对缺失视图和传感器变化的鲁棒性，从而实现更实用的真实场景部署。

TLDR: FlexMap constructs HD maps from flexible camera configurations using a geometry-aware foundation model and camera-aware decoder, eliminating the need for explicit geometric projections and per-configuration retraining. It demonstrates robustness to missing views and sensor variations, leading to more practical real-world deployment.

简要说明: FlexMap利用几何感知基础模型和相机感知解码器，从灵活的相机配置构建高清地图，无需显式几何投影和每次配置的重新训练。它对缺失视图和传感器变化具有鲁棒性，从而实现更实际的真实世界部署。

Coarse-to-Real: Generative Rendering for Populated Dynamic Scenes

Abstract (English): Traditional rendering pipelines rely on complex assets, accurate materials and lighting, and substantial computational resources to produce realistic imagery, yet they still face challenges in scalability and realism for populated dynamic scenes. We present C2R (Coarse-to-Real), a generative rendering framework that synthesizes real-style urban crowd videos from coarse 3D simulations. Our approach uses coarse 3D renderings to explicitly control scene layout, camera motion, and human trajectories, while a learned neural renderer generates realistic appearance, lighting, and fine-scale dynamics guided by text prompts. To overcome the lack of paired training data between coarse simulations and real videos, we adopt a two-phase mixed CG-real training strategy that learns a strong generative prior from large-scale real footage and introduces controllability through shared implicit spatio-temporal features across domains. The resulting system supports coarse-to-fine control, generalizes across diverse CG and game inputs, and produces temporally consistent, controllable, and realistic urban scene videos from minimal 3D input. We will release the model and project webpage at https://gonzalognogales.github.io/coarse2real/.

EditYourself: Audio-Driven Generation and Manipulation of Talking Head Videos with Diffusion Transformers

Abstract (English): Current generative video models excel at producing novel content from text and image prompts, but leave a critical gap in editing existing pre-recorded videos, where minor alterations to the spoken script require preserving motion, temporal coherence, speaker identity, and accurate lip synchronization. We introduce EditYourself, a DiT-based framework for audio-driven video-to-video (V2V) editing that enables transcript-based modification of talking head videos, including the seamless addition, removal, and retiming of visually spoken content. Building on a general-purpose video diffusion model, EditYourself augments its V2V capabilities with audio conditioning and region-aware, edit-focused training extensions. This enables precise lip synchronization and temporally coherent restructuring of existing performances via spatiotemporal inpainting, including the synthesis of realistic human motion in newly added segments, while maintaining visual fidelity and identity consistency over long durations. 摘要（中文）: 目前，生成式视频模型擅长根据文本和图像提示生成新内容，但忽略了一个关键缺口：编辑现有预录视频。在现有视频中，对口语脚本的微小改动需要保持动作、时间连贯性、说话者身份和准确的唇音同步。我们介绍 EditYourself，这是一个基于 DiT 的音频驱动视频到视频 (V2V) 编辑框架，能够基于文本转录修改人物对话视频，包括对视觉口语内容进行无缝添加、删除和重新定时。EditYourself 基于通用视频扩散模型，通过音频条件化和区域感知、以编辑为中心的训练扩展，增强了其 V2V 能力。这使得可以通过时空修复技术实现对现有表演的精确唇音同步和时间连贯性重构，包括在新添加片段中合成逼真的人体运动，同时在长时间内保持视觉保真度和身份一致性。这项工作代表了生成式视频模型朝着成为专业视频后期制作的实用工具迈出的基础性一步。

Authors: John Flynn, Wolfgang Paier, Dimitar Dinev, Sam Nhut Nguyen, Hayk Poghosyan, Manuel Toribio, Sandipan Banerjee, Guy Gafni

Continual Policy Distillation from Distributed Reinforcement Learning Teachers

Abstract (English): Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL) aims to develop lifelong learning agents to continuously acquire knowledge across diverse tasks while mitigating catastrophic forgetting. This requires efficiently managing the stability-plasticity dilemma and leveraging prior experience to rapidly generalize to novel tasks. While various enhancement strategies for both aspects have been proposed, achieving scalable performance by directly applying RL to sequential task streams remains challenging. In this paper, we propose a novel teacher-student framework that decouples CRL into two independent processes: training single-task teacher models through distributed RL and continually distilling them into a central generalist model. This design is motivated by the observation that RL excels at solving single tasks, while policy distillation -- a relatively stable supervised learning process -- is well aligned with large foundation models and multi-task learning. Moreover, a mixture-of-experts (MoE) architecture and a replay-based approach are employed to enhance the plasticity and stability of the continual policy distillation process. Extensive experiments on the Meta-World benchmark demonstrate that our framework enables efficient continual RL, recovering over 85% of teacher performance while constraining task-wise forgetting to within 10%.

摘要（中文）: 持续强化学习 (CRL) 旨在开发终身学习智能体，使其能够持续地跨越不同的任务获取知识，同时缓解灾难性遗忘。这需要有效地管理稳定性和可塑性之间的矛盾，并利用先前的经验来快速泛化到新的任务。虽然针对这两个方面已经提出了各种增强策略，但直接应用强化学习到顺序任务流来实现可扩展的性能仍然具有挑战性。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的师生框架，将 CRL 解耦为两个独立的过程：通过分布式强化学习训练单任务教师模型，并将它们持续地提炼到一个中心化的通用模型中。这种设计是受到以下观察结果的启发：强化学习擅长解决单个任务，而策略蒸馏——一种相对稳定的监督学习过程——与大型基础模型和多任务学习非常契合。此外，我们采用了混合专家 (MoE) 架构和基于回放的方法来增强持续策略蒸馏过程的可塑性和稳定性。在 Meta-World 基准上的大量实验表明，我们的框架能够实现高效的持续强化学习，在将任务遗忘限制在 10% 以内的同时，恢复超过 85% 的教师模型性能。

TLDR: The paper proposes a teacher-student framework for continual reinforcement learning, using distributed RL to train single-task teachers and then distilling their knowledge into a central generalist model, achieving good performance and mitigating forgetting.

Authors: Yuxuan Li, Qijun He, Mingqi Yuan, Wen-Tse Chen, Jeff Schneider, Jiayu Chen

Learning Reward Functions for Cooperative Resilience in Multi-Agent Systems

Abstract (English): Multi-agent systems often operate in dynamic and uncertain environments, where agents must not only pursue individual goals but also safeguard collective functionality. This challenge is especially acute in mixed-motive multi-agent systems. This work focuses on cooperative resilience, the ability of agents to anticipate, resist, recover, and transform in the face of disruptions, a critical yet underexplored property in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning. We study how reward function design influences resilience in mixed-motive settings and introduce a novel framework that learns reward functions from ranked trajectories, guided by a cooperative resilience metric. Agents are trained in a suite of social dilemma environments using three reward strategies: i) traditional individual reward; ii) resilience-inferred reward; and iii) hybrid that balance both. We explore three reward parameterizations-linear models, hand-crafted features, and neural networks, and employ two preference-based learning algorithms to infer rewards from behavioral rankings. Our results demonstrate that hybrid strategy significantly improve robustness under disruptions without degrading task performance and reduce catastrophic outcomes like resource overuse. These findings underscore the importance of reward design in fostering resilient cooperation, and represent a step toward developing robust multi-agent systems capable of sustaining cooperation in uncertain environments.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体系统通常运行在动态和不确定的环境中，智能体不仅要追求个体目标，还要保障集体功能。这种挑战在混合动机的多智能体系统中尤为突出。本工作侧重于合作韧性，即智能体面对干扰时进行预测、抵抗、恢复和转型的能力，这是多智能体强化学习中一种至关重要但未被充分探索的特性。我们研究了奖励函数设计如何影响混合动机环境中的韧性，并引入了一种新颖的框架，该框架基于合作韧性指标，从排序后的轨迹中学习奖励函数。智能体在一系列社会困境环境中使用三种奖励策略进行训练：i) 传统的个体奖励；ii) 韧性推导的奖励；iii) 平衡两者的混合奖励。我们探索了三种奖励参数化方法——线性模型、手工设计的特征和神经网络，并采用两种基于偏好的学习算法从行为排序中推断奖励。我们的结果表明，混合策略显著提高了干扰下的鲁棒性，且没有降低任务性能，并减少了资源过度使用等灾难性结果。这些发现强调了奖励设计在培养具有弹性的合作中的重要性，并代表着开发能够维持不确定环境中合作的鲁棒多智能体系统迈出了一步。

TLDR: This paper introduces a framework for learning reward functions that promote cooperative resilience in multi-agent systems, particularly in mixed-motive scenarios, demonstrating improved robustness against disruptions.

Authors: Manuela Chacon-Chamorro, Luis Felipe Giraldo, Nicanor Quijano

Latent Spherical Flow Policy for Reinforcement Learning with Combinatorial Actions

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) with combinatorial action spaces remains challenging because feasible action sets are exponentially large and governed by complex feasibility constraints, making direct policy parameterization impractical. Existing approaches embed task-specific value functions into constrained optimization programs or learn deterministic structured policies, sacrificing generality and policy expressiveness. We propose a solver-induced \emph{latent spherical flow policy} that brings the expressiveness of modern generative policies to combinatorial RL while guaranteeing feasibility by design. Our method, LSFlow, learns a \emph{stochastic} policy in a compact continuous latent space via spherical flow matching, and delegates feasibility to a combinatorial optimization solver that maps each latent sample to a valid structured action. To improve efficiency, we train the value network directly in the latent space, avoiding repeated solver calls during policy optimization. To address the piecewise-constant and discontinuous value landscape induced by solver-based action selection, we introduce a smoothed Bellman operator that yields stable, well-defined learning targets. Empirically, our approach outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by an average of 20.6\% across a range of challenging combinatorial RL tasks.

摘要（中文）: 组合动作空间的强化学习（RL）仍然具有挑战性，因为可行动作集呈指数级增长，且受限于复杂的约束条件，导致直接策略参数化不切实际。现有方法将特定任务的价值函数嵌入到约束优化程序中，或学习确定性的结构化策略，牺牲了通用性和策略表达能力。我们提出了一种求解器诱导的\emph{隐空间球面流策略}，将现代生成策略的表达能力带入组合RL，同时通过设计保证可行性。我们的方法，LSFlow，通过球面流匹配，在紧凑的连续隐空间中学习一种\emph{随机}策略，并将可行性问题委托给组合优化求解器，该求解器将每个隐空间样本映射到一个有效的结构化动作。为了提高效率，我们直接在隐空间中训练价值网络，避免在策略优化过程中重复调用求解器。为了解决基于求解器的动作选择所导致的片状常数和不连续的价值图景，我们引入了一种平滑的贝尔曼算子，从而产生稳定、明确的学习目标。在经验上，我们的方法在多个具有挑战性的组合RL任务中，比最先进的基线方法平均提高了20.6%。

TLDR: This paper introduces LSFlow, a novel reinforcement learning method for combinatorial action spaces that uses a latent spherical flow policy to guarantee feasibility and improve policy expressiveness, outperforming existing baselines.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为LSFlow的新型强化学习方法，用于解决组合动作空间问题。该方法使用潜在球形流策略来保证可行性并提高策略表达能力，优于现有基线。
