Authors: Lingkai Kong, Anagha Satish, Hezi Jiang, Akseli Kangaslahti, Andrew Ma, Wenbo Chen, Mingxiao Song, Lily Xu, Milind Tambe

Boosting CVaR Policy Optimization with Quantile Gradients

Abstract (English): Optimizing Conditional Value-at-risk (CVaR) using policy gradient (a.k.a CVaR-PG) faces significant challenges of sample inefficiency. This inefficiency stems from the fact that it focuses on tail-end performance and overlooks many sampled trajectories. We address this problem by augmenting CVaR with an expected quantile term. Quantile optimization admits a dynamic programming formulation that leverages all sampled data, thus improves sample efficiency. This does not alter the CVaR objective since CVaR corresponds to the expectation of quantile over the tail. Empirical results in domains with verifiable risk-averse behavior show that our algorithm within the Markovian policy class substantially improves upon CVaR-PG and consistently outperforms other existing methods.

摘要（中文）: 使用策略梯度优化条件风险价值 (CVaR) （也称为 CVaR-PG）面临着样本效率低下的重大挑战。这种低效率源于它专注于尾端表现，而忽略了许多采样的轨迹。我们通过用一个期望分位数项来增强 CVaR 来解决这个问题。分位数优化容许动态规划公式，可以利用所有采样数据，从而提高样本效率。由于 CVaR 对应于尾端分位数的期望，因此这不会改变 CVaR 目标。在具有可验证风险规避行为的领域中的经验结果表明，我们的算法在马尔可夫策略类中显著优于 CVaR-PG，并且始终优于其他现有方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a method to improve the sample efficiency of CVaR policy optimization by augmenting it with an expected quantile term, leading to better risk-averse performance in Markovian policy classes.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种通过使用期望分位数项来增强 CVaR 策略优化，提高其样本效率的方法，从而提升马尔可夫策略类的风险规避性能。

Authors: Yudong Luo, Erick Delage

Causal Imitation Learning Under Measurement Error and Distribution Shift

Abstract (English): We study offline imitation learning (IL) when part of the decision-relevant state is observed only through noisy measurements and the distribution may change between training and deployment. Such settings induce spurious state-action correlations, so standard behavioral cloning (BC) -- whether conditioning on raw measurements or ignoring them -- can converge to systematically biased policies under distribution shift. We propose a general framework for IL under measurement error, inspired by explicitly modeling the causal relationships among the variables, yielding a target that retains a causal interpretation and is robust to distribution shift. Building on ideas from proximal causal inference, we introduce \texttt{CausIL}, which treats noisy state observations as proxy variables, and we provide identification conditions under which the target policy is recoverable from demonstrations without rewards or interactive expert queries. We develop estimators for both discrete and continuous state spaces; for continuous settings, we use an adversarial procedure over RKHS function classes to learn the required parameters. We evaluate \texttt{CausIL} on semi-simulated longitudinal data from the PhysioNet/Computing in Cardiology Challenge 2019 cohort and demonstrate improved robustness to distribution shift compared to BC baselines.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了离线模仿学习 (IL)，在该场景下，部分与决策相关的状态只能通过带噪声的测量值观察到，且训练和部署之间分布可能发生变化。这种设置会引起虚假的状态-动作相关性，因此标准的行为克隆 (BC)——无论是条件作用于原始测量值还是忽略它们——可能在分布偏移下收敛到系统性偏差的策略。我们提出了一个在测量误差下进行 IL 的通用框架，其灵感来自于显式地建模变量之间的因果关系，从而产生一个保留因果解释且对分布偏移具有鲁棒性的目标。在近端因果推断的思想基础上，我们引入了 \texttt{CausIL}，它将带噪声的状态观测视为代理变量，并提供了识别条件，在这些条件下，目标策略可以从演示中恢复，而无需奖励或交互式的专家查询。我们为离散和连续状态空间开发了估计器；对于连续设置，我们使用基于 RKHS 函数类的对抗过程来学习所需的参数。我们在来自 PhysioNet/Computing in Cardiology Challenge 2019 队列的半模拟纵向数据上评估了 \texttt{CausIL}，并证明了与 BC 基线相比，其对分布偏移具有更高的鲁棒性。

TLDR: This paper proposes a causal imitation learning framework ( exttt{CausIL}) to address the issue of spurious state-action correlations caused by noisy state measurements and distribution shifts in offline imitation learning, demonstrating improved robustness compared to behavioral cloning.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种因果模仿学习框架 ( exttt{CausIL})，旨在解决离线模仿学习中由噪声状态测量和分布漂移引起的虚假状态-动作相关性问题，并证明与行为克隆相比，其鲁棒性有所提高。

Toward Fully Autonomous Driving: AI, Challenges, Opportunities, and Needs

Abstract (English): Automated driving (AD) is promising, but the transition to fully autonomous driving is, among other things, subject to the real, ever-changing open world and the resulting challenges. Authors: Lars Ullrich, Michael Buchholz, Klaus Dietmayer, Knut Graichen

ReloPush-BOSS: Optimization-guided Nonmonotone Rearrangement Planning for a Car-like Robot Pusher

Abstract (English): We focus on multi-object rearrangement planning in densely cluttered environments using a car-like robot pusher. The combination of kinematic, geometric and physics constraints underlying this domain results in challenging nonmonotone problem instances which demand breaking each manipulation action into multiple parts to achieve a desired object rearrangement. Prior work tackles such instances by planning prerelocations, temporary object displacements that enable constraint satisfaction, but deciding where to prerelocate remains difficult due to local minima leading to infeasible or high-cost paths. Our key insight is that these minima can be avoided by steering a prerelocation optimization toward low-cost regions informed by Dubins path classification. These optimized prerelocations are integrated into an object traversability graph that encodes kinematic, geometric, and pushing constraints. Searching this graph in a depth-first fashion results in efficient, feasible rearrangement sequences. Across a series of densely cluttered scenarios with up to 13 objects, our framework, ReloPush-BOSS, exhibits consistently highest success rates and shortest pushing paths compared to state-of-the-art baselines. Hardware experiments on a 1/10 car-like pusher demonstrate the robustness of our approach. Code and footage from our experiments can be found at: https://fluentrobotics.com/relopushboss.

摘要（中文）: 我们专注于使用类汽车机器人推杆，在密集杂乱环境中进行多目标重排列规划。该领域中运动学、几何和物理约束的结合导致了具有挑战性的非单调问题实例，这需要将每个操作动作分解成多个部分才能实现期望的对象重排列。先前的工作通过规划预重定位（一种临时的对象位移，以实现约束满足）来解决这些实例，但由于局部最小值导致不可行或高成本路径，因此决定预重定位的位置仍然很困难。我们的关键洞察是，通过将预重定位优化引导至由Dubins路径分类告知的低成本区域，可以避免这些最小值。这些优化的预重定位被整合到一个对象可遍历性图中，该图编码了运动学、几何和推动约束。以深度优先的方式搜索该图可以产生高效、可行的重排列序列。在一系列最多包含13个对象的密集杂乱场景中，我们的框架 ReloPush-BOSS与最先进的基准相比，始终表现出最高的成功率和最短的推动路径。在1/10类汽车推杆上的硬件实验证明了我们方法的稳健性。我们实验的代码和视频可以在以下网址找到：https://fluentrobotics.com/relopushboss。

TLDR: The paper presents ReloPush-BOSS, a novel framework for multi-object rearrangement planning in cluttered environments using a car-like robot pusher, achieving high success rates and shorter paths through optimization-guided prerelocations, demonstrated in both simulation and hardware.

简要说明: 本文介绍 ReloPush-BOSS，一个新颖的框架，用于使用类似汽车的机器人推手在杂乱环境中进行多目标重排规划。通过优化引导的预重定位，该框架实现了高成功率和更短的路径，并在仿真和硬件中得到了演示。

Authors: Jeeho Ahn, Christoforos Mavrogiannis

Aligning Microscopic Vehicle and Macroscopic Traffic Statistics: Reconstructing Driving Behavior from Partial Data

Abstract (English): A driving algorithm that aligns with good human driving practices, or at the very least collaborates effectively with human drivers, is crucial for developing safe and efficient autonomous vehicles. In practice, two main approaches are commonly adopted: (i) supervised or imitation learning, which requires comprehensive naturalistic driving data capturing all states that influence a vehicle's decisions and corresponding actions, and (ii) reinforcement learning (RL), where the simulated driving environment either matches or is intentionally more challenging than real-world conditions. Both methods depend on high-quality observations of real-world driving behavior, which are often difficult and costly to obtain. State-of-the-art sensors on individual vehicles can gather microscopic data, but they lack context about the surrounding conditions. Conversely, roadside sensors can capture traffic flow and other macroscopic characteristics, but they cannot associate this information with individual vehicles on a microscopic level. Motivated by this complementarity, we propose a framework that reconstructs unobserved microscopic states from macroscopic observations, using microscopic data to anchor observed vehicle behaviors, and learns a shared policy whose behavior is microscopically consistent with the partially observed trajectories and actions and macroscopically aligned with target traffic statistics when deployed population-wide. Such constrained and regularized policies promote realistic flow patterns and safe coordination with human drivers at scale.

摘要（中文）: 一种符合良好人类驾驶习惯，或者至少能与人类驾驶员有效协作的驾驶算法，对于开发安全高效的自动驾驶汽车至关重要。 在实践中，通常采用两种主要方法：（i）监督学习或模仿学习，这需要全面的自然驾驶数据，以捕获所有影响车辆决策的状态以及相应的动作；以及（ii）强化学习（RL），其中模拟驾驶环境匹配或者有意比真实世界条件更具挑战性。 这两种方法都依赖于对真实世界驾驶行为的高质量观察，而这些观察通常难以获得且成本高昂。 单个车辆上的最先进传感器可以收集微观数据，但它们缺乏关于周围环境的背景信息。 相反，路边传感器可以捕获交通流量和其他宏观特征，但它们无法将此信息与微观层面的单个车辆相关联。 受这种互补性的启发，我们提出了一种框架，该框架利用微观数据来锚定观察到的车辆行为，从而从宏观观察中重建未观察到的微观状态，并且学习一种共享策略，该策略的行为在微观上与部分观察到的轨迹和动作一致，在宏观上与大规模部署时的目标交通统计数据对齐。 这种受约束和正则化的策略促进了现实的交通流模式，并实现了与人类驾驶员的大规模安全协调。

TLDR: The paper proposes a framework to reconstruct microscopic vehicle states from macroscopic traffic observations, aiming to learn driving policies that align with real-world traffic statistics for autonomous vehicle development.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种从宏观交通观测重建微观车辆状态的框架，旨在学习与真实交通统计数据对齐的驾驶策略，以用于自动驾驶汽车的开发。

Authors: Zhihao Zhang, Keith Redmill, Chengyang Peng, Bowen Weng

EvoClinician: A Self-Evolving Agent for Multi-Turn Medical Diagnosis via Test-Time Evolutionary Learning

Abstract (English): Prevailing medical AI operates on an unrealistic ''one-shot'' model, diagnosing from a complete patient file. However, real-world diagnosis is an iterative inquiry where Clinicians sequentially ask questions and order tests to strategically gather information while managing cost and time. To address this, we first propose Med-Inquire, a new benchmark designed to evaluate an agent's ability to perform multi-turn diagnosis. Built upon a dataset of real-world clinical cases, Med-Inquire simulates the diagnostic process by hiding a complete patient file behind specialized Patient and Examination agents. They force the agent to proactively ask questions and order tests to gather information piece by piece. To tackle the challenges posed by Med-Inquire, we then introduce EvoClinician, a self-evolving agent that learns efficient diagnostic strategies at test time. Its core is a ''Diagnose-Grade-Evolve'' loop: an Actor agent attempts a diagnosis; a Process Grader agent performs credit assignment by evaluating each action for both clinical yield and resource efficiency; finally, an Evolver agent uses this feedback to update the Actor's strategy by evolving its prompt and memory. Our experiments show EvoClinician outperforms continual learning baselines and other self-evolving agents like memory agents. The code is available at https://github.com/yf-he/EvoClinician

摘要（中文）: 当前主流的医学人工智能运行在一个不切实际的“一次性”模型上，即从一个完整的患者档案进行诊断。然而，现实世界的诊断是一个迭代式的探究过程，临床医生按顺序提问和进行检查，以策略性地收集信息，同时管理成本和时间。为了解决这个问题，我们首先提出了Med-Inquire，一个新的基准，旨在评估智能体执行多轮诊断的能力。Med-Inquire建立在真实临床病例的数据集之上，通过隐藏在一个专门的患者和检查智能体背后的完整患者档案来模拟诊断过程。它们迫使智能体主动提问和进行检查，以逐片地收集信息。为了应对Med-Inquire带来的挑战，我们随后引入了EvoClinician，一种自主进化的智能体，它可以在测试时学习高效的诊断策略。它的核心是一个“诊断-评估-进化”循环：一个行动者智能体尝试诊断；一个过程评估者智能体通过评估每个行动的临床效益和资源效率来进行信用分配；最后，一个进化者智能体利用这个反馈，通过进化其提示和记忆来更新行动者的策略。我们的实验表明，EvoClinician的性能优于持续学习基线和其他自进化智能体，例如记忆智能体。代码可在https://github.com/yf-he/EvoClinician 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces Med-Inquire, a new benchmark for multi-turn medical diagnosis with sequential information gathering, and EvoClinician, a test-time evolving agent that outperforms baselines by iteratively diagnosing, grading, and evolving its strategy.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了Med-Inquire，一个新的多轮医疗诊断基准，侧重于序列信息收集；并介绍了EvoClinician，一个测试时进化的智能体，通过迭代诊断、评估和改进其策略，优于其他基线方法。

Authors: Yufei He, Juncheng Liu, Zhiyuan Hu, Yulin Chen, Yue Liu, Yuan Sui, Yibo Li, Nuo Chen, Jun Hu, Bryan Hooi, Xinxing Xu, Jiang Bian

Defining Operational Conditions for Safety-Critical AI-Based Systems from Data

Abstract (English): Artificial Intelligence (AI) has been on the rise in many domains, including numerous safety-critical applications. However, for complex systems found in the real world, or when data already exist, defining the underlying environmental conditions is extremely challenging. This often results in an incomplete description of the environment in which the AI-based system must operate. Nevertheless, this description, called the Operational Design Domain (ODD), is required in many domains for the certification of AI-based systems. Traditionally, the ODD is created in the early stages of the development process, drawing on sophisticated expert knowledge and related standards. This paper presents a novel Safety-by-Design method to a posteriori define the ODD from previously collected data using a multi-dimensional kernel-based representation. This approach is validated through both Monte Carlo methods and a real-world aviation use case for a future safety-critical collision-avoidance system. Moreover, by defining under what conditions two ODDs are equal, the paper shows that the data-driven ODD can equal the original, underlying hidden ODD of the data. Utilizing the novel, Safe-by-Design kernel-based ODD enables future certification of data-driven, safety-critical AI-based systems.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能(AI)已在众多领域蓬勃发展，包括大量安全攸关的应用。然而，对于现实世界中存在的复杂系统，或者当数据已经存在时，定义底层的环境条件极具挑战性。这常常导致对AI系统必须运行的环境描述不完整。尽管如此，这种被称为运行设计域(ODD)的描述，在许多领域对于AI系统认证而言是必需的。传统上，ODD是在开发过程的早期阶段创建的，借鉴了精深的专家知识和相关标准。本文提出了一种新颖的安全设计方法，通过多维度的基于核的表示，根据先前收集的数据事后定义ODD。该方法通过蒙特卡洛方法和针对未来安全攸关的防撞系统的真实世界航空用例进行了验证。此外，通过定义两个ODD在何种条件下相等，本文表明数据驱动的ODD可以等于数据的原始、底层的隐藏ODD。利用这种新颖的、安全设计的、基于核的ODD，能够实现未来数据驱动的、安全攸关的AI系统的认证。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel, Safety-by-Design method for defining the Operational Design Domain (ODD) of safety-critical AI systems from existing data using a multi-dimensional kernel-based representation, validated with Monte Carlo methods and an aviation use case. It aims to enable future certification of such systems.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新颖的安全设计方法，使用多维核表示从现有数据中定义安全关键型人工智能系统的操作设计域（ODD），并通过蒙特卡罗方法和航空用例进行验证。旨在为未来此类系统的认证提供支持。

Authors: Johann Christensen, Elena Hoemann, Frank Köster, Sven Hallerbach

EAG-PT: Emission-Aware Gaussians and Path Tracing for Indoor Scene Reconstruction and Editing

Abstract (English): Recent reconstruction methods based on radiance field such as NeRF and 3DGS reproduce indoor scenes with high visual fidelity, but break down under scene editing due to baked illumination and the lack of explicit light transport. In contrast, physically based inverse rendering relies on mesh representations and path tracing, which enforce correct light transport but place strong requirements on geometric fidelity, becoming a practical bottleneck for real indoor scenes. In this work, we propose Emission-Aware Gaussians and Path Tracing (EAG-PT), aiming for physically based light transport with a unified 2D Gaussian representation. Our design is based on three cores: (1) using 2D Gaussians as a unified scene representation and transport-friendly geometry proxy that avoids reconstructed mesh, (2) explicitly separating emissive and non-emissive components during reconstruction for further scene editing, and (3) decoupling reconstruction from final rendering by using efficient single-bounce optimization and high-quality multi-bounce path tracing after scene editing. Experiments on synthetic and real indoor scenes show that EAG-PT produces more natural and physically consistent renders after editing than radiant scene reconstructions, while preserving finer geometric detail and avoiding mesh-induced artifacts compared to mesh-based inverse path tracing. These results suggest promising directions for future use in interior design, XR content creation, and embodied AI.

摘要（中文）: 基于辐射场的最新重建方法，例如NeRF和3DGS，能够以高视觉保真度再现室内场景，但由于烘焙光照和缺乏显式光照传输，在场景编辑下会失效。相比之下，基于物理的逆渲染依赖于网格表示和路径追踪，这可以保证正确的光照传输，但对几何保真度要求很高，成为真实室内场景的一个实际瓶颈。在这项工作中，我们提出了发射感知高斯和路径追踪（EAG-PT），旨在利用统一的2D高斯表示实现基于物理的光照传输。我们的设计基于三个核心：（1）使用2D高斯作为统一的场景表示和方便传输的几何代理，从而避免重建网格；（2）在重建过程中显式地分离发射和非发射分量，以便进一步进行场景编辑；（3）通过使用高效的单次反弹优化和场景编辑后高质量的多次反弹路径追踪，将重建与最终渲染解耦。在合成和真实室内场景上的实验表明，与辐射场景重建相比，EAG-PT在编辑后产生了更自然和物理上一致的渲染结果，同时保留了更精细的几何细节，并且避免了基于网格的逆向路径追踪带来的网格伪影。这些结果为室内设计、XR内容创作和具身人工智能的未来应用提供了有希望的方向。

TLDR: EAG-PT introduces a novel approach for indoor scene reconstruction and editing by using Emission-Aware Gaussians and path tracing, achieving physically consistent renders after editing with finer geometric details compared to existing methods.

简要说明: EAG-PT提出了一种新颖的室内场景重建和编辑方法，该方法采用发射感知高斯函数和路径追踪，与现有方法相比，在编辑后实现了物理上一致的渲染效果，并具有更精细的几何细节。

Authors: Xijie Yang, Mulin Yu, Changjian Jiang, Kerui Ren, Tao Lu, Jiangmiao Pang, Dahua Lin, Bo Dai, Linning Xu

Value-at-Risk Constrained Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): We introduce the Value-at-Risk Constrained Policy Optimization algorithm (VaR-CPO), a sample efficient and conservative method designed to optimize Value-at-Risk (VaR) constraints directly. Empirically, we demonstrate that VaR-CPO is capable of safe exploration, achieving zero constraint violations during training in feasible environments, a critical property that baseline methods fail to uphold. To overcome the inherent non-differentiability of the VaR constraint, we employ the one-sided Chebyshev inequality to obtain a tractable surrogate based on the first two moments of the cost return. Additionally, by extending the trust-region framework of the Constrained Policy Optimization (CPO) method, we provide rigorous worst-case bounds for both policy improvement and constraint violation during the training process.

摘要（中文）: 我们引入了风险价值约束策略优化算法（VaR-CPO），这是一种样本高效且保守的方法，旨在直接优化风险价值（VaR）约束。实验表明，VaR-CPO能够进行安全探索，在可行环境中训练期间实现零约束违规，这是基线方法无法维持的关键特性。为了克服VaR约束固有的不可微性，我们采用单侧切比雪夫不等式来获得一个基于成本回报的一阶和二阶矩的可处理替代。此外，通过扩展约束策略优化（CPO）方法的信任区域框架，我们为训练过程中策略改进和约束违规提供了严格的最坏情况界限。

TLDR: The paper introduces VaR-CPO, a sample-efficient and conservative reinforcement learning algorithm that directly optimizes Value-at-Risk (VaR) constraints using a trust-region framework, achieving zero constraint violations during training.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为VaR-CPO的强化学习算法，该算法具有样本高效性和保守性，它使用信任域框架直接优化风险价值（VaR）约束，并在训练过程中实现零约束违规。

Authors: Rohan Tangri, Jan-Peter Calliess

Detect and Act: Automated Dynamic Optimizer through Meta-Black-Box Optimization

Abstract (English): Dynamic Optimization Problems (DOPs) are challenging to address due to their complex nature, i.e., dynamic environment variation. Evolutionary Computation methods are generally advantaged in solving DOPs since they resemble dynamic biological evolution. However, existing evolutionary dynamic optimization methods rely heavily on human-crafted adaptive strategy to detect environment variation in DOPs, and then adapt the searching strategy accordingly. These hand-crafted strategies may perform ineffectively at out-of-box scenarios. In this paper, we propose a reinforcement learning-assisted approach to enable automated variation detection and self-adaption in evolutionary algorithms. This is achieved by borrowing the bi-level learning-to-optimize idea from recent Meta-Black-Box Optimization works. We use a deep Q-network as optimization dynamics detector and searching strategy adapter: It is fed as input with current-step optimization state and then dictates desired control parameters to underlying evolutionary algorithms for next-step optimization. The learning objective is to maximize the expected performance gain across a problem distribution. Once trained, our approach could generalize toward unseen DOPs with automated environment variation detection and self-adaption. To facilitate comprehensive validation, we further construct an easy-to-difficult DOPs testbed with diverse synthetic instances. Extensive benchmark results demonstrate flexible searching behavior and superior performance of our approach in solving DOPs, compared to state-of-the-art baselines.

摘要（中文）: 动态优化问题（DOPs）因其复杂性，即动态环境变化，而难以解决。进化计算方法通常在解决DOPs方面具有优势，因为它们类似于动态生物进化。然而，现有的进化动态优化方法严重依赖于人工设计的自适应策略来检测DOPs中的环境变化，然后相应地调整搜索策略。这些手工设计的策略可能在开箱即用的场景中表现不佳。在本文中，我们提出了一种强化学习辅助的方法，以实现进化算法中的自动变异检测和自适应。这通过借鉴最近的元黑盒优化工作中的双层学习优化思想来实现。我们使用深度Q网络作为优化动态检测器和搜索策略适配器：它以当前步骤的优化状态作为输入，然后将所需的控制参数指示给底层进化算法以进行下一步优化。学习目标是最大化整个问题分布的预期性能增益。一旦训练完成，我们的方法就可以推广到具有自动环境变异检测和自适应的未知DOP。为了便于全面验证，我们进一步构建了一个由易到难的DOPs测试平台，其中包含各种合成实例。大量的基准测试结果表明，与最先进的基线方法相比，我们的方法在解决DOPs方面具有灵活的搜索行为和卓越的性能。

TLDR: This paper proposes a reinforcement learning-assisted evolutionary algorithm for dynamic optimization problems, using a deep Q-network for automated variation detection and self-adaptation of search strategies, demonstrating superior performance on a newly constructed DOPs testbed.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于强化学习的进化算法来解决动态优化问题。该方法利用深度Q网络自动检测环境变化并自适应调整搜索策略，并在新建的DOPs测试平台上展示了优越的性能。

Authors: Zijian Gao, Yuanting Zhong, Zeyuan Ma, Yue-Jiao Gong, Hongshu Guo

DRL-Enabled Trajectory Planing for UAV-Assisted VLC: Optimal Altitude and Reward Design

Abstract (English): Recently, the integration of unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) and visible light communication (VLC) technologies has emerged as a promising solution to offer flexible communication and efficient lighting. This letter investigates the three-dimensional trajectory planning in a UAV-assisted VLC system, where a UAV is dispatched to collect data from ground users (GUs). The core objective is to develop a trajectory planning framework that minimizes UAV flight distance, which is equivalent to maximizing the data collection efficiency. This issue is formulated as a challenging mixed-integer non-convex optimization problem. To tackle it, we first derive a closed-form optimal flight altitude under specific VLC channel gain threshold. Subsequently, we optimize the UAV horizontal trajectory by integrating a novel pheromone-driven reward mechanism with the twin delayed deep deterministic policy gradient algorithm, which enables adaptive UAV motion strategy in complex environments. Simulation results validate that the derived optimal altitude effectively reduces the flight distance by up to 35% compared to baseline methods. Additionally, the proposed reward mechanism significantly shortens the convergence steps by approximately 50%, demonstrating notable efficiency gains in the context of UAV-assisted VLC data collection.

摘要（中文）: 近期，无人机(UAV)和可见光通信(VLC)技术的融合已成为一种有前景的解决方案，可提供灵活的通信和高效的照明。本文研究了无人机辅助VLC系统中的三维轨迹规划，其中派遣无人机从地面用户(GU)收集数据。核心目标是开发一种轨迹规划框架，以最小化无人机飞行距离，这等同于最大化数据采集效率。该问题被表述为一个具有挑战性的混合整数非凸优化问题。为了解决这个问题，我们首先推导出在特定VLC信道增益阈值下的闭式最优飞行高度。随后，我们通过将一种新型的信息素驱动奖励机制与双延迟深度确定性策略梯度算法相结合，来优化无人机的水平轨迹，从而在复杂环境中实现自适应的无人机运动策略。仿真结果表明，与基线方法相比，所推导出的最优高度有效地将飞行距离减少了高达35%。此外，所提出的奖励机制将收敛步骤显著缩短了约50%，展示了在无人机辅助VLC数据收集方面显著的效率提升。

TLDR: This paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework for UAV trajectory planning in VLC systems, aiming to minimize flight distance by optimizing altitude and horizontal trajectory with a pheromone-driven reward mechanism. Simulation results show improved flight distance and convergence speed compared to baselines.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于深度强化学习（DRL）的可见光通信（VLC）系统中无人机轨迹规划框架，旨在通过优化高度和水平轨迹，并结合信息素驱动的奖励机制来最小化飞行距离。仿真结果表明，与基线方法相比，飞行距离和收敛速度均有所提升。

Authors: Tian-Tian Lin, Yi Liu, Xiao-Wei Tang, Yunmei Shi, Yi Huang, Zhongxiang Wei, Qingqing Wu, Yuhan Dong

Gaussian Process Bandit Optimization with Machine Learning Predictions and Application to Hypothesis Generation

Abstract (English): Many real-world optimization problems involve an expensive ground-truth oracle (e.g., human evaluation, physical experiments) and a cheap, low-fidelity prediction oracle (e.g., machine learning models, simulations). Meanwhile, abundant offline data (e.g., past experiments and predictions) are often available and can be used to pretrain powerful predictive models, as well as to provide an informative prior. We propose Prediction-Augmented Gaussian Process Upper Confidence Bound (PA-GP-UCB), a novel Bayesian optimization algorithm that leverages both oracles and offline data to achieve provable gains in sample efficiency for the ground-truth oracle queries. PA-GP-UCB employs a control-variates estimator derived from a joint Gaussian process posterior to correct prediction bias and reduce uncertainty. We prove that PA-GP-UCB preserves the standard regret rate of GP-UCB while achieving a strictly smaller leading constant that is explicitly controlled by prediction quality and offline data coverage. Empirically, PA-GP-UCB converges faster than Vanilla GP-UCB and naive prediction-augmented GP-UCB baselines on synthetic benchmarks and on a real-world hypothesis evaluation task grounded in human behavioral data, where predictions are provided by large language models. These results establish PA-GP-UCB as a general and sample-efficient framework for hypothesis generation under expensive feedback.

摘要（中文）: 许多现实世界的优化问题都涉及昂贵的真值预言机（例如，人工评估、物理实验）和一个廉价的、低保真度的预测预言机（例如，机器学习模型、模拟）。同时，大量的离线数据（例如，过去的实验和预测）通常是可用的，并且可以用来预训练强大的预测模型，以及提供信息丰富的先验知识。我们提出了预测增强的高斯过程上置信界（PA-GP-UCB），一种新颖的贝叶斯优化算法，它利用这两种预言机和离线数据来在真值预言机查询的采样效率上实现可证明的提升。PA-GP-UCB采用从联合高斯过程后验导出的控制变量估计器来校正预测偏差并降低不确定性。我们证明了PA-GP-UCB保留了GP-UCB的标准遗憾率，同时实现了严格较小的首项常数，该常数由预测质量和离线数据覆盖率显式控制。在经验上，PA-GP-UCB在合成基准测试和基于人类行为数据的真实假设评估任务上，比Vanilla GP-UCB和朴素的预测增强GP-UCB基线收敛更快，其中预测由大型语言模型提供。这些结果将PA-GP-UCB确立为在高成本反馈下进行假设生成的一种通用且采样高效的框架。

TLDR: The paper introduces Prediction-Augmented Gaussian Process Upper Confidence Bound (PA-GP-UCB), a Bayesian optimization algorithm that utilizes both expensive ground-truth oracles and cheap prediction oracles along with offline data to improve sample efficiency, particularly for hypothesis generation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种预测增强高斯过程上置信界 (PA-GP-UCB) 算法，该算法利用昂贵的真实数据源和廉价的预测数据源以及离线数据来提高样本效率，尤其适用于假设生成任务。

Authors: Xin Jennifer Chen, Yunjin Tong

SMOG: Scalable Meta-Learning for Multi-Objective Bayesian Optimization

Abstract (English): Multi-objective optimization aims to solve problems with competing objectives, often with only black-box access to a problem and a limited budget of measurements. In many applications, historical data from related optimization tasks is available, creating an opportunity for meta-learning to accelerate the optimization. Bayesian optimization, as a promising technique for black-box optimization, has been extended to meta-learning and multi-objective optimization independently, but methods that simultaneously address both settings - meta-learned priors for multi-objective Bayesian optimization - remain largely unexplored. We propose SMOG, a scalable and modular meta-learning model based on a multi-output Gaussian process that explicitly learns correlations between objectives. SMOG builds a structured joint Gaussian process prior across meta- and target tasks and, after conditioning on metadata, yields a closed-form target-task prior augmented by a flexible residual multi-output kernel. This construction propagates metadata uncertainty into the target surrogate in a principled way. SMOG supports hierarchical, parallel training: meta-task Gaussian processes are fit once and then cached, achieving linear scaling with the number of meta-tasks. The resulting surrogate integrates seamlessly with standard multi-objective Bayesian optimization acquisition functions.

摘要（中文）: 多目标优化旨在解决具有相互竞争目标的问题，通常只能通过黑盒方式访问问题，且测量预算有限。在许多应用中，可以获得来自相关优化任务的历史数据，从而为元学习创造机会以加速优化。贝叶斯优化作为一种有前景的黑盒优化技术，已被独立地扩展到元学习和多目标优化，但同时解决这两种情况的方法——多目标贝叶斯优化的元学习先验——仍然在很大程度上未被探索。我们提出了SMOG，一种可扩展且模块化的元学习模型，该模型基于多输出高斯过程，显式地学习目标之间的相关性。SMOG构建了一个跨元任务和目标任务的结构化联合高斯过程先验，并在根据元数据进行条件化后，产生一个封闭形式的目标任务先验，并由一个灵活的残差多输出核增强。这种构造以一种原则性的方式将元数据的不确定性传播到目标代理模型中。SMOG支持分层、并行训练：元任务高斯过程只需拟合一次然后缓存，从而实现与元任务数量的线性缩放。由此产生的代理模型可以无缝集成到标准的多目标贝叶斯优化采集函数中。

TLDR: The paper introduces SMOG, a scalable meta-learning model for multi-objective Bayesian Optimization that leverages a multi-output Gaussian process to learn correlations between objectives, enabling faster optimization in black-box scenarios.

简要说明: 本文介绍了SMOG，一种可扩展的元学习模型，用于多目标贝叶斯优化。该模型利用多输出高斯过程学习目标之间的相关性，从而在黑盒场景中实现更快的优化。

Authors: Leonard Papenmeier, Petru Tighineanu

About an Automating Annotation Method for Robot Markers

Abstract (English): Factory automation has become increasingly important due to labor shortages, leading to the introduction of autonomous mobile robots for tasks such as material transportation. Markers are commonly used for robot self-localization and object identification. In the RoboCup Logistics League (RCLL), ArUco markers are employed both for robot localization and for identifying processing modules. Conventional recognition relies on OpenCV-based image processing, which detects black-and-white marker patterns. However, these methods often fail under noise, motion blur, defocus, or varying illumination conditions. Deep-learning-based recognition offers improved robustness under such conditions, but requires large amounts of annotated data. Annotation must typically be done manually, as the type and position of objects cannot be detected automatically, making dataset preparation a major bottleneck. In contrast, ArUco markers include built-in recognition modules that provide both ID and positional information, enabling automatic annotation. This paper proposes an automated annotation method for training deep-learning models on ArUco marker images. By leveraging marker detection results obtained from the ArUco module, the proposed approach eliminates the need for manual labeling. A YOLO-based model is trained using the automatically annotated dataset, and its performance is evaluated under various conditions. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method improves recognition performance compared with conventional image-processing techniques, particularly for images affected by blur or defocus. Automatic annotation also reduces human effort and ensures consistent labeling quality. Future work will investigate the relationship between confidence thresholds and recognition performance.

摘要（中文）: 工厂自动化由于劳动力短缺而变得日益重要，从而促进了自主移动机器人在物料运输等任务中的应用。标记常被用于机器人自定位和物体识别。在RoboCup物流联赛（RCLL）中，ArUco标记被同时用于机器人定位和识别处理模块。传统的识别依赖于基于OpenCV的图像处理，该处理检测黑白标记图案。然而，这些方法在噪声、运动模糊、散焦或变化的照明条件下通常会失效。基于深度学习的识别在这些条件下提供了更高的鲁棒性，但需要大量的标注数据。由于物体的类型和位置无法自动检测，通常必须手动完成标注，这使得数据集准备成为主要的瓶颈。相比之下，ArUco标记包含内置的识别模块，可以提供ID和位置信息，从而实现自动标注。本文提出了一种自动标注方法，用于在ArUco标记图像上训练深度学习模型。通过利用从ArUco模块获得的标记检测结果，所提出的方法消除了手动标注的需求。使用自动标注的数据集训练了一个基于YOLO的模型，并在各种条件下评估了其性能。实验结果表明，与传统的图像处理技术相比，该方法提高了识别性能，尤其是在受模糊或散焦影响的图像中。自动标注还减少了人力投入，并确保了一致的标注质量。未来的工作将研究置信度阈值与识别性能之间的关系。

TLDR: This paper proposes an automated annotation method for training deep-learning models to recognize ArUco markers, leveraging the markers' built-in recognition to avoid manual labeling and improving robustness compared to traditional OpenCV methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种自动标注方法，用于训练深度学习模型以识别 ArUco 标记。该方法利用标记内置的识别功能来避免手动标注，并提高了相对于传统 OpenCV 方法的鲁棒性。

Authors: Wataru Uemura, Takeru Nagashima

Assistive Robots and Reasonable Work Assignment Reduce Perceived Stigma toward Persons with Disabilities

Abstract (English): Robots are becoming more prominent in assisting persons with disabilities (PwD). Whilst there is broad consensus that robots can assist in mitigating physical impairments, the extent to which they can facilitate social inclusion remains equivocal. In fact, the exposed status of assisted workers could likewise lead to reduced or increased perceived stigma by other workers. We present a vignette study on the perceived cognitive and behavioral stigma toward PwD in the workplace. We designed four experimental conditions depicting a coworker with an impairment in work scenarios: overburdened work, suitable work, and robot-assisted work only for the coworker, and an offer of robot-assisted work for everyone. Our results show that cognitive stigma is significantly reduced when the work task is adapted to the person's abilities or augmented by an assistive robot. In addition, offering robot-assisted work for everyone, in the sense of universal design, further reduces perceived cognitive stigma. Thus, we conclude that assistive robots reduce perceived cognitive stigma, thereby supporting the use of collaborative robots in work scenarios involving PwDs.

摘要（中文）: 机器人正日益显著地协助残疾人士（PwD）。虽然在机器人能够缓解身体障碍方面存在广泛共识，但它们在多大程度上能够促进社会融合仍不确定。实际上，受助工人的暴露状态同样可能导致其他工人对其感知到的污名增加或减少。我们提出了一项关于工作场所中对残疾人士的认知和行为污名感知的实验情景研究。我们设计了四种实验条件，描绘了一名有工作障碍的同事在工作场景中的情况：工作负担过重、适合的工作、仅为该同事提供的机器人辅助工作，以及为所有人提供机器人辅助工作的提议。我们的结果表明，当工作任务适应个人的能力或通过辅助机器人增强时，认知污名会显著降低。此外，从通用设计的角度来看，为所有人提供机器人辅助工作会进一步降低感知的认知污名。因此，我们得出结论，辅助机器人可以减少感知的认知污名，从而支持在涉及残疾人士的工作场景中使用协作机器人。

TLDR: This paper investigates how assistive robots and appropriate work assignments impact perceived stigma towards persons with disabilities (PwD), finding that both robot assistance and suitable tasks reduce cognitive stigma, especially when robot assistance is offered universally.

简要说明: 本文研究了辅助机器人和合理的工作分配如何影响对残疾人（PwD）的刻板印象，发现机器人辅助和合适的任务都能减少认知上的歧视，尤其是在普遍提供机器人辅助的情况下。

Authors: Stina Klein, Birgit Prodinger, Elisabeth André, Lars Mikelsons, Nils Mandischer

Postural Virtual Fixtures for Ergonomic Physical Interactions with Supernumerary Robotic Bodies

Abstract (English): Conjoined collaborative robots, functioning as supernumerary robotic bodies (SRBs), can enhance human load tolerance abilities. However, in tasks involving physical interaction with humans, users may still adopt awkward, non-ergonomic postures, which can lead to discomfort or injury over time. In this paper, we propose a novel control framework that provides kinesthetic feedback to SRB users when a non-ergonomic posture is detected, offering resistance to discourage such behaviors. This approach aims to foster long-term learning of ergonomic habits and promote proper posture during physical interactions. To achieve this, a virtual fixture method is developed, integrated with a continuous, online ergonomic posture assessment framework. Additionally, to improve coordination between the operator and the SRB, which consists of a robotic arm mounted on a floating base, the position of the floating base is adjusted as needed. Experimental results demonstrate the functionality and efficacy of the ergonomics-driven control framework, including two user studies involving practical loco-manipulation tasks with 14 subjects, comparing the proposed framework with a baseline control framework that does not account for human ergonomics.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 作为超常机器人肢体（SRBs）运行的联合协作机器人可以增强人体负重能力。然而，在涉及与人体物理交互的任务中，用户可能仍然会采用笨拙、不符合人体工学的姿势，长期下来可能导致不适或受伤。在本文中，我们提出了一种新型控制框架，当检测到非人体工学姿势时，该框架向SRB用户提供动觉反馈，提供阻力以抑制此类行为。该方法旨在培养长期的人体工学习惯，并在物理交互过程中促进正确的姿势。为了实现这一目标，开发了一种虚拟夹具方法，并将其与连续的在线人体工学姿势评估框架相结合。此外，为了改善操作员和由安装在浮动底座上的机械臂组成的SRB之间的协调，根据需要调整浮动底座的位置。实验结果证明了以人体工程学驱动的控制框架的功能和有效性，包括两项涉及实际定位操作任务的用户研究，共有14名受试者参与，并将所提出的框架与不考虑人体工程学的基线控制框架进行了比较。

TLDR: This paper presents a control framework using virtual fixtures to provide kinesthetic feedback to users of supernumerary robotic bodies (SRBs) to encourage ergonomic postures and improve human-robot coordination, validated with user studies.

Authors: Theodora Kastritsi, Marta Lagomarsino, Arash Ajoudani

Accurate Pedestrian Tracking in Urban Canyons: A Multi-Modal Fusion Approach

Abstract (English): The contribution describes a pedestrian navigation approach designed to improve localization accuracy in urban environments where GNSS performance is degraded, a problem that is especially critical for blind or low-vision users who depend on precise guidance such as identifying the correct side of a street. To address GNSS limitations and the impracticality of camera-based visual positioning, the work proposes a particle filter based fusion of GNSS and inertial data that incorporates spatial priors from maps, such as impassable buildings and unlikely walking areas, functioning as a probabilistic form of map matching. Inertial localization is provided by the RoNIN machine learning method, and fusion with GNSS is achieved by weighting particles based on their consistency with GNSS estimates and uncertainty. The system was evaluated on six challenging walking routes in downtown San Francisco using three metrics related to sidewalk correctness and localization error. Results show that the fused approach (GNSS+RoNIN+PF) significantly outperforms GNSS only localization on most metrics, while inertial-only localization with particle filtering also surpasses GNSS alone for critical measures such as sidewalk assignment and across street error.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种行人导航方法，旨在提高城市环境中定位精度，特别是在GNSS性能下降的情况下。这个问题对于依赖精确引导的盲人或低视力用户尤为关键，例如识别街道的正确侧面。为了解决GNSS局限性和基于相机的视觉定位的不实用性，本文提出了一种基于粒子滤波的GNSS和惯性数据融合方法，该方法结合了来自地图的空间先验信息，例如无法通行的建筑物和不太可能的步行区域，可以作为一种概率形式的地图匹配。惯性定位由RoNIN机器学习方法提供，并且通过根据粒子与GNSS估计值和不确定性的一致性来加权粒子，实现与GNSS的融合。该系统在旧金山市中心的六条具有挑战性的步行路线上进行了评估，使用了与人行道正确性和定位误差相关的三个指标。结果表明，融合方法（GNSS+RoNIN+PF）在大多数指标上显着优于仅GNSS定位，而仅惯性定位与粒子滤波相比，在关键指标（例如人行道分配和跨街道误差）方面也优于单独的GNSS。

TLDR: This paper presents a pedestrian navigation system fusing GNSS, inertial data (using RoNIN), and map priors within a particle filter to improve localization accuracy, particularly for visually impaired users in urban canyons. Results indicate significant improvement over GNSS-only and inertial-only approaches.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种行人导航系统，该系统融合了GNSS、惯性数据（使用RoNIN）和地图先验，并在粒子滤波器中进行处理，以提高定位精度，尤其是在城市峡谷中为视力受损的用户提供服务。结果表明，该系统相对于仅使用GNSS和仅使用惯性的方法有了显著改进。

Authors: Shahar Dubiner, Peng Ren, Roberto Manduchi

Lantern: A Minimalist Robotic Object Platform

Abstract (English): Robotic objects are simple actuated systems that subtly blend into human environments. We design and introduce Lantern, a minimalist robotic object platform to enable building simple robotic artifacts. We conducted in-depth design and engineering iterations of Lantern's mechatronic architecture to meet specific design goals while maintaining a low build cost (~40 USD). As an extendable, open-source platform, Lantern aims to enable exploration of a range of HRI scenarios by leveraging human tendency to assign social meaning to simple forms. To evaluate Lantern's potential for HRI, we conducted a series of explorations: 1) a co-design workshop, 2) a sensory room case study, 3) distribution to external HRI labs, 4) integration into a graduate-level HRI course, and 5) public exhibitions with older adults and children. Our findings show that Lantern effectively evokes engagement, can support versatile applications ranging from emotion regulation to focused work, and serves as a viable platform for lowering barriers to HRI as a field.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 机器人物体是能够巧妙融入人类环境的简单驱动系统。我们设计并推出了Lantern，这是一个极简的机器人物体平台，旨在实现构建简单机器人制品的可能性。我们对Lantern的机电一体化架构进行了深入的设计和工程迭代，以满足特定的设计目标，同时保持较低的构建成本（约40美元）。作为一个可扩展的开源平台，Lantern旨在通过利用人类将社会意义赋予简单形式的倾向，从而实现对一系列人机交互（HRI）场景的探索。为了评估Lantern在人机交互方面的潜力，我们进行了一系列探索：1）协同设计工作坊，2）感官室案例研究，3）向外部人机交互实验室分发，4）集成到研究生级别的人机交互课程中，以及5）面向老年人和儿童的公开展览。我们的研究结果表明，Lantern能够有效地激发参与感，可以支持从情绪调节到专注工作等多种应用，并且作为一个可行的平台，能够降低人机交互作为一个领域的准入门槛。

Authors: Victor Nikhil Antony, Zhili Gong, Guanchen Li, Clara Jeon, Chien-Ming Huang

ReactEMG Stroke: Healthy-to-Stroke Few-shot Adaptation for sEMG-Based Intent Detection

Abstract (English): Surface electromyography (sEMG) is a promising control signal for assist-as-needed hand rehabilitation after stroke, but detecting intent from paretic muscles often requires lengthy, subject-specific calibration and remains brittle to variability. We propose a healthy-to-stroke adaptation pipeline that initializes an intent detector from a model pretrained on large-scale able-bodied sEMG, then fine-tunes it for each stroke participant using only a small amount of subject-specific data. Using a newly collected dataset from three individuals with chronic stroke, we compare adaptation strategies (head-only tuning, parameter-efficient LoRA adapters, and full end-to-end fine-tuning) and evaluate on held-out test sets that include realistic distribution shifts such as within-session drift, posture changes, and armband repositioning. Across conditions, healthy-pretrained adaptation consistently improves stroke intent detection relative to both zero-shot transfer and stroke-only training under the same data budget; the best adaptation methods improve average transition accuracy from 0.42 to 0.61 and raw accuracy from 0.69 to 0.78. These results suggest that transferring a reusable healthy-domain EMG representation can reduce calibration burden while improving robustness for real-time post-stroke intent detection.

摘要（中文）: 表面肌电图（sEMG）是一种颇具前景的辅助需求型卒中后手部康复控制信号，但从瘫痪肌肉中检测意图通常需要耗时的、针对特定个体的校准，并且对变异性仍然很敏感。我们提出了一种健康的到卒中的自适应流程，该流程首先利用在大规模健全人sEMG数据上预训练的模型初始化意图检测器，然后仅使用少量特定于卒中参与者的数据对其进行微调。利用从三名慢性卒中患者处收集的新数据集，我们比较了自适应策略（仅头部调整、参数高效的LoRA适配器和完整的端到端微调），并在包含真实分布偏移（如会话内漂移、姿势变化和臂带重新定位）的保留测试集上进行评估。在各种条件下，与在相同数据预算下的零样本迁移和仅卒中训练相比，健康预训练自适应始终能提高卒中意图检测的效果；最佳的自适应方法将平均转换准确率从0.42提高到0.61，将原始准确率从0.69提高到0.78。这些结果表明，转移可重用的健康领域EMG表示可以减轻校准负担，同时提高卒中后实时意图检测的鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper presents a healthy-to-stroke adaptation pipeline for sEMG-based intent detection, using pretraining on healthy subjects and fine-tuning on stroke patient data, achieving improved accuracy and robustness with limited subject-specific calibration data.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于表面肌电信号的健康-中风适应性意图检测流程，通过在健康受试者数据上进行预训练，并在中风患者数据上进行微调，从而在减少患者特定校准数据需求的同时，提高了准确性和鲁棒性。

Authors: Runsheng Wang, Katelyn Lee, Xinyue Zhu, Lauren Winterbottom, Dawn M. Nilsen, Joel Stein, Matei Ciocarlie

Leveraging Convolutional Sparse Autoencoders for Robust Movement Classification from Low-Density sEMG

Abstract (English): Reliable control of myoelectric prostheses is often hindered by high inter-subject variability and the clinical impracticality of high-density sensor arrays. This study proposes a deep learning framework for accurate gesture recognition using only two surface electromyography (sEMG) channels. The method employs a Convolutional Sparse Autoencoder (CSAE) to extract temporal feature representations directly from raw signals, eliminating the need for heuristic feature engineering. On a 6-class gesture set, our model achieved a multi-subject F1-score of 94.3% $\pm$ 0.3%. To address subject-specific differences, we present a few-shot transfer learning protocol that improved performance on unseen subjects from a baseline of 35.1% $\pm$ 3.1% to 92.3% $\pm$ 0.9% with minimal calibration data. Furthermore, the system supports functional extensibility through an incremental learning strategy, allowing for expansion to a 10-class set with a 90.0% $\pm$ 0.2% F1-score without full model retraining. By combining high precision with minimal computational and sensor overhead, this framework provides a scalable and efficient approach for the next generation of affordable and adaptive prosthetic systems.

摘要（中文）: 肌电假肢的可靠控制常常受到个体间高度差异和高密度传感器阵列临床应用局限性的阻碍。本研究提出了一种深度学习框架，仅使用两个表面肌电（sEMG）通道即可实现精确的手势识别。该方法采用卷积稀疏自编码器（CSAE）直接从原始信号中提取时间特征表示，无需启发式特征工程。在一个包含 6 类手势的数据集上，我们的模型实现了 94.3% $\pm$ 0.3% 的多被试 F1 值。为了解决被试特定差异，我们提出了一种小样本迁移学习协议，该协议通过最少的校准数据，将未见被试的性能从 35.1% $\pm$ 3.1% 的基线提高到 92.3% $\pm$ 0.9%。此外，该系统通过增量学习策略支持功能扩展，无需完全重新训练模型即可扩展到包含 10 类的数据集，并达到 90.0% $\pm$ 0.2% 的 F1 值。通过将高精度与最小的计算和传感器开销相结合，该框架为下一代经济实惠且自适应的假肢系统提供了一种可扩展且高效的方法。

TLDR: The paper introduces a deep learning framework using Convolutional Sparse Autoencoders (CSAE) for robust gesture recognition from low-density sEMG signals, achieving high accuracy and adaptability for prosthetic control.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种深度学习框架，使用卷积稀疏自编码器（CSAE）从低密度sEMG信号中进行鲁棒的手势识别，为假肢控制实现了高精度和适应性。

Authors: Blagoj Hristov, Zoran Hadzi-Velkov, Katerina Hadzi-Velkova Saneva, Gorjan Nadzinski, Vesna Ojleska Latkoska

Reinforcement Learning-Based Co-Design and Operation of Chiller and Thermal Energy Storage for Cost-Optimal HVAC Systems

Abstract (English): We study the joint operation and sizing of cooling infrastructure for commercial HVAC systems using reinforcement learning, with the objective of minimizing life-cycle cost over a 30-year horizon. The cooling system consists of a fixed-capacity electric chiller and a thermal energy storage (TES) unit, jointly operated to meet stochastic hourly cooling demands under time-varying electricity prices. The life-cycle cost accounts for both capital expenditure and discounted operating cost, including electricity consumption and maintenance. A key challenge arises from the strong asymmetry in capital costs: increasing chiller capacity by one unit is far more expensive than an equivalent increase in TES capacity. As a result, identifying the right combination of chiller and TES sizes, while ensuring zero loss-of-cooling-load under optimal operation, is a non-trivial co-design problem. To address this, we formulate the chiller operation problem for a fixed infrastructure configuration as a finite-horizon Markov Decision Process (MDP), in which the control action is the chiller part-load ratio (PLR). The MDP is solved using a Deep Q Network (DQN) with a constrained action space. The learned DQN RL policy minimizes electricity cost over historical traces of cooling demand and electricity prices. For each candidate chiller-TES sizing configuration, the trained policy is evaluated. We then restrict attention to configurations that fully satisfy the cooling demand and perform a life-cycle cost minimization over this feasible set to identify the cost-optimal infrastructure design. Using this approach, we determine the optimal chiller and thermal energy storage capacities to be 700 and 1500, respectively.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了商业暖通空调系统冷却基础设施的联合运行和容量确定，采用强化学习方法，目标是在30年时间内最小化全寿命周期成本。冷却系统由一台固定容量的电动冷水机组和一个蓄冷（TES）单元组成，二者联合运行以满足随时间变化的电价下的随机小时冷却需求。全寿命周期成本包括资本支出和折现运营成本，包括电力消耗和维护。一个关键挑战来自于资本成本的强烈不对称性：将冷水机组容量增加一个单位比等效地增加TES容量昂贵得多。因此，在确保最优运行下零冷却负荷损失的前提下，识别冷水机组和TES容量的正确组合是一个重要的协同设计问题。为了解决这个问题，我们将固定基础设施配置下的冷水机组运行问题建模为一个有限时域马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），其中控制动作是冷水机组的部分负荷率（PLR）。该MDP使用具有约束动作空间的深度Q网络（DQN）求解。学习到的DQN RL策略在冷却需求和电价的历史轨迹上最小化电力成本。对于每个候选的冷水机组-TES容量配置，评估经过训练的策略。然后，我们只关注完全满足冷却需求的配置，并在这个可行集上执行全寿命周期成本最小化，以识别成本最优的基础设施设计。使用这种方法，我们确定最佳的冷水机组和蓄冷容量分别为700和1500。

TLDR: This paper uses reinforcement learning (DQN) to optimize the co-design and operation of chiller and thermal energy storage systems for commercial HVAC, minimizing life-cycle costs.

简要说明: 本文利用强化学习 (DQN) 优化商用 HVAC 系统的冷却器和热能存储系统的协同设计和运行，以最大限度地降低生命周期成本。

Authors: Tanay Raghunandan Srinivasa, Vivek Deulkar, Aviruch Bhatia, Vishal Garg

Keep Rehearsing and Refining: Lifelong Learning Vehicle Routing under Continually Drifting Tasks

Abstract (English): Existing neural solvers for vehicle routing problems (VRPs) are typically trained either in a one-off manner on a fixed set of pre-defined tasks or in a lifelong manner on several tasks arriving sequentially, assuming sufficient training on each task. Both settings overlook a common real-world property: problem patterns may drift continually over time, yielding massive tasks sequentially arising while offering only limited training resources per task. In this paper, we study a novel lifelong learning paradigm for neural VRP solvers under continually drifting tasks over learning time steps, where sufficient training for any given task at any time is not available. We propose Dual Replay with Experience Enhancement (DREE), a general framework to improve learning efficiency and mitigate catastrophic forgetting under such drift. Extensive experiments show that, under such continual drift, DREE effectively learns new tasks, preserves prior knowledge, improves generalization to unseen tasks, and can be applied to diverse existing neural solvers.

摘要（中文）: 针对车辆路径问题（VRP）的现有神经求解器通常采取一次性方式在预定义的固定任务集上进行训练，或者以终身学习的方式在多个按顺序到达的任务上进行训练，并假设每个任务都经过了充分的训练。这两种设置都忽略了一个常见的现实世界属性：问题模式可能随着时间推移而持续漂移，导致大量的任务按顺序出现，而每个任务仅提供有限的训练资源。在本文中，我们研究了一种新型的神经VRP求解器终身学习范式，该范式在学习时间步长内处理持续漂移的任务，其中任何给定任务在任何时间都无法获得充分的训练。我们提出了一种基于经验增强的双重回放（DREE）方法，这是一个通用的框架，用于提高学习效率并缓解在此类漂移下的灾难性遗忘。大量的实验表明，在这种持续漂移的情况下，DREE能够有效地学习新任务，保留先验知识，提高对未见任务的泛化能力，并且可以应用于各种现有的神经求解器。

TLDR: This paper introduces a lifelong learning framework (DREE) for neural Vehicle Routing Problem (VRP) solvers that addresses the challenge of continually drifting tasks with limited training resources, showing improvements in learning efficiency and mitigating catastrophic forgetting.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种用于神经车辆路径问题（VRP）求解器的终身学习框架（DREE），该框架解决了训练资源有限的情况下不断漂移的任务带来的挑战，并在学习效率和减轻灾难性遗忘方面表现出改进。

Authors: Jiyuan Pei, Yi Mei, Jialin Liu, Mengjie Zhang, Xin Yao

RulePlanner: All-in-One Reinforcement Learner for Unifying Design Rules in 3D Floorplanning

Abstract (English): Floorplanning determines the coordinate and shape of each module in Integrated Circuits. With the scaling of technology nodes, in floorplanning stage especially 3D scenarios with multiple stacked layers, it has become increasingly challenging to adhere to complex hardware design rules. Current methods are only capable of handling specific and limited design rules, while violations of other rules require manual and meticulous adjustment. This leads to labor-intensive and time-consuming post-processing for expert engineers. In this paper, we propose an all-in-one deep reinforcement learning-based approach to tackle these challenges, and design novel representations for real-world IC design rules that have not been addressed by previous approaches. Specifically, the processing of various hardware design rules is unified into a single framework with three key components: 1) novel matrix representations to model the design rules, 2) constraints on the action space to filter out invalid actions that cause rule violations, and 3) quantitative analysis of constraint satisfaction as reward signals. Experiments on public benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness and validity of our approach. Furthermore, transferability is well demonstrated on unseen circuits. Our framework is extensible to accommodate new design rules, thus providing flexibility to address emerging challenges in future chip design. Code will be available at: https://github.com/Thinklab-SJTU/EDA-AI

摘要（中文）: 布局规划决定了每个模块在集成电路中的坐标和形状。随着技术节点的缩小，在布局规划阶段，尤其是在具有多个堆叠层的3D场景中，遵循复杂的硬件设计规则变得越来越具有挑战性。当前的方法只能处理特定且有限的设计规则，而其他规则的违反则需要人工和细致的调整。这导致专家工程师需要进行劳动密集型且耗时的后处理。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于深度强化学习的通用方法来解决这些挑战，并为先前方法未解决的真实集成电路设计规则设计了新颖的表示方法。具体来说，各种硬件设计规则的处理被统一到一个包含三个关键组件的框架中：1）用于建模设计规则的新型矩阵表示；2）对动作空间的约束，以过滤掉导致规则违反的无效动作；3）约束满足的定量分析作为奖励信号。在公共基准上的实验证明了我们方法的有效性和正确性。此外，在未见过的电路上的可迁移性也得到了很好的验证。我们的框架具有可扩展性，可以适应新的设计规则，从而为应对未来芯片设计中出现的新挑战提供了灵活性。代码将在以下网址提供：https://github.com/Thinklab-SJTU/EDA-AI

TLDR: The paper introduces RulePlanner, a deep reinforcement learning approach that unifies the handling of various hardware design rules in 3D IC floorplanning, using novel matrix representations and constraint-aware actions.

Authors: Ruizhe Zhong, Xingbo Du, Junchi Yan

Learning Provably Correct Distributed Protocols Without Human Knowledge

Abstract (English): Provably correct distributed protocols, which are a critical component of modern distributed systems, are highly challenging to design and have often required decades of human effort. These protocols allow multiple agents to coordinate to come to a common agreement in an environment with uncertainty and failures. We formulate protocol design as a search problem over strategies in a game with imperfect information, and the desired correctness conditions are specified in Satisfiability Modulo Theories (SMT). However, standard methods for solving multi-agent games fail to learn correct protocols in this setting, even when the number of agents is small. We propose a learning framework, GGMS, which integrates a specialized variant of Monte Carlo Tree Search with a transformer-based action encoder, a global depth-first search to break out of local minima, and repeated feedback from a model checker. Protocols output by GGMS are verified correct via exhaustive model checking for all executions within the bounded setting. We further prove that, under mild assumptions, the search process is complete: if a correct protocol exists, GGMS will eventually find it. In experiments, we show that GGMS can learn correct protocols for larger settings than existing methods.

摘要（中文）: 经过验证的正确分布式协议是现代分布式系统的关键组成部分，但其设计极具挑战性，往往需要数十年的努力。这些协议允许多个代理在存在不确定性和故障的环境中协调，以达成共识。我们将协议设计形式化为具有不完全信息博弈中的策略搜索问题，并通过基于可满足性模理论 (SMT) 的方式指定所需的正确性条件。然而，即便代理数量很小，用于解决多代理博弈的标准方法也无法在这种情况下学习到正确的协议。我们提出了一个学习框架 GGMS，它集成了蒙特卡洛树搜索的专用变体、基于 Transformer 的动作编码器、用于摆脱局部最小值的全局深度优先搜索，以及来自模型检查器的重复反馈。GGMS 输出的协议通过在有界设置下的所有执行路径进行穷举模型检查来验证其正确性。我们进一步证明，在温和假设下，搜索过程是完备的：如果存在正确的协议，GGMS 最终会找到它。在实验中，我们表明 GGMS 能够为比现有方法更大的规模学习正确的协议。

TLDR: The paper introduces GGMS, a learning framework that combines Monte Carlo Tree Search, transformer-based encoding, depth-first search, and model checking to automatically learn provably correct distributed protocols, exceeding the capabilities of existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为GGMS的学习框架，它结合了蒙特卡洛树搜索、基于Transformer的编码、深度优先搜索和模型检查，以自动学习可证明正确的分布式协议，超越了现有方法的能力。

Authors: Yujie Hui, Xiaoyi Lu, Andrew Perrault, Yang Wang

Learning to Recommend Multi-Agent Subgraphs from Calling Trees

Abstract (English): Multi-agent systems (MAS) increasingly solve complex tasks by orchestrating agents and tools selected from rapidly growing marketplaces. As these marketplaces expand, many candidates become functionally overlapping, making selection not just a retrieval problem: beyond filtering relevant agents, an orchestrator must choose options that are reliable, compatible with the current execution context, and able to cooperate with other selected agents. Existing recommender systems -- largely built for item-level ranking from flat user-item logs -- do not directly address the structured, sequential, and interaction-dependent nature of agent orchestration. We address this gap by \textbf{formulating agent recommendation in MAS as a constrained decision problem} and introducing a generic \textbf{constrained recommendation framework} that first uses retrieval to build a compact candidate set conditioned on the current subtask and context, and then performs \textbf{utility optimization} within this feasible set using a learned scorer that accounts for relevance, reliability, and interaction effects. We ground both the formulation and learning signals in \textbf{historical calling trees}, which capture the execution structure of MAS (parent-child calls, branching dependencies, and local cooperation patterns) beyond what flat logs provide. The framework supports two complementary settings: \textbf{agent-level recommendation} (select the next agent/tool) and \textbf{system-level recommendation} (select a small, connected agent team/subgraph for coordinated execution). To enable systematic evaluation, we construct a unified calling-tree benchmark by normalizing invocation logs from eight heterogeneous multi-agent corpora into a shared structured representation.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体系统（MAS）越来越多地通过编排从快速增长的市场中选择的智能体和工具来解决复杂任务。随着这些市场扩展，许多候选者在功能上变得重叠，使得选择不仅仅是一个检索问题：除了过滤相关智能体之外，编排器还必须选择可靠的、与当前执行上下文兼容的、并且能够与其他选定智能体合作的选项。现有的推荐系统——主要为基于扁平用户-物品日志的物品级别排序而构建——不能直接解决智能体编排的结构化、序列化和交互依赖性。我们通过\textbf{将MAS中的智能体推荐表述为一个约束决策问题}并引入一个通用的\textbf{约束推荐框架}来解决这一差距，该框架首先使用检索来构建一个基于当前子任务和上下文的紧凑候选集，然后在此可行集中使用一个学习到的评分器执行\textbf{效用优化}，该评分器考虑了相关性、可靠性和交互作用。我们将表述和学习信号都基于\textbf{历史调用树}，这些调用树捕获了MAS的执行结构（父子调用、分支依赖性和局部合作模式），超越了扁平日志所能提供的内容。该框架支持两个互补的设置：\textbf{智能体级别推荐}(选择下一个智能体/工具)和\textbf{系统级别推荐}(选择一个小的、连接的智能体团队/子图以进行协调执行)。为了实现系统评估，我们通过将来自八个异构多智能体语料库的调用日志标准化为共享的结构化表示，从而构建了一个统一的调用树基准。

TLDR: The paper introduces a constrained recommendation framework for selecting agents/tools in multi-agent systems, leveraging historical calling trees to optimize for relevance, reliability, and interaction effects at both agent and system levels.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个受约束的推荐框架，用于在多智能体系统中选择智能体/工具，利用历史调用树来优化相关性、可靠性和交互效应，从而支持智能体级别和系统级别的推荐。

Authors: Xinyuan Song, Liang Zhao

Development of Domain-Invariant Visual Enhancement and Restoration (DIVER) Approach for Underwater Images

Abstract (English): Underwater images suffer severe degradation due to wavelength-dependent attenuation, scattering, and illumination non-uniformity that vary across water types and depths. We propose an unsupervised Domain-Invariant Visual Enhancement and Restoration (DIVER) framework that integrates empirical correction with physics-guided modeling for robust underwater image enhancement. DIVER first applies either IlluminateNet for adaptive luminance enhancement or a Spectral Equalization Filter for spectral normalization. An Adaptive Optical Correction Module then refines hue and contrast using channel-adaptive filtering, while Hydro-OpticNet employs physics-constrained learning to compensate for backscatter and wavelength-dependent attenuation. The parameters of IlluminateNet and Hydro-OpticNet are optimized via unsupervised learning using a composite loss function. DIVER is evaluated on eight diverse datasets covering shallow, deep, and highly turbid environments, including both naturally low-light and artificially illuminated scenes, using reference and non-reference metrics. While state-of-the-art methods such as WaterNet, UDNet, and Phaseformer perform reasonably in shallow water, their performance degrades in deep, unevenly illuminated, or artificially lit conditions. In contrast, DIVER consistently achieves best or near-best performance across all datasets, demonstrating strong domain-invariant capability. DIVER yields at least a 9% improvement over SOTA methods in UCIQE. On the low-light SeaThru dataset, where color-palette references enable direct evaluation of color restoration, DIVER achieves at least a 4.9% reduction in GPMAE compared to existing methods. Beyond visual quality, DIVER also improves robotic perception by enhancing ORB-based keypoint repeatability and matching performance, confirming its robustness across diverse underwater environments.

摘要（中文）: 水下图像由于波长相关的衰减、散射以及随水域类型和深度而变化的光照不均匀性而遭受严重的降质影响。我们提出了一种无监督的域不变视觉增强与恢复（DIVER）框架，该框架集成了经验校正与物理引导建模，以实现鲁棒的水下图像增强。DIVER首先应用IlluminateNet进行自适应亮度增强或应用光谱均衡滤波器进行光谱归一化。然后，自适应光学校正模块使用通道自适应滤波来精细化色调和对比度，而Hydro-OpticNet采用物理约束学习来补偿后向散射和波长相关的衰减。IlluminateNet和Hydro-OpticNet的参数通过使用复合损失函数的无监督学习进行优化。DIVER在涵盖浅水、深水和高度浑浊环境的八个多样化数据集上进行了评估，这些数据集包括自然光照不足和人工照明场景，并使用了参考和非参考指标。虽然WaterNet、UDNet和Phaseformer等最先进的方法在浅水中表现良好，但它们在深度、光照不均或人工照明条件下的性能会下降。与之相反，DIVER在所有数据集上始终如一地实现最佳或接近最佳的性能，展示了强大的域不变能力。DIVER在UCIQE上至少比SOTA方法提高了9%。在低光照SeaThru数据集上，颜色调色板参考允许对颜色恢复进行直接评估，DIVER比现有方法在GPMAE上至少降低了4.9%。除了视觉质量外，DIVER还通过增强基于ORB的关键点可重复性和匹配性能来改善机器人感知，证实了其在各种水下环境中的鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces DIVER, an unsupervised domain-invariant underwater image enhancement and restoration framework leveraging empirical correction and physics-guided modeling, achieving state-of-the-art performance across diverse underwater datasets and improving robotic perception.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为DIVER的无监督域不变水下图像增强和恢复框架，该框架利用经验校正和物理引导建模，在各种水下数据集上实现了最先进的性能，并提高了机器人感知能力。

Authors: Rajini Makam, Sharanya Patil, Dhatri Shankari T M, Suresh Sundaram, Narasimhan Sundararajan

Under-Canopy Terrain Reconstruction in Dense Forests Using RGB Imaging and Neural 3D Reconstruction

Abstract (English): Mapping the terrain and understory hidden beneath dense forest canopies is of great interest for numerous applications such as search and rescue, trail mapping, forest inventory tasks, and more. Existing solutions rely on specialized sensors: either heavy, costly airborne LiDAR, or Airborne Optical Sectioning (AOS), which uses thermal synthetic aperture photography and is tailored for person detection. We introduce a novel approach for the reconstruction of canopy-free, photorealistic ground views using only conventional RGB images. Our solution is based on the celebrated Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF), a recent 3D reconstruction method. Additionally, we include specific image capture considerations, which dictate the needed illumination to successfully expose the scene beneath the canopy. To better cope with the poorly lit understory, we employ a low light loss. Finally, we propose two complementary approaches to remove occluding canopy elements by controlling per-ray integration procedure. To validate the value of our approach, we present two possible downstream tasks. For the task of search and rescue (SAR), we demonstrate that our method enables person detection which achieves promising results compared to thermal AOS (using only RGB images). Additionally, we show the potential of our approach for forest inventory tasks like tree counting. These results position our approach as a cost-effective, high-resolution alternative to specialized sensors for SAR, trail mapping, and forest-inventory tasks.

摘要（中文）: 绘制隐藏在茂密森林冠层下的地形和林下植被对于包括搜索和救援、路径绘制、森林资源清查等在内的众多应用具有重要意义。现有的解决方案依赖于专门的传感器：要么是沉重且昂贵的机载激光雷达，要么是机载光学切片(AOS)，后者使用热合成孔径摄影，专为人员检测而设计。 我们介绍了一种新颖的方法，仅使用传统的RGB图像即可重建无冠层的逼真地面视图。我们的解决方案基于著名的神经辐射场(NeRF)，这是一种新兴的3D重建方法。此外，我们加入了特定的图像采集考量，即确定成功曝光冠层下方场景所需的照明。为了更好地应对光线不足的林下空间，我们采用了低光损耗。最后，我们提出了两种互补的方法，通过控制每条光线的积分过程来移除遮挡的冠层元素。 为了验证我们方法的价值，我们展示了两个可能的下游任务。对于搜索和救援(SAR)任务，我们证明了我们的方法能够进行人员检测，与热成像AOS相比（仅使用RGB图像）取得了可喜的成果。此外，我们展示了我们的方法在森林资源清查任务（如树木计数）中的潜力。这些结果将我们的方法定位为一种经济高效、高分辨率的替代方案，取代用于SAR、路径绘制和森林资源清查任务的专用传感器。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel RGB-based approach using NeRFs to reconstruct terrain under dense forest canopies, validated through person detection for SAR and forest inventory tasks, offering a cost-effective alternative to LiDAR or AOS.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新颖的基于RGB图像和NeRF的森林冠层下地形重建方法，通过人员检测（用于搜救）和森林盘点任务验证了其有效性，为LiDAR或AOS提供了一种经济高效的替代方案。

Authors: Refael Sheffer, Chen Pinchover, Haim Zisman, Dror Ozeri, Roee Litman

Neural Clothing Tryer: Customized Virtual Try-On via Semantic Enhancement and Controlling Diffusion Model

Abstract (English): This work aims to address a novel Customized Virtual Try-ON (Cu-VTON) task, enabling the superimposition of a specified garment onto a model that can be customized in terms of appearance, posture, and additional attributes. Compared with traditional VTON task, it enables users to tailor digital avatars to their individual preferences, thereby enhancing the virtual fitting experience with greater flexibility and engagement. To address this task, we introduce a Neural Clothing Tryer (NCT) framework, which exploits the advanced diffusion models equipped with semantic enhancement and controlling modules to better preserve semantic characterization and textural details of the garment and meanwhile facilitating the flexible editing of the model's postures and appearances. Specifically, NCT introduces a semantic-enhanced module to take semantic descriptions of garments and utilizes a visual-language encoder to learn aligned features across modalities. The aligned features are served as condition input to the diffusion model to enhance the preservation of the garment's semantics. Then, a semantic controlling module is designed to take the garment image, tailored posture image, and semantic description as input to maintain garment details while simultaneously editing model postures, expressions, and various attributes. Extensive experiments on the open available benchmark demonstrate the superior performance of the proposed NCT framework.

摘要（中文）: 本研究旨在解决一种新型的定制化虚拟试穿（Cu-VTON）任务，该任务能够将指定的服装叠加到外观、姿势和附加属性均可定制的模型上。与传统的VTON任务相比，它允许用户根据个人偏好定制数字虚拟形象，从而通过更大的灵活性和参与度来增强虚拟试穿体验。为了解决这一任务，我们引入了一个神经服装试穿器（NCT）框架，该框架利用配备了语义增强和控制模块的先进扩散模型，从而更好地保留服装的语义特征和纹理细节，同时促进模型姿势和外观的灵活编辑。具体而言，NCT引入了一个语义增强模块来获取服装的语义描述，并利用视觉-语言编码器来学习跨模态的对齐特征。这些对齐特征作为扩散模型的条件输入，以增强服装语义的保留。然后，设计了一个语义控制模块，它将服装图像、定制的姿势图像和语义描述作为输入，在保持服装细节的同时，编辑模型的姿势、表情和各种属性。在公开基准数据集上进行的大量实验证明了所提出的NCT框架的优越性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces Neural Clothing Tryer (NCT), a framework utilizing diffusion models with semantic enhancement and controlling modules for customized virtual try-on, allowing users to tailor avatars and garments with greater flexibility.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为神经服装试穿器（NCT）的框架，该框架利用具有语义增强和控制模块的扩散模型来实现定制化的虚拟试穿，使用户能够更灵活地定制头像和服装。

Authors: Zhijing Yang, Weiwei Zhang, Mingliang Yang, Siyuan Peng, Yukai Shi, Junpeng Tan, Tianshui Chen, Liruo Zhong

Active Learning-Driven Lightweight YOLOv9: Enhancing Efficiency in Smart Agriculture

Abstract (English): This study addresses the demand for real-time detection of tomatoes and tomato flowers by agricultural robots deployed on edge devices in greenhouse environments. Under practical imaging conditions, object detection systems often face challenges such as large scale variations caused by varying camera distances, severe occlusion from plant structures, and highly imbalanced class distributions. These factors make conventional object detection approaches that rely on fully annotated datasets difficult to simultaneously achieve high detection accuracy and deployment efficiency. To overcome these limitations, this research proposes an active learning driven lightweight object detection framework, integrating data analysis, model design, and training strategy. First, the size distribution of objects in raw agricultural images is analyzed to redefine an operational target range, thereby improving learning stability under real-world conditions. Second, an efficient feature extraction module is incorporated to reduce computational cost, while a lightweight attention mechanism is introduced to enhance feature representation under multi-scale and occluded scenarios. Finally, an active learning strategy is employed to iteratively select high-information samples for annotation and training under a limited labeling budget, effectively improving the recognition performance of minority and small-object categories. Experimental results demonstrate that, while maintaining a low parameter count and inference cost suitable for edge-device deployment, the proposed method effectively improves the detection performance of tomatoes and tomato flowers in raw images. Under limited annotation conditions, the framework achieves an overall detection accuracy of 67.8% mAP, validating its practicality and feasibility for intelligent agricultural applications.

摘要（中文）: 本研究旨在解决温室环境下农业机器人对边缘设备上部署的番茄和番茄花卉进行实时检测的需求。在实际成像条件下，目标检测系统常面临诸如因相机距离变化引起的大尺度变化、植物结构导致的严重遮挡以及高度不平衡的类别分布等挑战。这些因素使得依赖完全标注数据集的传统目标检测方法难以同时实现高检测精度和部署效率。为克服这些局限，本研究提出一种主动学习驱动的轻量级目标检测框架，整合了数据分析、模型设计和训练策略。首先，分析原始农业图像中目标的大小分布，重新定义操作目标范围，从而提高真实世界条件下的学习稳定性。其次，引入高效的特征提取模块以降低计算成本，同时引入轻量级注意力机制以增强多尺度和遮挡场景下的特征表示。最后，采用主动学习策略，在有限的标注预算下迭代地选择高信息量的样本进行标注和训练，有效地提高了少数类别和小目标类别的识别性能。实验结果表明，该方法在保持适合边缘设备部署的低参数量和推理成本的同时，有效提高了原始图像中番茄和番茄花卉的检测性能。在有限标注条件下，该框架实现了67.8%的平均精度均值 (mAP) 的整体检测精度，验证了其在智能农业应用中的实用性和可行性。

TLDR: This paper presents an active learning-driven lightweight YOLOv9 framework for real-time detection of tomatoes and tomato flowers in challenging greenhouse environments, achieving 67.8% mAP under limited annotation.

Authors: Hung-Chih Tu, Bo-Syun Chen, Yun-Chien Cheng

GaussianOcc3D: A Gaussian-Based Adaptive Multi-modal 3D Occupancy Prediction

Abstract (English): 3D semantic occupancy prediction is a pivotal task in autonomous driving, providing a dense and fine-grained understanding of the surrounding environment, yet single-modality methods face trade-offs between camera semantics and LiDAR geometry. Existing multi-modal frameworks often struggle with modality heterogeneity, spatial misalignment, and the representation crisis--where voxels are computationally heavy and BEV alternatives are lossy. We present GaussianOcc3D, a multi-modal framework bridging camera and LiDAR through a memory-efficient, continuous 3D Gaussian representation. We introduce four modules: (1) LiDAR Depth Feature Aggregation (LDFA), using depth-wise deformable sampling to lift sparse signals onto Gaussian primitives; (2) Entropy-Based Feature Smoothing (EBFS) to mitigate domain noise; (3) Adaptive Camera-LiDAR Fusion (ACLF) with uncertainty-aware reweighting for sensor reliability; and (4) a Gauss-Mamba Head leveraging Selective State Space Models for global context with linear complexity. Evaluations on Occ3D, SurroundOcc, and SemanticKITTI benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving mIoU scores of 49.4%, 28.9%, and 25.2% respectively. GaussianOcc3D exhibits superior robustness across challenging rainy and nighttime conditions.

摘要（中文）: 三维语义占据预测是自动驾驶中一项关键任务，它提供了对周围环境的密集和精细理解，但单模态方法面临着相机语义和激光雷达几何结构之间的权衡。现有的多模态框架通常难以应对模态异质性、空间错位以及表示危机——体素计算量大，而BEV替代方案则是有损的。我们提出了GaussianOcc3D，一个通过内存高效的连续三维高斯表示来桥接相机和激光雷达的多模态框架。我们引入了四个模块：（1）激光雷达深度特征聚合（LDFA），使用深度方向可变形采样将稀疏信号提升到高斯基元上；（2）基于熵的特征平滑（EBFS），以减轻领域噪声；（3）自适应相机-激光雷达融合（ACLF），采用不确定性感知重加权来实现传感器可靠性；以及（4）一个高斯-Mamba头部，利用选择性状态空间模型以线性复杂度获取全局上下文。在Occ3D、SurroundOcc和SemanticKITTI基准测试上的评估表明，该方法具有最先进的性能，分别实现了49.4%、28.9%和25.2%的mIoU分数。GaussianOcc3D在具有挑战性的雨天和夜间条件下表现出卓越的鲁棒性。

TLDR: GaussianOcc3D is a novel multi-modal 3D occupancy prediction framework utilizing Gaussian primitives and a Mamba-based head to achieve SOTA performance on various benchmarks, improving robustness in challenging conditions.

简要说明: GaussianOcc3D是一个新颖的多模态3D occupancy预测框架，它利用高斯基元和基于Mamba的网络头，在各种基准测试上实现了SOTA性能，并提高了在具有挑战性条件下的鲁棒性。

UniGeo: A Unified 3D Indoor Object Detection Framework Integrating Geometry-Aware Learning and Dynamic Channel Gating

Abstract (English): The growing adoption of robotics and augmented reality in real-world applications has driven considerable research interest in 3D object detection based on point clouds. While previous methods address unified training across multiple datasets, they fail to model geometric relationships in sparse point cloud scenes and ignore the feature distribution in significant areas, which ultimately restricts their performance. To deal with this issue, a unified 3D indoor detection framework, called UniGeo, is proposed. To model geometric relations in scenes, we first propose a geometry-aware learning module that establishes a learnable mapping from spatial relationships to feature weights, which enabes explicit geometric feature enhancement. Then, to further enhance point cloud feature representation, we propose a dynamic channel gating mechanism that leverages learnable channel-wise weighting. This mechanism adaptively optimizes features generated by the sparse 3D U-Net network, significantly enhancing key geometric information. Extensive experiments on six different indoor scene datasets clearly validate the superior performance of our method.

摘要（中文）: 以下是一个可能的翻译： 机器人和增强现实在现实世界应用中日益普及，推动了对基于点云的3D目标检测的极大研究兴趣。尽管先前的方法致力于跨多个数据集的统一训练，但它们未能对稀疏点云场景中的几何关系进行建模，并且忽略了重要区域中的特征分布，这最终限制了它们的性能。为了解决这个问题，本文提出了一种统一的3D室内检测框架，称为UniGeo。为了建模场景中的几何关系，我们首先提出了一个几何感知学习模块，该模块建立了从空间关系到特征权重的可学习映射，从而实现了显式的几何特征增强。然后，为了进一步增强点云特征表示，我们提出了一种动态通道门控机制，该机制利用可学习的通道级权重。这种机制自适应地优化了稀疏3D U-Net网络生成的特征，显著增强了关键的几何信息。在六个不同的室内场景数据集上进行的大量实验清楚地验证了我们方法的优越性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces UniGeo, a unified 3D indoor object detection framework using geometry-aware learning and dynamic channel gating to improve performance on sparse point cloud data across multiple datasets.

Authors: Xing Yi, Jinyang Huang, Feng-Qi Cui, Anyang Tong, Ruimin Wang, Liu Liu, Dan Guo

TTSA3R: Training-Free Temporal-Spatial Adaptive Persistent State for Streaming 3D Reconstruction

Abstract (English): Streaming recurrent models enable efficient 3D reconstruction by maintaining persistent state representations. However, they suffer from catastrophic memory forgetting over long sequences due to balancing historical information with new observations. Recent methods alleviate this by deriving adaptive signals from attention perspective, but they operate on single dimensions without considering temporal and spatial consistency. To this end, we propose a training-free framework termed TTSA3R that leverages both temporal state evolution and spatial observation quality for adaptive state updates in 3D reconstruction. In particular, we devise a Temporal Adaptive Update Module that regulates update magnitude by analyzing temporal state evolution patterns. Then, a Spatial Contextual Update Module is introduced to localize spatial regions that require updates through observation-state alignment and scene dynamics. These complementary signals are finally fused to determine the state updating strategies. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of TTSA3R in diverse 3D tasks. Moreover, our method exhibits only 15% error increase compared to over 200% degradation in baseline models on extended sequences, significantly improving long-term reconstruction stability. Our codes will be available soon.

摘要（中文）: 流式循环模型通过维护持久的状态表示来实现高效的3D重建。然而，由于需要在历史信息和新观测之间进行平衡，它们在长序列中会遭受灾难性的记忆遗忘。最近的方法通过从注意力角度导出自适应信号来缓解这个问题，但它们在单个维度上操作，而没有考虑时间和空间一致性。为此，我们提出了一种名为TTSA3R的免训练框架，该框架利用时间状态演化和空间观测质量来进行3D重建中的自适应状态更新。具体而言，我们设计了一个时间自适应更新模块，通过分析时间状态演化模式来调节更新幅度。然后，引入一个空间上下文更新模块，通过观测-状态对齐和场景动态来定位需要更新的空间区域。这些互补的信号最终被融合起来，以决定状态更新策略。大量实验证明了TTSA3R在各种3D任务中的有效性。此外，我们的方法在扩展序列上仅表现出15%的误差增长，而基线模型的降级超过200%，显著提高了长期重建的稳定性。我们的代码即将开源。

TLDR: The paper proposes a training-free framework (TTSA3R) for streaming 3D reconstruction that adaptively updates the persistent state by considering both temporal state evolution and spatial observation quality, significantly improving long-term reconstruction stability. It outperforms baseline models on extended sequences.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于流式3D重建的免训练框架（TTSA3R），它通过考虑时间状态演化和空间观测质量自适应地更新持久状态，从而显著提高长期重建的稳定性。在扩展序列上，该方法优于基线模型。

Authors: Zhijie Zheng, Xinhao Xiang, Jiawei Zhang

Hybrid Cross-Device Localization via Neural Metric Learning and Feature Fusion

Abstract (English): We present a hybrid cross-device localization pipeline developed for the CroCoDL 2025 Challenge. Our approach integrates a shared retrieval encoder and two complementary localization branches: a classical geometric branch using feature fusion and PnP, and a neural feed-forward branch (MapAnything) for metric localization conditioned on geometric inputs. A neural-guided candidate pruning strategy further filters unreliable map frames based on translation consistency, while depth-conditioned localization refines metric scale and translation precision on Spot scenes. These components jointly lead to significant improvements in recall and accuracy across both HYDRO and SUCCU benchmarks. Our method achieved a final score of 92.62 (R@0.5m, 5°) during the challenge.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种为 CroCoDL 2025 挑战赛开发的混合跨设备定位流程。 我们的方法整合了一个共享检索编码器和两个互补的定位分支：一个使用特征融合和 PnP 的经典几何分支，以及一个用于度量定位的神经前馈分支（MapAnything），其以几何输入为条件。 基于平移一致性的神经引导候选剪枝策略进一步过滤掉不可靠的地图帧，而深度条件定位则优化了 Spot 场景上的度量尺度和平移精度。 这些组件共同显著提高了 HYDRO 和 SUCCU 基准测试上的召回率和准确率。 在挑战赛期间，我们的方法获得了 92.62 (R@0.5m, 5°) 的最终得分。

TLDR: This paper presents a hybrid cross-device localization pipeline using neural metric learning and feature fusion, achieving strong performance in the CroCoDL 2025 Challenge.

Authors: Meixia Lin, Mingkai Liu, Shuxue Peng, Dikai Fan, Shengyu Gu, Xianliang Huang, Haoyang Ye, Xiao Liu

EndoCaver: Handling Fog, Blur and Glare in Endoscopic Images via Joint Deblurring-Segmentation

Abstract (English): Endoscopic image analysis is vital for colorectal cancer screening, yet real-world conditions often suffer from lens fogging, motion blur, and specular highlights, which severely compromise automated polyp detection. We propose EndoCaver, a lightweight transformer with a unidirectional-guided dual-decoder architecture, enabling joint multi-task capability for image deblurring and segmentation while significantly reducing computational complexity and model parameters. Specifically, it integrates a Global Attention Module (GAM) for cross-scale aggregation, a Deblurring-Segmentation Aligner (DSA) to transfer restoration cues, and a cosine-based scheduler (LoCoS) for stable multi-task optimisation. Experiments on the Kvasir-SEG dataset show that EndoCaver achieves 0.922 Dice on clean data and 0.889 under severe image degradation, surpassing state-of-the-art methods while reducing model parameters by 90%. These results demonstrate its efficiency and robustness, making it well-suited for on-device clinical deployment. Code is available at https://github.com/ReaganWu/EndoCaver.

摘要（中文）: 内窥镜图像分析对于结直肠癌筛查至关重要，但真实环境下的图像常受镜头起雾、运动模糊和镜面反射等问题影响，严重损害了息肉自动检测的性能。我们提出了一种轻量级的Transformer模型EndoCaver，它采用单向引导的双解码器架构，能够实现图像去模糊和分割的联合多任务能力，同时显著降低计算复杂度和模型参数量。具体而言，它集成了用于跨尺度聚合的全局注意力模块（GAM）、用于传递复原线索的去模糊-分割对齐器（DSA）以及用于稳定多任务优化的基于余弦的调度器（LoCoS）。在Kvasir-SEG数据集上的实验表明，EndoCaver在清晰数据上获得了0.922的Dice系数，在严重图像退化情况下获得了0.889的Dice系数，超越了现有最先进的方法，同时模型参数量减少了90%。这些结果表明了其效率和鲁棒性，使其非常适合在设备上进行临床部署。代码可在https://github.com/ReaganWu/EndoCaver上获取。

TLDR: EndoCaver is a lightweight transformer-based model for joint deblurring and segmentation of endoscopic images, achieving state-of-the-art performance on degraded images with significantly fewer parameters, making it suitable for on-device clinical applications.

简要说明: EndoCaver是一个轻量级的基于Transformer的模型，用于内窥镜图像的联合去模糊和分割。它在低质量图像上实现了最先进的性能，且模型参数显著减少，使其适用于设备端的临床应用。

Authors: Zhuoyu Wu, Wenhui Ou, Pei-Sze Tan, Jiayan Yang, Wenqi Fang, Zheng Wang, Raphaël C. -W. Phan

SplineFlow: Flow Matching for Dynamical Systems with B-Spline Interpolants

Abstract (English): Flow matching is a scalable generative framework for characterizing continuous normalizing flows with wide-range applications. However, current state-of-the-art methods are not well-suited for modeling dynamical systems, as they construct conditional paths using linear interpolants that may not capture the underlying state evolution, especially when learning higher-order dynamics from irregular sampled observations. Constructing unified paths that satisfy multi-marginal constraints across observations is challenging, since naïve higher-order polynomials tend to be unstable and oscillatory. We introduce SplineFlow, a theoretically grounded flow matching algorithm that jointly models conditional paths across observations via B-spline interpolation. Specifically, SplineFlow exploits the smoothness and stability of B-spline bases to learn the complex underlying dynamics in a structured manner while ensuring the multi-marginal requirements are met. Comprehensive experiments across various deterministic and stochastic dynamical systems of varying complexity, as well as on cellular trajectory inference tasks, demonstrate the strong improvement of SplineFlow over existing baselines. Our code is available at: https://github.com/santanurathod/SplineFlow.

摘要（中文）: 流匹配是一种可扩展的生成框架，用于表征具有广泛应用的连续归一化流。然而，目前最先进的方法不太适合建模动力系统，因为它们使用线性插值构造条件路径，而线性插值可能无法捕捉到潜在的状态演化，尤其是在从不规则采样的观测数据中学习高阶动力学时。构造满足跨观测数据的多边缘约束的统一路径具有挑战性，因为朴素的高阶多项式往往不稳定并具有振荡性。我们引入了 SplineFlow，这是一种理论上可靠的流匹配算法，它通过 B 样条插值联合建模跨观测数据的条件路径。具体而言，SplineFlow 利用 B 样条基的平滑性和稳定性，以结构化的方式学习复杂的潜在动力学，同时确保满足多边缘要求。在各种不同复杂度的确定性和随机动力系统以及细胞轨迹推断任务中的综合实验表明，SplineFlow 相对于现有基线有显著改进。我们的代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/santanurathod/SplineFlow。

TLDR: SplineFlow introduces a novel flow matching algorithm using B-spline interpolation for modeling complex dynamical systems, outperforming existing methods in capturing higher-order dynamics and handling irregular sampling.

简要说明: SplineFlow 提出了一种新的流匹配算法，该算法使用 B 样条插值来建模复杂的动力系统，优于现有方法，能够捕获高阶动力学并处理不规则采样。
